<form><strong style="color:darkred; font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size:14pt">瑜伽師地論科句披尋記卷第五十九</strong></form>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:#000000"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　彌勒菩薩說</span></span></span><br />
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:#000000"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　唐三藏沙門玄奘奉詔譯</span></span></span><br />
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:#000000"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　韓清淨科記</span></span></span><br />
<a name="58p4781"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">攝決擇分中有尋有伺等三地之二</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　〈有尋有伺等三地〉總共有三地：〈有尋有伺地〉、〈無尋唯伺地〉、及〈無尋無伺地〉。在〈攝決擇分〉中有四卷，卷58、卷59、卷60、及卷61，解釋這三地。卷58：決擇〈有尋有伺等三地〉之一，是第一個部分的解釋。卷59：決擇〈有尋有伺等三地〉之二，是第二個部分的解釋。卷60：決擇〈有尋有伺等三地〉之三，是第三個部分的解釋。卷61：決擇〈有尋有伺等三地〉之四，是第四個部分的解釋。卷58分三科解釋煩惱雜染，第一科是明建立，以五法來建立煩惱雜染；第二科是會諸經，以七科來說明經典上對於煩惱的譬喻；這兩科在卷58已解釋完了。第三科廣分別煩惱雜染，卷59解釋這段文，並解釋業雜染的自性相及方便。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">壬三、廣分別2　癸一、長行釋2　子一、釋差別7　丑一、煩惱發業2　寅一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科廣分別，詳細分別煩惱雜染的特性，分二科；第一科長行釋，用較長的文解釋，又分二科；第一科釋差別，解釋煩惱雜染的差別，又分七科；第一科煩惱發業，由煩惱發動造業，又分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：貪等十煩惱幾能發業？幾不能發？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：貪、恚、慢、無明、疑，及薩迦耶見、見取見、戒禁取見、邊執見、邪見等，前面說的十種煩惱，哪一些可以發出身語意三業，哪一些不能發業？&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、答2　卯一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科標，標列出來。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：一切能發。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：所有的煩惱都能夠使令有情造業，都能夠發動造業。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、辨2　辰一、由猛利</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科辨，辨別引發的原因，再做詳細的說明，分二科；第一科由猛利，因為這些煩惱猛利現行。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若諸煩惱猛利現行，方能發起往惡趣業，非諸失念而現行者。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若是這十種煩惱，包括愛煩惱和見煩惱，現行時要很猛利、很有力量，才能夠發起往三惡道的不善業，不是說一時忘失正念而現行的煩惱能發起往惡趣的不善業。煩惱力量強大發起的不善業力量也大。《法華經玄贊要集》卷26說：十不善業道有三品，上品十不善業，資助地獄五支種子，能招感地獄果報；中品不善業，資助餓鬼五支種子，能招感餓鬼果報；下品不善業，資助畜生五支種子，能招感畜生果報。如果是一時忘失正念而有煩惱，一方面容易察覺、對治，一方面因為煩惱力量屬於中下小品，所發的不善業也小，沒有力量招感惡趣果。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、由分別</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科由分別，由分別心發動造業。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又分別起能發此業，非任運起。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又由內心分別生起的愛、見煩惱，屬於見道所斷的煩惱，能夠發起往惡趣業，不是俱生、任運起、屬於修道所斷的愛、見煩惱，能夠發起往惡趣業。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="59p4782"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》非諸失念而現行者者：失念現行，諸聖或有，然彼決定不往惡趣，即由此義應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這裡提醒我們一點： 如果現行忘失正念，連聖人有時候也會有，可是他們決定不會到三惡道去，因為失念的煩惱不是極猛利的煩惱，由這個道理可以知道這件事情。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　卷58說欲界分別起的十種煩惱，若具足三種因緣決定往生惡趣，餘則不定，這三種因緣是：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、極多修習，殷重、無間計為功德，不見其失、不見其患，縱情而起。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、用此煩惱以為依處，由身語意，於諸惡行作及增長。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、由此煩惱斷他善品，授不善品。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　煩惱具足這三種因緣時特別有力量，決定往生惡趣領受異熟果。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　（連結：<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/C59-01.htm">發業煩惱</a>）</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑二、煩惱相2　寅一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科煩惱相，說明煩惱的相狀，分二科；第一科問，提出問題。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：諸煩惱有幾相？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：諸煩惱有幾種相貌 ？&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、答2　卯一、標列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科標，標出相貌。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：略有三相。一、自相，二、共相，三、差別相。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：要略而言，煩惱有自相、共相、差別相三種相貌。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、隨釋3　辰一、自相</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科隨釋，接著將標列出來的自相、共相、差別相詳細解釋，分三科；第一科自相，解釋煩惱的自相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">自相者，謂貪瞋等各各自性所攝相。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　煩惱的自相方面，是指貪、瞋等各各有其自性所攝的體相。如貪瞋的自相，本論卷8說：貪者，由親近不善丈夫、聞非正法、不如理作意故；又由任運失念故，於外及內可愛境界，若分別不分別，染著為體；恚者，由親近不善丈夫、聞非正法、不如理作意故；及由任運失念故，於外及內非愛境界，若分別不分別，憎恚為體。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、共相</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科共相，解釋煩惱的共相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">共相者，謂諸煩惱無有差別，一切皆同不寂靜相。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　煩惱的共相方面，是指煩惱與煩惱彼此之間沒有什麼差別，一切都是不寂靜相。一個人心不寂靜就一定有煩惱，有煩惱一定心不能寂靜下來，心中妄想分別、散亂不能得定、也障礙成就聖道，這個不寂靜相就是煩惱的共相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="59p4783"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰三、差別相2　巳一、標列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科差別相，說明煩惱的差別相，分二科；第一科標列，標示列出二種。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">差別相者，復有二種。一、門差別相，二、轉差別相。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　煩惱的差別相方面，又有門差別相、轉差別相二種。門差別相，煩惱出入的處所稱為門。〈本地分‧有尋有伺等三地〉卷8，229頁說，由纏門及隨眠門二門煩惱所惱。纏門由不寂靜住故、由障礙善故、由發起惡趣惡行故、由攝受現法鄙賤故、由能感生等苦故等五門。隨眠門是由與諸纏作所依故，及能引發生等苦故，於見及修能為障礙。包括邪解了故，不解了故，解了不解了故，邪解了迷執故，彼因依處故，彼怖所生故，任運現行故等七門。由此可知煩惱門的差別相。轉差別相，是指煩惱生起、現前的種種差別相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、隨釋2　午一、門差別相</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科隨釋，接著解釋門差別相、轉差別相，分二科；第一科門差別相，說明門差別相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">門差別相者，謂結、縛、隨眠、隨煩惱、纏等，如本地分已說。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　門差別相方面，是指結乃至纏等，如〈本地分〉卷8說明煩惱有二十六種，依煩惱不同的特性安立不同的名稱。例如說「結」，是指能和合苦，使令有情與苦和合在一起；縛，繫縛，是指令於善法不隨所欲，有煩惱繫縛時就不能隨心自在行善；隨眠，是指一切世間增上種子之所隨逐，有煩惱的種子，就能招感三界五趣世間生死的果報；隨煩惱，指倒染心，隨順煩惱能夠顛倒染汙這一念心；纏，是指數起現行，煩惱常常生起現行纏繞眾生令不自在。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》如本地分已說者：本地分中有尋有伺地說煩惱差別，一一別釋應知。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/08.htm#47478:5478">陵本八卷六頁563</a>）</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　〈本地分‧有尋有伺地〉卷8，232頁，說煩惱差別有二十六種，從不同角度來看煩惱，煩惱的作用不同，名字也不同，這是第一種差別相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、轉差別相2　未一、列七種</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科轉差別相，煩惱生起的差別相，分二科；第一科列七種，列出來七種。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">轉差別相者，謂隨眠轉故、所緣轉故、現行轉故、品差別轉故、力無力轉故、因果轉故、迷行轉故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　煩惱生起的種種差別相方面，是指煩惱種子的生起、煩惱生起的所緣境、煩惱現行的生起、煩惱生起的軟中上品差別、煩惱的生起是由有力量的分別而起或由沒有力量的任運而起的、煩惱生起是由因的種子現前或是由等流果等引發的現行、煩惱生起是由於心行的迷惑等。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、隨別釋6　申一、隨眠轉2　酉一、釋差別2　戌一、標列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科隨別釋，接著各別詳細解釋，分六科；第一科隨眠轉，煩惱種子轉相，又分二科；第一科釋差別，解釋煩惱種子的差別，又分二科；第一科標列，標示列舉出十八種。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，隨眠轉相略有十八。一、隨逐自境隨眠，二、隨逐他境隨眠，三、被損隨眠，四、不被損隨眠，五、隨增隨眠，六、不隨增隨眠，七、具分隨眠，八、不具分隨眠，九、可害隨眠，十、不可害隨眠，十一、增上隨眠，十二、平等隨眠，十三、下劣隨眠，十四、覺悟隨眠，十五、不覺悟隨眠，十六、能生多苦隨眠，十七、能生少苦隨眠，十八、不能生苦隨眠。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，煩惱種子生起的相貌，要略而言有十八種。如隨逐自境隨眠乃至不能生苦隨眠，這十八種隨眠，總共有八組：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、自他境對：指1、隨逐自境隨眠 2、隨逐他境隨眠；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、損不損對：指3、被損隨眠 4、不被損隨眠；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、增不增對：指5、隨增隨眠 6、不隨增隨眠；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、具不具對：指7、具分隨眠 8、不具分隨眠；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、害不害對：指9、可害隨眠 10、不可害隨眠；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　六、增等劣對：指11、增上隨眠 12、平等隨眠 13、下劣隨眠；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　七、覺不覺：指14、覺悟隨眠 15、不覺悟隨眠；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　八、生苦多少對：指16、能生多苦隨眠 17、能生少苦隨眠 18、不能生苦隨眠。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　先列出名稱，下文再逐一解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、隨釋18　亥一、隨逐自境隨眠</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科隨釋，接著解釋，分十八科；第一科逐自境隨眠，隨逐三界中自地的隨眠。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="59p4784"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">隨逐自境隨眠者，謂三界中自地所攝隨眠。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　隨逐自境隨眠方面，是指三界中各有自地所攝的煩惱種子所隨逐。例如生到欲界的人，有欲界的煩惱種子所隨逐；生到色界的天人，有色界的煩惱種子所隨逐；生到無色界的天人，有無色界的煩惱種子所隨逐，三界中的有情都有屬於自地的煩惱種子所隨逐。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、隨逐他境隨眠</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科隨逐他境隨眠，指有不是自地境所攝的煩惱種子隨逐。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">隨逐他境隨眠者，謂生上下地，下上煩惱所逐隨眠。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　隨逐他境隨眠方面，是指雖然生到上地的色界無色界，還是有下地欲界的煩惱種子所隨逐；或是生到下地欲界，還是有色界及無色界的煩惱種子所隨逐，有不屬於自地境所攝的煩惱種子隨逐。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥三、被損隨眠</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科被損隨眠，已經被損害的煩惱種子。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">被損隨眠者，謂世間離欲下地隨眠。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　被損害的隨眠方面，是依世間道，修習禪定，遠離欲界欲，證得世間初靜慮，乃至非想非非想處定，此時欲界等下地的煩惱種子被損害、降伏，不能生現行。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥四、不被損隨眠</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科不被損隨眠，沒有被損害的煩惱種子。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">不被損隨眠者，謂已離欲、或未離欲自地隨眠。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　沒有被損害的隨眠方面，是指已經離欲、或未離欲者，自身還為自地的煩惱種子所隨逐。例如已經離欲界欲生到上地色界或無色界，還是有色界及無色界的煩惱種子所隨逐，這色界及無色界的煩惱種子沒有被損害，是屬於自地的隨眠；或生到下地欲界，還沒有離欲，還是有欲界的煩惱種子所隨逐，屬於自地的隨眠沒有被損害。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥五、隨增隨眠</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科隨增隨眠，指展轉增強的隨眠。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">隨增隨眠者，謂自地隨眠。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　隨增隨眠方面，是指生到自地，自地煩惱種子不斷熏習增強它的力量。例如，屬於欲界的人有欲界自地的煩惱種子，數數熏習後會不斷增強，如受用諸欲、生起惡行，使貪欲不斷熏習增強；色界無色界天人，有相對應的色界無色界自地的煩惱種子，數數熏習後它的力量就會隨順增加、增強。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥六、不隨增隨眠</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科不隨增隨眠，不會隨增的隨眠。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">不隨增隨眠者，謂他地隨眠。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　不隨增隨眠方面，是指於自地中，他地隨眠的煩惱種子不會增加、不會增強力量，因為只有自地煩惱種子才會數數熏習，力量才會隨之增加、增強。例如，生在欲界，色界無色界的煩惱種子不會熏習增加、增強，因為常生起的就是欲界的煩惱，所以熏習的是自地的煩惱種子，不是他地色無色界的煩惱種子。色界、無色界的天人也是一樣，自地的煩惱種子可以隨增，他地的就不會增加增強了，因為沒有數數現行、數數熏習，所以不隨增隨眠，是指他地的隨眠。（連結：<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/C59-02.htm">隨增隨眠</a>）</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥七、具分隨眠</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第七科具分隨眠，具足所有的煩惱種子。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">具分隨眠者，謂諸異生所有隨眠。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　具分隨眠方面，是指凡夫阿賴耶識中所有的煩惱種子；也就是所有的煩惱種子，是完整的，尚未被斷除的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="59p4785"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥八、不具分隨眠</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第八科不具分隨眠，只有部分的煩惱種子。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">不具分隨眠者，謂諸有學非異生者所有隨眠。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　不具分隨眠方面，是指有學聖者，包括初果乃至四果向的聖人，在阿賴耶識中仍有尚未斷除的俱生煩惱種子。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥九、可害隨眠</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第九科可害隨眠，可以斷除的隨眠。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">可害隨眠者，謂般涅槃法所有隨眠。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　可損害隨眠方面，是指具聲聞乘，緣覺乘，或者是菩薩乘三乘無漏種性的人，可以依般涅槃法斷除所有的隨眠，他們的煩惱種子是能被斷除損害的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥十、不可害隨眠</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十科不可害隨眠，不可以斷除的隨眠。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">不可害隨眠者，謂不般涅槃法所有隨眠。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　不可損害的隨眠方面，是指有一類的眾生，沒有三乘無漏的種性，沒有善根，他們的煩惱種子是不能被斷除損害的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥十一、增上隨眠</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十一科增上隨眠，會增上加強的隨眠。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">增上隨眠者，謂貪等行所有隨眠。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　增上隨眠方面，是指貪等行所有隨眠。世間有情，每個人煩惱的特性、強度不一樣，有些貪的煩惱種子特別強，稱為貪行者；有些瞋的煩惱種子特別強，稱為瞋行者；有些愚癡的煩惱種子特別強，稱為愚癡行者；有些尋思的煩惱種子特別強，散亂心多的人，稱為尋思行者。有些高慢心的煩惱種子特別強，稱為慢行者；有些疑惑心的煩惱種子特別強，稱為疑行者。貪、瞋、癡、尋思、慢、疑等行者，所具有的特別重的煩惱種子。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥十二、平等隨眠</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十二科平等隨眠，強度差不多的隨眠。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">平等隨眠者，謂等分行所有隨眠。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　平等隨眠方面，是指等分行所有隨眠。世間有情，有些人所具有的各各煩惱種子的強度都差不多，不會有某個煩惱種子特別強、特別重，所有煩惱的力量都差不多，稱為等分行，這種人所具有的煩惱種子，稱為平等隨眠。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥十三、下劣隨眠</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十三科下劣隨眠，力量薄弱的隨眠。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">下劣隨眠者，謂薄塵行所有隨眠。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　下劣隨眠方面，是指薄塵行所有隨眠。世間有情，有些人所具有的煩惱種子力量比較小，這就是薄塵行者。薄就是微薄，塵就是煩惱，煩惱很微薄的人所具有的煩惱種子，稱為下劣隨眠。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥十四、覺悟隨眠</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十四科覺悟隨眠，煩惱種子生現行。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="59p4786"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">覺悟隨眠者，謂諸纏果與纏俱轉隨眠。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　覺悟隨眠方面，是指纏果與纏俱轉隨眠。纏，是指煩惱現行數數生起；纏果，是指煩惱種子，也就是隨眠。纏果與纏俱轉和合，是指煩惱種子，遇緣生起現行的煩惱纏，這樣能產生「種生現、現熏種」種現熏三法同時現起的俱時因果、合乎俱有義的隨眠，這類諸纏果與纏俱轉隨眠，也就是覺悟隨眠，是醒過來了的煩惱種子，種子生現行了。可參閱《攝大乘論講記》中闡述種子六義中的「果俱有」義。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》謂諸纏果與纏俱轉隨眠者：此中纏果，謂即隨眠，由從彼纏所熏生故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　纏果是指煩惱種子，煩惱種子是由煩惱的現行熏習所生的，熏習以後，下一次遇緣還會再生起現行，煩惱種子生現行，稱為覺悟隨眠。覺悟譬喻種子生現行，醒過來了。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥十五、不覺悟隨眠</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十五科不覺悟隨眠，還沒有生現行的煩惱種子。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">不覺悟隨眠者，謂離諸纏而恆隨逐隨眠。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　不覺悟隨眠方面，是指這類煩惱種子現在還沒有生現行（煩惱纏），在阿賴耶識中睡眠，沒有醒過來，能產生種子生種子的異時因果、合乎恆隨轉義的隨眠，這類離諸纏而恆隨逐隨眠，也就是不覺悟隨眠。雖然沒有現行出來，煩惱的功能性還在。可參閱《攝大乘論講記》中闡述種子六義中的「恆隨轉」義。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥十六、能生多苦隨眠</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十六科能生多苦隨眠，能使有情產生很多苦惱的煩惱種子。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">能生多苦隨眠者，謂欲界隨眠。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　能生多苦隨眠方面，是指欲界的煩惱種子，使令有情生出種種的苦：苦苦、壞苦、行苦，愛別離乃至老病死等苦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥十七、能生少苦隨眠</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十七科能生少苦隨眠，能生少苦的煩惱種子。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">能生少苦隨眠者，謂色無色界隨眠。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　能生少苦隨眠方面，是指色界、無色界有情的煩惱種子。上二界的煩惱種子屬有覆無記，因為其性染污，覆障聖道，又能蔽心，使心不淨，稱為有覆；然因勢用薄弱、昧略，不能引生異熟果，得可愛或不可愛的果報，稱為無記，合稱有覆無記。這類煩惱屬於壞苦的樂受及行苦，不苦不樂受所攝，能生少苦。壞苦包括樂受及煩惱；行苦，行，指遷流不息，因為貪瞋癡等煩惱種子還在，只是壓抑著暫時不生現行，來世隨時有轉變為苦苦或壞苦的可能性，因此行苦仍名之為苦。上二界有情只有喜樂捨受，喜樂受屬壞苦，四禪天以上都是捨受屬行苦，這二種苦相對於欲界的苦苦屬於少苦，所以上二界有情的煩惱種子，名能生少苦隨眠。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥十八、不能生苦隨眠</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十八科不能生苦隨眠，不能生苦的煩惱種子。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">不能生苦隨眠者，謂得自在菩薩所有隨眠。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　不能生苦隨眠方面，是指已得自在、八地以上菩薩的煩惱種子。八地以上菩薩雖然有煩惱種子，由於是得無生法忍的菩薩，永伏煩惱現行，分段生死我執的種子已伏斷，不會引發到三界生死輪迴的果報，因此這些煩惱種子，不能稱為生多苦或生少苦的隨眠；由大悲願所攝持故，直到成佛前一剎那在金剛喻定中才斷除所有的煩惱種子。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、辨麤重2　戌一、辨異不異2　亥一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科辨麤重，隨眠沒有堪能性的情況，分二科；第一科辨異不異，說明煩惱品麤重的差異，分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="59p4787"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：如說麤重體性名隨眠，此煩惱品麤重望彼諸行，當言有異？為不異耶？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：如說麤重的體性稱為隨眠，麤重是指沒有堪能性，這些煩惱品種子的麤重對望諸行，與現行的五蘊等有為法，應當說有差異，還是沒有差異？&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》如說麤重體性名隨眠等者：本地分意地中說：諸自體中所有種子，若煩惱品所攝，名為麤重，亦名隨眠。若異熟品所攝，及餘無記品所攝，唯名麤重，不名隨眠。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/02.htm#47528:951">陵本二卷二頁112</a>）由是應知種子差別。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　〈本地分‧意地〉卷2，54頁中說：於自身阿賴耶識中所有的種子，如果是煩惱品所攝的種子，稱為麤重，也稱為隨眠；如果屬於異熟品所攝的種子，以及其餘無記品所攝的種子。無記品所攝的種子勢用薄弱、昧略，因為它們沒有善惡之別，無記品種子所造的業沒有什麼力量，這類種子雖也使令有情沒有堪能性，只能稱為麤重，不稱為隨眠。由此應當知道種子有這些差別。總之，有一種種子稱為麤重，但不稱為隨眠，這是指無記品及異熟品；另外有一種種子稱為麤重，也稱為隨眠，是指煩惱品所攝的種子。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、答3　天一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分三科；第一科標，標出有異。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：當言有異。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：應當說煩惱品的麤重，與現行五蘊的有為法有差異。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">何以故？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　怎麼說？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天三、釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科釋，加以解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由阿羅漢永害一切煩惱麤重，而諸行相續猶未斷絕故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　因為阿羅漢已永遠斷除三界分別起及俱生起的煩惱麤重，將阿賴耶識中煩惱障品類的種子，全部斷除了，但前生由煩惱麤重所造成的現行果報，色受想行識五蘊，還是繼續存活著，還沒有斷絕，所以說煩惱品的種子（煩惱麤重），與色受想行識五蘊是有差別的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、辨彼相攝2　亥一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科辨彼相攝，說明麤重的相貌，分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="28686:47536"></a>問：有幾麤重攝諸麤重？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：有幾種麤重可以含攝這些麤重品類？這裡作概略性的說明，接下來詳細說明。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《瑜伽論記》卷1說：麤重有三種定義：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、損惱義，唯指染污法，煩惱品所攝的種子。煩惱的種子隨附依身，能生煩惱，煩惱生時沒有堪能性，順諸雜染，違順清淨，因此這類的種子稱為麤重也稱為隨眠。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、無堪能義，包括煩惱品所攝及異熟品所攝、及其餘無記品所攝的種子。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、性有漏義，包括有漏三性心法。其中有漏善，雖然是善法但還是有漏，也稱為麤重。有漏的善不稱為隨眠，但是有一分更深刻的定義，如果煩惱種子尚未斷除，使得善法還是夾雜著俱生起的煩惱，令有情無堪能性，因此有漏的善法也可以稱為麤重。例如：聞法是一種善法，熏習無漏的善法，由於內心有煩惱，使令無漏善法的堪能性不大，雖然熏習了，斷煩惱的力量還是很小，因此有漏善也有麤重的意義。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《成唯識論了義燈》卷5窺基大師說：總攝經論諸文麤重有四種。一、現行有漏諸心心所；二、現行二障；三、二障種子；四、二障習氣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、答2　天一、標列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科標列，標示列出麤重。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="59p4788"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：略有十八。一、自性異熟麤重，二、自性煩惱麤重，三、自性業麤重，四、煩惱障麤重，五、業障麤重，六、異熟障麤重，七、蓋麤重，八、不正尋思麤重，九、愁惱麤重，十、怖畏麤重，十一、劬勞麤重，十二、飲食麤重，十三、眠夢麤重，十四、婬欲麤重，十五、界不平等麤重，十六、時分變異麤重，十七、終沒麤重，十八、遍行麤重。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：要略而言這種沒有堪能性的麤重品類有十八種相貌，包括自性異熟麤重乃至遍行麤重。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　各家論師對這十八種麤重品類的解釋不太相同，都可參考。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《瑜伽論記》卷17說：前六種麤重。印度有三種說法：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、護法菩薩說：前三種麤重約法爾種，後三種麤重約新熏種。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、護月菩薩說：前三種麤重約種子，後三種麤重約現行。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、勝軍師說：前三種麤重無始已來熏成，後三種麤重包括現行和種子。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　景法師說：前三種麤重即舉一切煩惱、業、報麤重；次三種麤重即唯舉三障麤重。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《顯揚聖教論》卷9中說有二十種麤重；《大乘阿毘達磨雜集論》卷10〈1 諦品〉說有二十四種麤重都可參考閱讀。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、自性異熟麤重，指果報自性上的無堪能性，是引業的麤重。三界五趣的果報都是由煩惱造業招感而得，得到果報體時，已有煩惱種子的無堪能性在其中，令果報無堪能性。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、自性煩惱麤重，指煩惱種子的自性。煩惱本身就是一種麤重，沒有堪能性。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、自性業麤重，指有漏業習氣的自性，有雜染，業雜染的體性也是麤重的，也是沒有堪能性的。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、煩惱障麤重，煩惱障是指長時、猛利的煩惱性。煩惱已經現行，稱為煩惱障麤重。煩惱的相貌就是不寂靜，不寂靜的人請他安穩坐著聽聞佛法、修止觀是辦不到的，這就是沒有堪能性。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、業障麤重，是指殺父、殺母、殺阿羅漢、破合和僧、出佛身血等五無間業使令有情沒有堪能性修止觀、得聖道；而不是一般人所造的輕業，輕業障礙有情得聖道的傷害還不是很大。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　六、異熟障麤重，是果報上的麤重，滿業的麤重。例如天生頭腦比較不好，或是眼睛不明亮、耳朵也很遲鈍，也是一種麤重，使有情沒有堪能性。由於前生造的業力使令今生果報有種種的障礙，例如有的人得了先天性的某種毛病就必須去治療，乃至全家都有這種病，使令不能讀書做事，必須花全部的時間治病，這也是一種果報上的麤重。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　七、蓋麤重，蓋即蓋覆之義。有五法，貪欲、瞋恚、昏沈睡眠、掉舉惡作、疑，這五法能蓋覆心性而不生善法。這些蓋障使令有情沒有堪能性修習止觀、證得聖道，所以五蓋也是麤重。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　八、不正尋思麤重，不正尋思是指不正思惟、不合道理的分別心，如欲、恚、害、親里、國土、不死、家勢相應、輕懱相應等八種尋思（請參閱本論卷89，2648~2649頁）。它能擾亂心、令心不寂靜住，也能染汙心、令心不清淨，使令有情沒有堪能性修習止觀、證得聖道，因此不正尋思也是麤重。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　九、愁惱麤重，整個心都陷在憂愁苦惱中，心不寂靜沒有堪能性修學聖道，因此也是麤重。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　十、怖畏麤重，指心中有恐怖害怕，使令有情沒有堪能性，不能勇猛修行的麤重。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　十一、劬勞麤重，作事作得太辛苦，身體非常疲勞，沒有堪能性繼續修行的麤重。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　十二、飲食麤重，指飲食吃得太多容易昏沈、睡眠，吃得太少又沒有力氣，或者吃錯東西就生病了，由於飲食的不當，導至身心麤重、無堪能性，不利於修行。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　十三、眠夢麤重，眠夢會令身不自在，因為人在睡夢之中，身體之屈伸取捨，都不能自主；眠夢也會使心昧略，眠夢中的第六意識緣境時，不與前五識俱起，不能明了取境，令心沒有堪能性而有麤重。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　十四、婬欲麤重，淫欲使令有情身心疲勞，也是一種麤重。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　十五、界不平等麤重，地水火風不調，如火大過盛，心浮氣躁、水大過盛產生水腫、風大過盛呼吸不順，地大過盛身體僵硬，這些身體的不適，障礙修行，也是一種麤重。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　十六、時分變異麤重，時分變異是指老了、退化了，老的時候身心退化，不能隨心意而轉，因此有人說：老來無三昧，也是一種麤重。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　十七、終沒麤重，終沒就是死的時候。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《雜集論》卷10說：死麤重，是指臨命終時諸根亂性。將命終時，由業力所得的果報身受用已到盡頭，諸根衰退，已無堪能性，地水火風四大分解，會有解肢節的痛苦，使得身心都麤重。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　十八、遍行麤重，是指行苦，遍行於由煩惱而取得的五蘊果報體中。有情於此五蘊果報體不苦不樂受中，不能了知一切有為法皆是無常變壞法，隨時有轉變為苦苦或壞苦的可能性，於樂受、苦受、不苦不樂受等三受不得解脫，為三受種子之所隨逐，由不安穩行而趣入行苦。因此行苦也是一種麤重，令有情沒有堪能性。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》遍行麤重者：此謂行苦。應知遍行一切若樂受中、若苦受中、若不苦不樂受中故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　遍行麤重，是指行苦。應該知道行苦遍行於一切樂受中、苦受中、不苦不樂受中的緣故。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、指釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科指釋，根據前面所說解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是麤重，如前應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以上十八種麤重，如同前文所解釋的應該知道。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》如是麤重如前應知者：前說：略有二種麤重。一、漏麤重，二、有漏麤重。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/58.htm#47543:47213">陵本五十八卷十七頁4761</a>）此中十八，彼二所攝，故指如前。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　前文說：要略而言有二種麤重。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、漏麤重，是指煩惱的麤重。阿羅漢等修道所斷煩惱斷時，皆悉永離。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、有漏麤重，又名煩惱習麤重。屬於前一生造業招感而得的有漏果報體的無堪能性，也是一種習氣的麤重。如阿羅漢雖然斷了煩惱，可是由前生的業力取得的身體，還是有煩惱習氣，這些煩惱習氣是一種有漏麤重。在〈決擇‧有尋有伺等三地〉卷58，1937頁那裡有說到，這十八種麤重可以涵攝在這二種麤重裡面。如果是煩惱品的屬於漏麤重，是不善性；果報上的煩惱習氣所產生的沒有堪能性，屬於有漏麤重，是無記性。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、所緣現行轉</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科所緣現行轉，煩惱所緣、現行二法的生起相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，所緣、現行二轉，於其自處當廣宣說。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，煩惱隨著不同的所緣境而起現行，下文還會再詳細解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》所緣現行二轉等者：下說煩惱緣境略有十五，煩惱現行有二十種，如彼廣說應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　下文說：煩惱的所緣境，要略而言有十五種，煩惱的現行有二十種，如下文廣說應當了知。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="59p4789"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申三、品差別轉</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科品差別轉，煩惱的品類差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">品差別轉，當知如前蘊善巧說。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　煩惱的品類差別方面，應該知道如同前文卷55中的蘊善巧所解釋的品類差別可知。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》品差別轉等者：蘊善巧中，建立煩惱軟中上品。謂最後所斷名軟品，中間所斷名中品，最初所斷名上品。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/55.htm#47551:43263">陵本五十五卷八頁4418</a>）如彼應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　蘊善巧中，建立煩惱有軟品、中品及上品三種。軟品是指微細的煩惱，需要上品能斷的智慧才能斷除；中間所斷的煩惱稱為中品，中等的煩惱，由中品能斷的智慧就可以斷除；最初所斷的是指最粗的煩惱，最粗的煩惱，由下品能斷的智慧就能夠斷除了。請參閱〈決擇‧五識身相應地意地〉卷55，1618頁就可以知道。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申四、力無力轉</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科力無力轉，煩惱的活動有力無力。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">力無力轉，當知如前本地分說。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　煩惱生起時是有力量的或無力的，如同以前〈本地分〉卷8所解釋的應該知道。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》力無力轉等者：謂彼煩惱，若由親近不善丈夫、聞非正法、不如理作意轉者，當知有力。若由任運失念轉者，當知無力。一一分別，如本地分有尋有伺地說。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/08.htm#47554:5348">陵本八卷二頁548</a>）</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　煩惱很有力量，是因為親近不善丈夫，親近惡知識，不是聽聞佛法，聽的是邪法，對一切法不能離染污心，不持清淨心，不能如諸法實相的真理來作意，令心活動，這時煩惱就有力量。如果是任運的、自然而生起的失去正念，不需特別的分別，這樣的煩惱是無力的，通常是指一種習慣或是習氣，這種任運失念的煩惱是沒有力量的。詳細分別，如〈本地分‧有尋有伺等三地〉卷8，225頁所說可知。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申五、因果轉2　酉一、標隨應</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科因果轉，因果轉相，分二科；第一科標隨應，標出惑業果都以煩惱為因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">因果轉者，謂煩惱業生皆以煩惱為因。果亦如是，隨應當知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　煩惱的因、果轉相方面，是指煩惱雜染、業雜染、與生雜染都是以無明煩惱為因。果也是如此，應該了知。煩惱、業是生死的因，所有的煩惱中都有無明，因無明而造業，因業而有生；生雜染是後有業產生的異熟果，也還有惑業苦的種子在其中，遇緣還能生起煩惱，也有有漏麤重，所以說果亦如是。總之惑業苦都以無明煩惱為因，惑業是以無明煩惱為因，果也是以無明煩惱為因，稱因果轉；如果沒有煩惱，生死輪轉中惑業因及惑業果都已沒有。不論是在因地或在果地時都是煩惱在作祟。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《瑜伽論記》卷17景法師說：煩惱業生皆以煩惱為因方面，是說從煩惱種生現煩惱，是生起因。從現起煩惱生現起煩惱，是引發因。從現起煩惱生現起業若因性者，亦是引發因。從不善煩惱種生報，是牽引因。亦有從業種生現起，是生起因。從善不善業種生報，是牽引因。從現行不善業生因性煩惱，亦是引發因。言果亦如是隨應當知者，從五支名言種，生未來生老死果，即從異熟生異熟是生起因。從異熟生煩惱及生於業，是攝受因。」</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="59p4790"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》煩惱業生等者：分別緣起初勝法門經說：無明普於一切煩惱雜染、諸業雜染、諸生雜染能作因緣根本依處。由是故說煩惱為因。異熟自體，從後有業煩惱所生，能隨順生一切煩惱，由是說言果亦如是。三界差別，隨應當知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《分別緣起初勝法門經》說：根本無明是普遍存在於一切煩惱的雜染、諸業雜染、諸生雜染中。有煩惱的時候都有無明，造業的時候也有無明，因為不明白事情的真相就會去造作種種的業（諸業雜染），造不同的業將來就會得到不一樣的異熟果報（諸生雜染），而到欲界、色界及無色界三界去受生，這些雜染都是因為無明造成的。無明是諸雜染因緣的根本依處，所以說煩惱為諸雜染的因，此處煩惱是指無明。異熟自體，是從後有業煩惱所生。現在有煩惱造業將來就會得一個異熟果報體，將來得到的果報體稱為後有，而成就果報體的業煩惱，稱為後有業煩惱。有果報體以後，依果報體還能生出種種的煩惱。煩惱為因造業潤生得異熟果，異熟果為因又生出煩惱，所以說果也是一樣。三界的因果都是不離無明煩惱，都是無明煩惱所攝。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、簡差別</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科簡差別，簡別煩惱感果與否的差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">欲界一分不善煩惱，有異熟果。應知所餘，無異熟果。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　欲界有善法、無記法及不善法的煩惱，只有屬於不善性的煩惱品類有不可愛的異熟果。煩惱使令有情造業，因而招感異熟果。應知所餘不發惡業的善、無記法，不會招感不可愛的異熟果。這裡異熟果指的是往惡趣的異熟果。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》欲界一分不善煩惱等者：欲界煩惱，一分能發業者，當知不善，能往惡趣有異熟果。若彼所餘不發業者，非不善故，當知無異熟果。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　欲界的煩惱有一部分能夠造惡業的是屬於不善性的，能夠令有情得到生往惡趣的異熟果，墮到三惡道。如果是其餘的煩惱種子還在隨眠狀態尚未引發業力，或者善、無記法，不是不善的，不會引發造作惡業，因此不會得到惡趣的異熟果報。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申六、迷行轉2　酉一、麤相2　戌一、指前列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科迷行轉，迷惑於真理的轉相，分二科；第一科麤相，說明麤相，又分二科；第一科指前列，指出如前〈本地分〉已列出七種。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="43254:47563"></a>迷行轉者，如本地分七種已列。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　迷行轉方面，是指內心有煩惱，迷惑於真理，不明白諸法實相；有煩惱迷惑的心有種種的相貌，如前〈本地分〉中說有七種，已經列出說明。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》如本地分七種已列者：本地分說：又由七門，一切煩惱於見及修能為障礙應知。謂邪解了故，不解了故，解了不解了故，邪解了迷執故，彼因依處故，彼怖所生故，任運現行故。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/08.htm#47564:5424">陵本八卷四頁557</a>）今決擇彼，故指彼說。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在〈本地分‧有尋有伺等三地〉卷8，230頁那裡列出七種，但只有列出名字沒有解釋，現在決擇分的文，要將這段文取出來說明。這七種煩惱能夠障礙見道及修道，令有情無法成就聖道、成為聖人、成為阿羅漢、成就無上菩提。七種煩惱，一是邪解了，對緣起法、世出世間的因果有錯誤的認知；二是不解了，對緣起法、世出世間的因果不明白；三是解了不解了，對緣起法、世出世間的因果有懷疑；四是邪解了迷執故，對緣起法、世出世間的因果有錯誤的認知又生起執著，這是見道所斷分別起的煩惱；五是彼因依處故，這些煩惱的依止處指苦諦與集諦；六是彼怖所生故，由迷滅、道二諦而生怖畏的煩惱；七是任運現行故，俱生起任運現行、屬於修所斷的煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、釋義別2　亥一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋義別，解釋道理的差別，分二科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">義別云何？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這七種迷於緣起諸行而生的煩惱，在義理麼上有什差別？&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="59p4791"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、釋7　天一、邪了行</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分七科；第一科邪了行，邪解了的相貌。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="5428:47570"></a>謂薩迦耶見、邊執見、邪見，此三於所知境起邪了行，於四聖諦迷行轉故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　迷行轉的煩惱，第一種稱為邪了行。邪了行的相貌有三種，一有薩迦耶見：有我見。二有邊執見：有斷見、常見。三有邪見：有撥無因果、無父、無母、無真阿羅漢等邪見。這三種分別起的煩惱，於所知境界生起錯誤認知的心行，之所以會有這樣的邪解了行的煩惱，這是因為對於苦集滅道四聖諦有迷惑不了解造成的，這是卷8所說的邪解了。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、不了行</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科不了行，對緣起法、世出世間的因果不明白。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">無明一種，是不了行。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　迷行轉的煩惱，第二種稱為不了行。不了行就是無明煩惱，無明是指不明白諸法實相的煩惱。前面卷9曾說過十九種無明，對於自己過去、現在、未來的五蘊不明白，因果不明白，從煩惱因所生五蘊諸行不明白，苦集滅道四諦、佛法僧三寶通通不明白等，這是卷8所說的不解了。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天三、了不了行</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科了不了行，於諦寶等有了解、不了解行不能決定。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">疑，是了不了行。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　迷行轉的煩惱，第三種稱為了不了行。疑就是了不了行，心懷二路，一知半解，懷疑苦集滅道四諦底是有？還是沒有？四諦的道理是真實的？還是虛妄的？這是卷8所說的解了不解了行。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天四、執邪了行</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科執邪了行，有邪執的了解。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">見取、戒禁取及貪瞋等，緣見為境、見所斷者，彼一切皆是執邪了行。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　迷行轉的煩惱，第四種稱為執邪了行，包括見取、戒禁取及貪瞋等，緣見為境。見取是指對薩迦耶見、邊執見、和邪見等三種不正見，取著不捨，以為最勝、最妙、最上，以為由此見故，能得清淨解脫之果。戒禁取見是指隨順見取執行或受持邪戒，錯認以為是正戒。譬如有人持牛戒、狗戒等，以為是生天之因，又有一般人塗灰斷食，錯認以為是涅槃之道等；還有遇可愛境界生起貪心、耽染愛著。遇不可愛境界生起瞋心、瞋恚忿怒。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這些煩惱都是以我見為根本而產生的，擾惱有情身心，所以說緣見為境；這些都是不如理作意分別所起的煩惱，不是俱生的，因此說為見道所斷的煩惱。以上所敘述的煩惱都是屬於執邪了行，也就是卷8所說的邪解了迷執故。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天五、迷彼因緣所依處行</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科迷彼因緣所依處行，迷於因緣依處所生執著的邪了行。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">即此一切迷苦、集諦者，是迷彼因緣所依處行。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　迷行轉的煩惱，第五種稱為迷彼因緣所依處行，迷惑生彼世間因果之因緣所依處的煩惱心行，也就是迷惑於四諦中的苦諦與集諦的種種煩惱。因為不明白苦諦，也不明白集諦，不明白生死流轉因緣所依止的處所，所以不斷於三界生死輪迴，這是卷8所說的彼因依處故。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="59p4792"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》是迷彼因緣所依處行者：攝事分說：觀彼後際集諦依處，當知即是現在苦諦。後際苦諦所依止處，當知即是後際集諦。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/93.htm#47580:71090">陵本九十三卷七頁7008</a>）由是故說，苦集是因依處。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　〈攝事分〉說：觀察將來生命體的集諦（後有愛）的依止處，當知就是現在的苦諦，也就是現在的生命體。以現在的生命體為依止，希求來生有更可愛的生命體，就會產生將來生命體的苦諦（果）。將來生命體的苦諦（果）所依止的地方，也就是產生的因緣，是將來生命體的集諦，即後有愛及業，集諦是因，苦諦是果。所以說，苦集是生死因緣所依處。在〈攝事分〉卷93，2744頁還會再解釋。這是第五種迷彼因緣所依處行，也就是卷8所說的彼因依處故。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天六、迷彼怖畏生行</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科迷彼怖畏生行，由迷惑怖畏所生執邪了行。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">即此一切迷滅、道諦者，是迷彼怖畏生行。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　迷行轉的煩惱，第六種稱為迷彼怖畏生行，是迷惑於四諦中的滅諦與道諦所生的種種煩惱。成就道諦的功德，證得滅諦滅靜妙離的境界，對於這件事內心有迷惑，有所怖畏，所以不願意去修行成就聖道，是卷8所說的彼怖所生故。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天七、任運現行迷執行</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第七科任運現行迷執行，由於俱生任運現行的迷執行。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">即彼一切任運所起修道斷者，是任運現行迷執行。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　迷行轉的煩惱，第七種稱為任運現行迷執行，就是任運所起修道所斷的一切煩惱。任運、自然而生起的微細煩惱，是俱生的，不是不如理作意分別起的煩惱，也就是卷8所說的任運現行故。現在迷行轉的七種煩惱，其實就是在解釋前面的十種煩惱，薩迦耶見、邊執見、邪見、見取見、戒禁取見、貪、恚、慢、無明、及疑，只是換另外一個角度來說明。迷行轉將煩惱的相貌，分為見道所斷的前六種與修道所斷的第七種，做七種解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、細相2　戌一、牒前生後</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科細相，前面說的是迷行轉的麤相，現在要說迷行轉的細相，闡釋比較微細的相貌，分二科；第一科牒前生後，牒是表白的意思，說明前文生起後文。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，如前所說一切煩惱障治差別，但依化宜顯示麤相，建立煩惱迷執邪行。為令所化有情於種種煩惱諸行過失易生解故，今當總辯一切煩惱如實巨細之相，建立迷執諸行差別。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，如前文所說的煩惱雜染障礙對治差別：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、相續成熟對治（十三種資糧道）；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、近斷對治（煗頂忍世第一法決擇分善）；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、一分斷對治（見道），四、具分斷對治（修道）。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　請參閱〈決擇‧有尋有伺等三地〉卷58，1935頁煩惱障對治差別。這是論主為了教化眾生應該先說明煩惱的麤相，施設建立有煩惱眾生迷惑、執著、錯誤認知的內心情況，前面說的是麤相。為了使令所教化的眾生，更一步對於種種煩惱產生的邪行過失，能夠容易了解，現在要總體的、巨細靡遺的說明一切煩惱真實的相貌，（巨，指全面的、廣泛的、粗顯的。細，指細緻的、微細的、不易察覺的），依有事無事、諸根相應差別施設建立有煩惱眾生迷惑執著錯誤認知的種種心行差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、辨釋差別2　亥一、有事無事辨2　天一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科辨釋差別，詳細說明它的差別，分二科；第一科有事無事辨，說明什麼是有事什麼是無事，又分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="46734:47588"></a>問：如是諸煩惱，幾有事？幾無事？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：前面所說的十種煩惱，哪一些是有事？哪一些是沒有事？事，乃依阿賴耶識中種子所變現的根身、器界、前七轉識等因緣變所生之性境（本質境）說為有，即世俗實有。換言之，當所貪、所瞋、所癡、所執之見的所緣境，涉及世俗實有那一分，該貪等煩惱即屬於有事。也就是說，我見依因緣因緣變所生法之五蘊性境（本質境）說我之一分，乃屬有事；依此類推邊見一分、我慢一分亦屬有事。以上為修道所斷。無事，乃相對事說無，即事的反面，或說為理。理，乃依因緣因緣變所生法為空，依空理而安立，理依事顯，理本身不是事，名無事煩惱。換言之，當所貪一分、所瞋一分、所癡一分、所疑全分、所執之見一分可在見道時依理除遣之，該貪等煩惱即說為無事。又，前說所執之見一分，可包括見取見全分、戒禁取見全分、邪見全分、我見可依理除遣之一分。依此類推，可知有屬於無事之邊見一分、我慢一分。以上乃見道所斷。備註：見、修所斷煩惱採取〈本地分〉中所說，《披尋記》將有事歸為修道所斷，無事則屬於見道所斷。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　註：因緣變指由因緣所變現之法，為分別變的對稱。唯識家將心所緣之境（即相分），分為因緣與分別二變；其中以先業異熟（善惡業種子）為增上緣，由諸法自身之種子為因所變現者稱為因緣變；而從能緣心之作意、計度等分別力所生者為分別變。《成唯識論》卷2云︰「有漏識變略有二種︰一、隨因緣勢力故變，二、隨分別勢力故變。初必有用，後但為境。」</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、答3　地一、無事</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分三科；第一科無事，依止於無事而生起的煩惱事。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：諸見與慢是無事，於諸行中實無有我而分別轉故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：諸見包括薩迦耶見一分、邊執見一分、見取見全分、戒禁取見全分及邪見全分，這些見以及高慢心一分的煩惱是屬於無事的。因為這些煩惱是由分別我執，即前說「薩迦耶見一分」所引起的，雖然一切有為法五蘊諸行當中，依因緣變所生法為空之理，根本沒有我這件事，唯由內心虛妄分別、不如理作意的分別而生起 ，所以說是屬於無事的煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="59p4793"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地二、有事</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科有事，依止於有事而生起的煩惱事。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">貪、恚是有事。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　貪心一分是緣可愛的世俗實有境界所引起的，瞋心一分是緣不可愛的世俗實有境界所引起的，所以說是屬於有事的煩惱。貪、瞋僅一分有事。然而受論文所限，餘有事煩惱只有從略。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地三、通二</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科通二，通二種。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">無明、疑通二種。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　此處論文說：無明及疑這二種煩惱通於無事及有事，於事及理不明白都可生起無明和疑。若依前備註而詮釋，則疑應僅通無事，為見道所斷之煩惱。</span></span></span></div>
