<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》貪恚是有事者：緣愛非愛事境生故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　因為緣到可愛或不可愛事的世俗實有境界而所引生貪恚，所以說貪恚是有事。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、諸根相應辨2　天一、明建立2　地一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科諸根相應辨，諸根是指苦樂憂喜捨五受根，說明煩惱與五受根相應的情況，分二科；第一科明建立，建立諸根相應，又分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="46724:47599"></a>問：是諸煩惱，幾與樂根相應？乃至幾與捨根相應？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：這些煩惱，哪些是與樂根相應？乃至哪些是與捨根相應？&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地二、答2　玄一、約任運生煩惱辨2　黃一、總標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科約任運生煩惱辨，約任運產生的煩惱來說明，又分二科；第一科總標，全部標示出來。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：若任運生一切煩惱，皆於三受現行可得。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：非分別起的，或說俱生起的，稱為任運生，任運生的煩惱，於順境相、違境相、及中容境相皆不相違，所以三受現行當中都存在任運生的一切煩惱。領順境相，適悅身心，說名樂受；領違境相，逼迫身心，說名苦受；領中容境相，於身於心，非逼非悅，名不苦不樂受。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》若任運生一切煩惱等者：若諸煩惱非分別起，名任運生。於一切位皆不相違，是故三受現行可得。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如這一類的煩惱不是由分別而生起的，稱為任運生。於順境相、違逆境相、及中容境相，這些煩惱都會自然而然的產生，三受現行當中都存在任運生的一切煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">黃二、別辨</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科別辨，各別說明任運生煩惱與諸根相應的情況。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">是故通一切識身者，與一切根相應；不通一切識身者，與意地一切根相應。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果這類煩惱通於前五識及六一切識身，即通俱生起的身心二受則能與苦、樂、捨等三受根相應。如果這類煩惱不通於前五識身，只通於心受，則與意地的一切的苦、樂、捨三受根相應。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="59p4794"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》通一切識身等者：通五識身及與意地，名通一切識身，彼諸煩惱與苦、樂、喜、憂、捨相應。若唯意地，不通五識，是名不通一切識身，彼諸煩惱唯與意地喜、憂、捨根相應。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　通於前五識與六識，稱為通一切識身。通一切識身生起的一切煩惱與苦、樂、喜、憂、捨受都會相應。如果只是通於意地的六七八識，不通於前五識，稱為不通一切識身。唯通於意地生起的一切煩惱只有與喜、憂、捨等三根相應。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《成唯識論俗詮》卷5解釋這段文：「一切識身者，指前五識。取五塵境，名為身受。身是異熟果，名無覆無記性。言徧與一切根相應者，一切根，即苦樂捨根。謂無覆無記苦、無覆無記樂、無覆無記捨。通三受。不通一切識身者，是除去身受。意地一切根相應者，意地是心，取法塵境，名為心受。通善不善、有覆無記、各與三受相應。謂善苦受、善樂受、善捨受；不善苦受、不善樂受、不善捨受；有覆無記苦受、有覆無記樂受、有覆無記捨受。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　綜合上二種解釋，俱生起的身心二受則能與苦、樂、捨等三受根相應。如果這類煩惱不通於前五識身，只通於心受，則與意地的一切的苦、樂、捨三受根相應。不說憂喜二受，是因為憂喜二受唯與意識的分別相應。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　此處《披尋記》的解釋，應是依據《瑜伽論記》卷17景法師說：「任運唯意地得與憂喜捨三根相應。」所以這樣解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">玄二、約不任運生煩惱辨3　黃一、標說一切</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科約不任運生煩惱辨，辨明不是任運生的煩惱與諸根相應的情況，分三科；第一科標說一切，標出來說明一切。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">不任運生一切煩惱，隨其所應諸根相應，我今當說。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　不是任運生起的煩惱，也就是分別起的煩惱，隨其所相應的諸根，苦、樂、喜、憂、捨等五根（五受），產生煩惱的相貌，下文將詳細說明。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">黃二、舉十煩惱8　宇一、貪相應2　宙一、略標舉</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科舉十煩惱，舉出十種煩惱與諸受相應的情形，分八科；第一科貪相應，說明貪相應的情況，又分二科；第一科略標舉，先要略標示列舉出來。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">貪於一時樂、喜相應，或於一時憂、苦相應，或於一時與捨相應。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　生起貪煩惱時，有時是與樂受、喜受相應；或有時與憂受、苦受相應；或有時在捨受時也會有貪。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">宙二、問答辨2　洪一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科問答辨，提出問題而後回答說明，分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：如何等？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：怎麼樣在五受當中生起貪心？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">洪二、答3　荒一、憂苦相應</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分三科；第一科憂苦相應，說明與憂苦相應的情形。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：如有一，或於樂受起會遇愛、不乖離愛而現在前，遂於樂受不會遇、非會遇，若乖離、非和合；或於苦受起不會愛、若乖離愛而現在前，遂於苦受合會、非不合會，不乖離、非乖離。由是因緣，貪於一時憂、苦相應。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：假如有一位眾生，希望遇到樂受，與樂受和合在一起，不願離開樂受，這種不乖離愛生起時，可是對於樂受的境不能會遇、也沒機會再遇到樂受，對樂受形同乖離，無法與樂受和合在一起。此時因為想得到樂受卻得不到樂受，所以稱為與憂受相應的貪煩惱。或是不想與苦受和合在一起，希望不要有苦受，這種乖離愛生起時，結果無法不與苦受和合在一起，不想得到苦受卻還是會遇到苦受，這是與苦受相應的貪煩惱。由於上面的種種因緣，貪煩惱有時與憂受、苦受相應。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="59p4795"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">荒二、喜樂相應</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科喜樂相應，說明喜樂相應。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">與此相違，喜、樂相應。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　與憂、苦相應的貪煩惱情況相反，就是與喜、樂相應的貪煩惱。想要遇到樂受與樂受和合在一起，剛好碰到的境界也是快樂，此時因為想得到樂受也得到樂受了，這是與喜樂受相應的貪煩惱；不想要與苦受和合在一起，希望不要有苦受，剛好碰到的境界也是如意的，此時因為不想得到苦受也如願的離開苦受，這是與樂受相應的貪煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">荒三、捨根相應</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科捨根相應，說明捨根相應的貪煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若於不苦不樂位而生味著，當知此貪捨根相應。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　假如對於處在不苦不樂受的五蘊諸行，生起愛味、貪著，譬如對於身體生起貪愛心，應當知道這是有貪的捨根相應。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》由是因緣貪於一時憂苦相應者：樂受生時，起和合愛；苦受生時，起別離愛。於爾所時，違緣現前，憂、苦相應，義如前知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　樂受生起來時，希望與樂受在一起，起和合愛；苦受生起時，希望離開苦受，起別離愛。在那個時候，想要得到的境界與出現的情況剛好相反，所求不如意，貪煩惱就與憂、苦根相應，道理如前面所說的，應該容易明白。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">宇二、恚相應2　宙一、略標舉</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科恚相應，前一科是說貪相應，現在說到恚相應，說明瞋心相應的情況，分二科；第一科略標舉，要略標示列舉出來。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">恚於一時憂、苦相應，或有一時喜、樂相應。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　瞋心有時候是與憂、苦根相應，有時候是與喜、樂根相應，以下再詳細說明。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">宙二、問答辨2　洪一、憂苦相應</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科問答辨，提出問題回答說明，分二科；第一科憂苦相應，與憂苦相應的恚。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：如何等？答：如有一，自然為苦逼切身心，遂於內苦作意思惟，發恚恨心；或於非愛諸行有情及諸法所作意思惟，發恚恨心。由是故恚憂、苦相應。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：這種情況怎麼說？答：假如有一位眾生，身體與心靈為苦所逼迫時，於是內心對於苦受不如意的境界，有所警覺而引起思量的運作，自然發起瞋恨心；或是對於不喜歡的人、怨敵、事、以及有為法，於是內心對於所憂慮的境界，有所警覺而引起思量的運作，發起瞋恨心。由上述的情況，所以說瞋心與憂、苦根相應。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">洪二、喜樂相應</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科喜樂相應，與喜樂相應也會生起瞋心。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="59p4796"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：恚與喜、樂相應，如何等？答：如有一，於怨家等非愛有情起恚惱心，作意思惟：願彼沒苦，沒已不濟；或不得樂，得已還失。若遂所願，便生喜、樂。由是故恚喜、樂相應。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：瞋心與喜、樂根相應是怎麼樣發生的？答：假如有一位眾生，對於有怨恨的人、仇人等有情，生起瞋恚惱怒的心，有這樣的想法：希望他們早點死，或沈沒在痛苦裡面；死了以後沒有人救濟同情、幫他們辦理後事，或沈沒在痛苦裡面沒有人救濟同情，解救他們的痛苦；或者活的時候得不到快樂，就算得到快樂也會很快失去。這位眾生因瞋心這樣作願，也真的如他所願，於是便生喜、樂之心。因為上述的情況，所以說瞋心與喜、樂根相應。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">宇三、薩迦耶見及邊執見相應2　宙一、舉常見攝3　洪一、喜根相應</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科薩迦耶見及邊執見相應，說明有我見、邊見時與受根相應的情形，分二科；第一科舉常見攝，舉出常見所攝，又分三科；第一科喜根相應，說明常見與喜根相應的狀況。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">薩迦耶見及邊執見，若於樂俱行蘊觀我我所，或觀為常，喜根相應。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　我見及邊執見，如果於享有快樂的人天五蘊，觀察思惟後，認為樂受俱行的五蘊是我，或者是我所擁有的，或者認為是常恆住不變異的，這是屬於喜根相應。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">洪二、憂根相應</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科憂根相應，說明常見與憂根相應的情形。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若於苦俱行蘊觀我我所，或觀為常，憂根相應。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果於感覺痛苦的三惡道的五蘊，觀察思惟後，認為苦受俱行的五蘊是我，或者是我所擁有的，或者認為是常恆住不變異的，這是屬於憂根相應。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">洪三、捨根相應</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科捨根相應，說明常見與捨根相應的情形。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若於捨俱行蘊觀我我所，或觀為常，捨根相應。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果對於五趣眾生的五蘊捨受的本質，觀察思惟後，認為捨受俱行的五蘊是我，或者是我所擁有的，或者認為是常恆住不變異的，這是屬於捨根相應。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">宙二、例斷見攝</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例斷見攝，說明斷見所攝的情況。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">斷見攝邊執見，當知一切與彼相違。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　斷見所攝的邊執見，應當知道與常見所攝的邊執見相反。如果與樂俱行蘊的時候，認為我或我所會斷滅，因為擔心死了以後現在的快樂就沒有了，是屬於憂根相應。如果與苦俱行蘊，認為我或我所會斷滅，因為現在很苦，死了以後現在的痛苦就沒有，將來就不用再受了，是屬於樂根相應。這是與常見所攝的邊執見相反。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">宇四、見取戒禁取相應</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科見取戒禁取相應，說明見取、戒禁取與受相應的情形。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">見取、戒禁取，取彼見故，隨其所應，如彼相應。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　見取是執著薩迦耶見等諸見，認為自己所執的諸見是最高的、最殊勝的見解；戒禁取，是隨順見取的執著，而產生所有身語戒禁，這二種都是取著前面所說的薩迦耶見、邊執見，因此與五受根相應的情形，與薩迦耶見、邊執見的情形一樣。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="59p4797"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》見取戒禁取等者：由見取、戒禁取，取彼薩迦耶見、或邊執見為境，諸根相應，如彼見說，於俱行蘊苦、樂、捨別，隨應當知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如前文所說的，因為見取及戒禁取，取著前面所說的薩迦耶見、或者是邊執見為境，與五受根相應的情況，就如前面我見還有邊執見所說的一樣。見取及戒禁取於苦受、樂受、或者是捨受俱行相應的五蘊生起執取與諸受相應，與薩迦耶見於諸受俱行相應的五蘊觀我我所，或觀為常而生諸受的情況是一樣的，應當知道。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">宇五、邪見相應</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科邪見相應，說明邪見與受相應的情形。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">邪見一種，先作妙行，憂根相應；先作惡行，喜根相應。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　邪見這一種，於過去造作善好的業因，因有邪見而與憂根相應，認為自己做好事沒有好的果報，白白浪費。據《阿毘達磨大毘婆沙論》卷52說：或有一類人本來好行施與好行愛樂（養）、好行祠祀。彼人後來若遇邪見外道，聞說無施與、無愛樂、無祠祀、無妙行、無惡行、無妙惡行業果異熟，聞已憂慼作是念言：我從本來好行施與乃至祠祀極為唐捐。由於此人後悔所作妙行，因為妙行無果、無異熟故。這類邪見憂根相應。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有邪見這又於過去若造作惡的業因，有喜根相應。據《阿毘達磨大毘婆沙論》卷52說：或有一類人本來不好施與、不好愛樂、不好祠祀。彼人後來若遇邪見外道，聞說無施與、無愛樂、無祠祀、無妙行、無惡行、無妙惡行業果異熟，聞已歡喜作是念言：我從本來不好施與乃至祠祀甚為好事，因為布施等無果、無異熟故，這類撥無因果的邪見，喜根相應。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　總之邪見之人撥無因果，沒有因果觀念，於自己過去所做的妙行，心生憂悔而與憂根相應；於過去所做的惡行，認為不會有惡果而與喜根相應，這想見解與因果的道理剛好是相反的，是錯誤的想法，由此形成邪見。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">宇六、慢相應2　宙一、略標舉</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科慢相應，高慢心與五受根相應的情形，分二科；第一科略標舉，要略標示列舉出來。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">慢於一時喜根相應，或於一時憂根相應。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　慢也是一樣，有時候是與喜根相應，有時候與憂根相應。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">宙二、問答辨2　洪一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科問答辨，提出問題來回答這件事情，分二科；第一科問，提問。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：如何等？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：這件事怎麼說？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">洪二、答2　荒一、標列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科標列，標示列出二種。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：略有二慢。一、高舉慢，二、卑下慢。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：要略而言高慢心有二種：一種是與其他有情比較之後，自己實際上比較優秀，心就高舉起來了，這就是高舉慢。一種是與其他有情比較之後，事實上自己比較差，但自己卻認為沒差其他有情很多，這就是卑下慢。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">荒二、隨釋2　日一、喜根相應2　月一、廣高舉3　盈一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科隨釋，接著解釋這二種情況，分二科；第一科喜根相應，高慢心與喜根相應的情況，又分二科；第一科是廣高舉，詳細說明高舉的情況，又分三科；第一科標，標列出來。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又高舉慢，有三高舉。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又高舉慢，心高舉起來的情況有三種。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">盈二、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="59p4798"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">何等為三？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　到底是哪三種？&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">盈三、列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科列，列出來。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂稱量高舉、解了高舉、利養高舉。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　與其他有情比較之後，自己實際上比較殊勝，心就高舉起來了，是稱量高舉；明白事情的時候，了解得快，看得透，這樣使心高舉起來，是解了高舉；自己比較有錢，物質條件比較好，其他有情比較窮，心就高舉起來了，是利養高舉。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">月二、明相應</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科明相應，說明慢心與喜根相應。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此高舉慢，喜根相應。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　上面這三種高舉的慢心是喜根相應。稱量高舉，條件很好，與其他有情比，贏過他人。解了高舉，智慧高，明白事情快，事情看得透，學甚麼也都很快。利養高舉，確實比其他有情有錢，物質條件比他人好。因為這三種情況產生的高舉慢，讓自己生歡喜心，所以是喜根相應。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">日二、憂根相應</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科憂根相應，說明慢心與憂根相應。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若卑下慢，與彼相違，憂根相應。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果與其他有情比較，確實是條件比不上他人，但是覺得也沒有差很多；明明看不清楚事情，可是認為他人也不見得對；自己不是很有錢，對方很有錢，但認為自己的財富差不多，或者認為自己只是現在暫時沒有錢，也覺得有錢沒什麼了不起。這些卑下慢，與喜根相應的高舉慢是相反的，因為事實上自己條件是不太夠的，所以與憂根相應。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">宇七、疑相應2　宙一、憂根相應</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第七科疑相應，說明疑煩惱相應，分二科；第一科憂根相應，說明疑與憂根相應。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">疑，若於利養、恭敬、稱譽、樂善趣等決定事中，他所導引令猶豫者，憂根相應。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　疑，若是有人於善行能得到名聞利養、受他人恭敬、面前稱讚、後歎譽、及得到快樂的人天果報等決定事中，值遇惡知識告訴他說：根本沒有這些事。他心裡就會開始猶豫，這些事到底有或沒有？修善行的人死後可以得到人天的果報嗎？到人天趣是不是真的很快樂？這些事本來是好的，事實上他原來也覺得這些事情是殊勝的，可是現在又不決定了，真的是這樣子嗎？因此，他就不會覺得那麼歡喜，而與憂根相應。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">宙二、喜根相應</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科喜根相應，說明疑與喜根相應。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於無利養、不敬、譏毀、苦惡趣等決定事中，他所導引令猶豫者，喜根相應。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若是有人於惡行得不到利養，不受他人的恭敬、受他人的譏笑、毀謗，及得到痛苦的三惡道果報等決定事中，值遇惡知識告訴他說：根本就沒有這些事。他心裡就會開始猶豫了，這些事到底有沒有？修惡行的人，死了會得到三惡道的果報嗎？到三惡道是不是真的很痛苦？這些事本來是不好的，事實上他原來也覺得這些事情是令人痛苦的、害怕的，可是現在又不決定了，真的是這樣子嗎？因此，他就不會覺得那麼痛苦、害怕，就會與喜根相應。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">宇八、無明相應</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第八科無明相應，說明無明與五受根相應。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="59p4799"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">無明，通與五根相應。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　還沒有證得聖道以前，對諸法實相都是有疑惑的，這就是無明，無明通與一切苦樂憂喜捨受相應。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">黃三、略不說餘</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科略不說餘，要略說到此處，餘不多說。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">所餘相應，引事指斥，文不復現。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其他的隨煩惱與五受根相應的情況，引出事例來說明的文不再出現。以上是第一科明建立。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《大乘阿毘達磨雜集論》卷7〈1 諦品〉與此處所說略有不同，其中說到：「何故諸煩惱皆與捨相應？以一切煩惱墮中庸位方息沒故。所以者何？煩惱生起展轉相續漸漸微薄，勢力將盡墮處中位，於此位中必與捨受相應。」又所有煩惱背後都有無明為助伴，所有受都有不苦不樂受為助伴，所以所有煩惱必定都與捨受相應。此處對照〈決擇‧有尋有伺等三地〉卷58，1921頁所說，也可證明所以所有煩惱必定都與捨受相應。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、辨差別2　地一、指前說</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科辦差別，說明諸根相應差別的情況，分二科；第一科指前說，指出如前說。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">先辯煩惱諸根相應，但約麤相道理建立，令初行者解無亂故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如前所說煩惱與五受根相應，只是約粗相的道理來施設建立，為使令剛剛開始修學佛法的人正確理解，不生錯亂，因為他們一開始沒辦法了解得太深入，所以只大約這樣說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地二、顯今義</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科顯今義，顯示此處的義理。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">今約巨細道理建立，令久行者了自他身種種行解差別轉故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　現在這裡，以全面的、廣泛的、詳細的說明這個道理，建立任運生煩惱和不任運生煩惱與諸根相應的道理，使令久修的佛弟子，明白自己與他人種種身心的活動、種種煩惱的差別運轉的情況。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑三、煩惱聚2　寅一、總明三聚2　卯一、略標列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科煩惱聚，說明煩惱聚集的情況，分二科；第一科總明三聚，總相說明三聚，又分二科；第一科略標列，要略標列出來。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，諸煩惱略有三聚。一、欲界繫，二、色界繫，三、無色界繫。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，諸多煩惱要略而言有三聚，聚表示很多的意思，也就是說每一聚都包含了很多煩惱。這三聚是：一、屬於欲界的煩惱，二、屬於色界的煩惱，三、屬於無色界的煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、問答辨2　辰一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科問答辯，以問答的方式說明煩惱的三聚，分二科；第一科問，提問。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：如是三聚，幾不善？幾無記？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：在這欲界、色界、無色界三聚的眾生們都有煩惱，這些煩惱，哪一些是屬於不善？哪一些是屬於無記？&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、答2　巳一、釋差別</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科釋差別，解釋煩惱的差別。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：初聚一分是不善，餘二聚是無記。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：欲界眾生的煩惱，有一部分是不善的，色界與無色界的眾生也有煩惱，不過是無記的，就是有覆無記。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="59p4800"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、別料簡</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科別料簡，單獨思量簡別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">諸不善者是有異熟，非餘。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　不善法就是有煩惱，煩惱品這種不善法會有異熟果，會到三惡道去受果報，其他的善法及無記法，不會到三惡道受異熟果。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》初聚一分是不善者：此中義顯，欲繫煩惱亦有無記，今為簡彼，故說一分性是不善。此有異熟，非餘，是故前說欲界一分不善煩惱有異熟果，應知所餘無異熟果。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　此處文中義理上顯示，屬於欲界繫的煩惱也有無記性的，現在為了減除這一分無記的煩惱，因此說其中的一部分是不善的。不善法的煩惱品，能令感得三惡道的異熟果，不是其他的善法及無記法的煩惱品，因為善法招感樂果，有覆無記法力量不強，也不會到三惡道。所以前面說欲界屬於不善煩惱的這一部分，包括根本煩惱，隨煩惱，若這些煩惱很粗重很猛利，會感得三惡道的異熟果，其他的善法及無記法的煩惱品是沒有三惡道異熟果的。這裡是與前面相呼應的地方，就是色界無色界的煩惱都是無記的。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、辨聚體性2　卯一、長行列2　辰一、舉多少性</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科辨聚體性，說明煩惱聚的體性，分二科；第一科長行列，用長行列舉出來，</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又分二科；第一科舉多少性，舉出多或者是少的體性。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：幾多性？幾少性？答：初多性，餘不爾。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：這些三界的煩惱，哪一些是屬於很多的？那一些是屬於很少的？&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：初欲界的煩惱是很多的，因為緣六塵的境界而轉。餘上界的煩惱，譬如色界初禪雖然也能緣色、聲、觸、法四塵，但四種禪天的有情都只內緣法塵而生煩惱，無色界也只內緣法塵而生煩惱。可知欲界的人所緣境多煩惱也多，上二界的人所緣境少煩惱也少。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、例餘一切</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例餘一切，依例推理其他一切煩惱性。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如多性、少性，如是猛利長時染惱性、非猛利長時染惱性，發起外門雜染性、發起內門雜染性，發起惡行性、發起非惡行性，能生多苦性、能生少苦性，大有罪性、小有罪性，遲離欲性、速離欲性，不離欲所顯性、離欲所顯性，三摩地相違性、非三摩地相違性，非一種相生決定性、一種相生決定性等，當知亦爾。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　就如同欲界是多性，上二界是少性一樣，如是欲界的煩惱是非常勇猛、有力量而且發作的時間很長、相續不斷；而上二界的煩惱力量不是很強而且也不是長時間的。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　欲界眾生，緣慮外界的色聲香味觸而引起煩惱；上二界眾生，沒有欲界的欲，但味著禪定，緣慮內境而起煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　欲界眾生，會發出身語意的惡行，造作罪惡的行為；上二界眾生，因為已無瞋心，雖然也有煩惱，但是不會發起惡行。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　欲界眾生的煩惱，能產生很多的痛苦；上二界眾生的煩惱，能夠產生的痛苦不大。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　欲界的煩惱，能產生的罪過很大；上二界眾生的煩惱，能夠產生的罪過是很小的。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　欲界眾生很難離欲；上二界眾生，很容易就離欲了。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　欲界眾生沒有離欲；上二界眾生，已經離欲。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　欲界眾生沒有禪定，是三摩地相違性；上二界眾生已得禪定，是非三摩地相違性。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　欲界的眾生，所緣慮的境界有各式各樣的情況。如同欲界是多性，上二界是少性一樣。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　欲界的眾生有男有女，有各式各樣、高矮胖瘦等種種情況，是非一種相生決定性；上二界眾生，因為有禪定，內心所緣慮的是同一個境界，又色界眾生的身體都是一樣光明的相貌而且都沒有男女根，無色界眾生都一樣無業果色，是一種相生決定性等，應當知道也是一樣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="59p4801"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》非一種相等者：色無色繫定地所緣心一境性，名一種相生決定性。欲繫不爾，不能繫心於一所緣，名非一種相生決定性。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　得到色界天或無色界天定地的眾生，因為有禪定，內心所緣慮的是同一種境界，稱為一種相生決定性。欲界的眾生思想很混亂，想東想西，不能安住在同一種境界，稱為非一種相生決定性。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、嗢柁南結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科嗢柁南結，用一個偈頌總結前文，彙集上面這一段文的要義，重新以偈頌顯示，也稱重頌，因為這個偈頌是在文的中間，稱為中嗢柁南。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">中嗢柁南曰：</span></strong></span></span><br />
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　多染惱外門　惡行生諸苦　有罪遲離欲　三摩地生等</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以一個偈頌，說明三界眾生煩惱的特性及差別。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　多染惱外門：多，指欲界煩惱的事多；少，指色無色界煩惱的事少；染惱，欲界是猛利長時的染惱，色無色界不是猛利長時的染惱；外門，欲界是緣慮外界的色聲香味觸而引起煩惱；內門，色無色界是緣慮內境而起煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　惡行生諸苦：惡行，欲界發起惡行的煩惱，色無色界發起非惡行的煩惱；生諸苦，欲界的煩惱產生很多的痛苦，色無色界的煩惱產生較少的痛苦。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有罪遲離欲：有罪，欲界的煩惱產生的罪過是大的，色無色界的煩惱少有罪性；遲離欲，欲界眾生不容易離欲，色無色界眾生已離欲。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三摩地生等：三摩地，欲界眾生沒有禪定，色無色界眾生有禪定；生等，欲界眾生心裡有種種的所緣境，色聲香味觸眼耳鼻舌身，貪瞋癡男女，心裡想東想西，屬於非一種相生決定性，色無色界眾生的所緣境，只有一種，心一境性，屬於一種相生決定性。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑四、煩惱斷2　寅一、總徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科煩惱斷，說明煩惱斷的情況，分二科；第一科總徵，總相提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，云何能斷煩惱？齊何當言已斷煩惱？從何煩惱而可說斷？斷諸煩惱為頓、為漸？云何次第斷諸煩惱？諸煩惱斷，復有幾種？煩惱斷已，有何等相？諸煩惱斷有何勝利？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，怎麼樣才能夠斷煩惱？這是第一個問題。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　齊何，是一個分際，達到怎麼樣的境界、程度、界限，才可說已經斷除煩惱？這是第二個問題。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　從什麼樣的道理，說明煩惱是可以斷除？這是第三個問題。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　斷煩惱到底是頓斷還是漸斷？這是第四個問題。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如何次第的斷除煩惱？這是第五個問題。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　煩惱斷有幾種情況？這是第六個問題。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　煩惱斷了以後表現出來的相貌是怎麼樣？這是第七個問題。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　煩惱斷了能得到什麼殊勝的利益？這是第八個問題。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　連續提出八個問題，都是修行人最關心的問題。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、別釋7　卯一、能斷已斷6　辰一、約地差別辨</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科別釋，各別解釋回答這些問題，總共八個問題，將第一個能斷問題及第二個已斷問題歸納成一科合起來回答，分七科；第一科能斷已斷，說明能斷已斷的煩惱，又分六科；第一科約地差別辨，約境界的差別來說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂善法資糧已積集故，已得證入方便地故，證得見地故，積習修地故，能斷煩惱；得究竟地，當言已斷一切煩惱。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　大乘瑜伽唯識學將修行分成五個階位：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第一個階位是順解脫分的資糧位，這位階的善法資糧已經積聚圓滿，稱為善法資糧已積集故。善法資糧包含各式各樣的善法，如〈聲聞地〉卷22所說：自他圓滿善法欲等十四種資糧。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二個階位是順決擇分的加行位，是指已經進入到暖頂忍世第一四加行位的佛弟子，稱為已得證入方便地故，已經得到證入諸法實相的前方便，此時至少已成就未到地定，能於定中修習四諦等觀行。修行人要有未到地定以上的定力，才有能力開始斷煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三個階位是見道位，證得見道位的佛弟子，小乘的初果和大乘的初地菩薩，稱為證得見地故。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四個階位是修道位，已見道的佛弟子積極的修行往究竟位前進，但尚未得究竟位，這些修道位的佛弟子，稱為積習修地故，已經歷以上諸階位，能夠斷除煩惱，但尚未究竟斷除煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五個階位是究竟位，是指成就阿羅漢果、辟支佛、或是成就無上菩提的佛，達到究竟位，可斷除一切的煩惱。二乘是完全斷除煩惱障，大乘則煩惱障與所知障全部都斷除了，稱為得究竟地，因此說當言已斷一切煩惱。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以上以位階與斷煩惱的次第不同來說明，一、資糧位，努力積聚資糧；二、加行位，能夠證入方便，在奢摩他中修毗鉢舍那斷煩惱；三、見道位，斷除煩惱，見到諸法實相；四、修道位，繼續斷除剩餘俱生起的煩惱；五、究竟位，能斷除一切的煩惱。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="59p4802"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》謂善法資糧至已斷一切煩惱者：集論中說：道有五種，謂資糧道、加行道、見道、修道、究竟道。（集論六卷一頁）今說善法資糧，乃至得究竟地，如其次第，義顯五種道別，如彼廣釋應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《集論》中說：修行這條道路，分為五種位階，就是資糧道、加行道、見道、修道、究竟道。這五種位階上面已做詳細說明。現在這裡說善法資糧乃至得究竟地，如同《集論》的次第顯示有五種道別。在《集論》卷6，1頁廣泛詳細說明這五種位階，參考該處所詳細解釋的文應該能理解。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、約修瑜伽辨2　巳一、辨差別</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科約修瑜伽辨，由修止觀的角度說明，分二科；第一科辨差別，說明修止觀後斷煩惱的差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復有差別。謂由修習四種瑜伽，能斷煩惱；若善修習如是四種，當言已斷一切煩惱。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又有差別，修止觀後，尚有能斷煩惱與已斷煩惱的差別，這是說經由修習四種止觀，有能力斷除煩惱；如果善修習這四種止觀圓滿後，應當可說已斷除一切煩惱。善修習，是如理作意，運用善巧方便，數數修習，練習到非常的熟悉，可以很靈活的運用。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、指前說</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科指前說，什麼稱為四種瑜伽？前面已經說過，所以這裡不解釋了。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">四種瑜伽，如聲聞地已說其相。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這四種瑜伽，四種修止觀的方法，如〈聲聞地〉已經詳細說明它們的相貌了。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》四種瑜伽等者：信、欲、精進、方便，是名四種瑜伽。如聲聞地別釋應知。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/28.htm#47705:23494">陵本二十八卷九頁2354</a>）</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在〈本地分‧聲聞地〉卷28曾說明這四種瑜伽。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、信瑜伽：有二種行相與二種依處，能使心與止觀相應。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二種行相：一是信順行相，對佛說的三寶四諦能夠忍可、相信、隨順；二是清淨行相，於三寶四諦實有的功德能起清淨行的信。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二種依處，一是觀察諸法道理依處，於聞說三寶四諦的道理之後，能於其中觀察染淨因果實有不虛，依此產生信心；二是信解補特伽羅神力依處，見佛菩薩或聖弟子示現神通變化，因此生信。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　觀察諸法道理是法及理的力量，信解補特伽羅神力是人及事的力量，依這二種令行者內心具足信順行相及清淨行相，稱為信瑜伽。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、欲瑜伽：要有想修學善法的願。欲的內容包括：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　1. 為證得欲，要有為證得三乘聖道或無上菩提的願望，修學佛法才能有力量、能夠斷煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　2. 為請問欲，能很精進的去請問佛門中的善知識、修瑜伽有成就者，以廣聽聞深入思惟。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　3. 為修集資糧欲，想要成就聖道，必須有認真積聚資糧的願望。為隨順瑜伽欲，要有隨順修止觀的願望，努力去做，內心法喜充滿。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、精進瑜伽：有欲以後就要精進，才能成就，精進的內容包括：為聞精進，精進的聽聞佛法。為思精進，聽聞佛法之後，精進思惟、分別、觀察其中的道理。為修精進，為成就聖道，要數數修習止觀。為障淨精進，日夜精進的修習止觀，努力清除成就止觀的障礙，斷除五蓋。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、方便瑜伽：方便就是善巧的方法，成就修止觀要有方法，方法也有四種。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　1. 尸羅律儀增上力，要持戒，守持律儀，持戒清淨。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　2. 善守其念，要很注意自己這一念心，能夠常常安住在正念裡面。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　3. 能無放逸，因為善守其念，能令身語意三門毫無放逸。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　4. 心正於內，修習止觀。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　照著上面的方法，學習信、欲、精進、方便，這四種瑜伽，能夠斷煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在〈本地分‧聲聞地〉卷28，949頁那裡有詳細的說明，這是由第二個角度回答「云何能斷煩惱？齊何當言已斷煩惱？」。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="59p4803"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰三、約涅槃緣辨</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科約涅槃緣，緣慮涅槃來說明，以第三個角度的回答是約涅槃緣。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復有差別。謂相續成熟故，得隨順教故，內正作意故，對治道生故，能斷煩惱；修對治道已到究竟，當言已斷一切煩惱。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其中又有差別。以〈本地分‧修所成地〉卷20中所說的四處、七支，配合約涅槃緣辨斷煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、相續成熟，配第一支生圓滿。內外圓滿成熟時，自身信進念定慧五善根栽培成熟，也得到善知識的教導，稱為相續成熟。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、得隨順教，配第二支聞正法圓滿。包含正說法及正聞法圓滿，得到隨順修習止觀的教法。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、內正作意，配第三支涅槃為上首及第四支能熟解脫慧之成熟。聞正法圓滿後，必須內正作意，內心如佛法所說的去作意思惟，勤修止觀，以涅槃為上首，才能夠成熟解脫的智慧。修止觀的動機，要以追求聲聞乘無餘涅槃及大乘無住涅槃為終極的目標。在趣入最終目標的過成程中，止觀能夠逐漸有力量，也就能夠成熟解脫的智慧，讓我們智見清淨。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、對治道生，配第五支修習對治。修習止觀了以後就能夠對治煩惱，稱為對治道生。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　經過這四個步驟就能夠斷煩惱。修對治道已到究竟，配第六支世間一切種清淨及第七支出世間一切種清淨。世間一切種清淨，得到世間的四禪八定；出世間一切種清淨，斷除所有煩惱，從初果一直修到阿羅漢，或者是從初地一直修到無上菩提，對治煩惱這件事情已經圓滿了，稱為已斷一切煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以上是約涅槃緣辨明能斷煩惱及已斷煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》相續成熟等者：本地分中修所成地說：略由四處，當知普攝修所成地。何等四處？一者、修處所，二者、修因緣，三者、修瑜伽，四者、修果。如是四處，七支所攝。何等為七？一、生圓滿；二、聞正法圓滿；三、涅槃為上首；四、能熟解脫慧之成熟；五、修習對治；六、世間一切種清淨；七、出世間一切種清淨。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/20.htm#47710:16681">陵本二十卷一頁1699</a>）今此中說相續成熟，謂生圓滿；當知修處所攝。得隨順教，謂聞正法圓滿；內正作意，謂涅槃為上首、能熟解脫慧之成熟；當知修因緣攝。對治道生，謂修習對治；當知修瑜伽攝。修對治道已到究竟，謂世間一切種清淨、出世間一切種清淨；當知此修果攝。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　〈本地分‧修所成地〉卷20，709頁起裡面有說，要略由四個次第可以完全包含〈修所成地〉的內容。這四個次第是：&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一者、修處所，修止觀成就聖道的處所，包括內外等十種生圓滿。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二者、修因緣，諸法皆由因緣所生的，修止觀也要有因緣。因緣包括聞正法圓滿、涅槃為上首、能熟解脫慧之成熟三種。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三者、修瑜伽，說明正式修學止觀後，所遇到的障礙及能對治的方法。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四者、修果，修止觀有成就了，或證得世間清淨的禪定，或出世間清淨的聖道，名為修果。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這四處，是七支所攝。是哪七支？一、生圓滿；二、聞正法圓滿；三、涅槃為上首；四、能熟解脫慧之成熟；五、修習對治；六、世間一切種清淨；七、出世間一切種清淨。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　現在此處說相續成熟，指生圓滿；應當知道是修處所所攝。得隨順教，指聞正法圓滿；內正作意，指涅槃為上首、能熟解脫慧之成熟，應當知道是修因緣所攝。對治道生，指修習對治，應當知道是修瑜伽所攝。修對治道已到究竟，指世間一切種清淨、出世間一切種清淨，應當知道是修果所攝。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰四、約遍知永斷辨</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科約遍知永斷辨，約所遍知蘊處界事辨明煩惱能斷、已斷的差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復有差別。謂了知煩惱事故，了知煩惱自性故，了知煩惱過患故，煩惱生已不堅著故，攝受對治故，能斷煩惱；對治已生，當言已斷一切煩惱。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又有差別，從遍知永斷角度，來談能斷煩惱及已斷一切煩惱。於一切法，五蘊十二處十八界，無不了知的智慧稱為遍知，這種智慧能夠永遠斷除一切煩惱，成就此智慧的五個次第是：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、要了知煩惱事，煩惱的依止處，稱為煩惱事。煩惱會產生一定有依止處，這個依止處是不清淨的，這件事要認識。如果不知道這依止處是不清淨的，就沒辦法察覺有煩惱，也就不會去斷煩惱。這不清淨的依止處是對於一切法，五蘊十二處十八界，不清楚的認知造成的；不明了五蘊等一切法，是因緣所生，是無常、苦、空與無我的，由此而生煩惱。詳細說如〈決擇‧五識身相應地意地〉卷55所說貪由十事生等。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、要了知煩惱自性，若法生時其相自然不寂靜起，由彼起故，不寂靜行相續而轉，是名煩惱自性。煩惱的自性是不寂靜，煩惱有各式各樣的，要清楚的了解各種煩惱的自相、共相、差別相，才能一一對治種種的煩惱；例如，什麼是貪瞋癡慢疑？什麼稱為薩迦耶見？所以具備了知煩惱自性的知識是很重要的。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、要了知煩惱過患，要了解這些煩惱會帶來很多的過患，過去會有，現在也會有，將來還會有；這些過患會造就很多的罪，過去有罪，現在也有罪，將來還有罪；使令自己不自在，過去苦，現在也苦，將來還是苦。如果不知道有煩惱過患，就不會想要斷除煩惱了。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、要煩惱生已不堅著，每個人沒有圓滿成佛前，遇到境緣就容易產生煩惱，煩惱生了後，能正覺了分辨這是錯的，很快棄捨煩惱令心轉還，不堅著煩惱，要能夠如此對治煩惱，必須努力修行才做得到。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、要攝受對治故，就是如理作意，修習對治煩惱的方法，也就是修止觀。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　經過上面五個次第後，就能斷煩惱了。修止觀成功後，成就對治煩惱的智慧，能夠完全斷除煩惱，稱為當言已斷一切煩惱。以上是約遍知永斷辨，說明能斷煩惱的智慧及已斷一切煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》了知煩惱事故者：煩惱依處，名煩惱事。如前已說，貪由十事生，瞋事亦有十種，無明依七事起，慢依六事生，見依二事生，疑依六事生。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/55.htm#47713:43272">陵本五十五卷八頁4419</a>）如彼別釋應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　煩惱的依止處，也就是產生煩惱的因由，稱為煩惱事。如同前面已經有說明，貪心可以由十種事生起。能夠令生瞋心的事情也有十種；無明依止七種事情生起。高慢心依止六種事生起。種種的見取，執著思想上的煩惱，依止二種事生起。對聖道產生疑惑心是依止六種事生起。在〈決擇‧五識身相應地意地〉卷55，1817頁那裡有詳細的說明。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰五、約善修止觀辨2　巳一、辨差別</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科約善修止觀辨，約完整圓滿的修止觀來說明這件事情，分二科；第一科辨差別，說明它的差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="59p4804"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復有差別。修奢摩他故，修毗鉢舍那故，能斷煩惱；若諸相縛已得解脫，諸麤重縛亦得解脫，當言已斷一切煩惱。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　斷除煩惱，有二種差別。一是需要斷除心對於境相的執著，一是斷除煩惱的種子。必須能夠修止、修觀，既修止也修觀，才能夠斷除煩惱。如果已經解脫相的繫縛，煩惱種子麤重的繫縛也能得到解脫，則可以說已斷除一切煩惱。相縛，是色聲香味觸法六塵等相，緣境相而被繫縛，如果看到境相要知道它是不真實的，這是第一個要點。第二個要點，煩惱種子也解脫了，才能說已斷一切煩惱。若看到相，杯子、水就執著它是真實的，看到你、我、他都是真實的，第一種相縛就不能解脫，當然煩惱種子也沒辦法解脫。不能通達凡所有相皆是虛妄，就不能斷除煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、引教證</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科引教證，引聖教所說證明。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如世尊言：相縛縛眾生，亦由麤重縛。善雙修止觀，方乃俱解脫。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如佛在經中這樣說：眾生都被這些相牢牢的繫縛住，產生種種的煩惱，遇到境界發生各種的反應，這些反應就綁住心識，也因為有煩惱的種子，心被繫縛。唯有善巧、完整、圓滿的修習止觀，才能解脫相縛和麤重縛。如果只修觀會成乾慧、狂慧；如果只修止沒有智慧，缺乏智慧也不能斷煩惱。所以止觀都要圓滿的修行，才能解脫相縛和麤重縛。在斷分別我執的時候，證得無分別智，才能解脫相縛。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰六、約瑜伽所作辨</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科約瑜伽所作辨，約修止觀的作用來說明。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復有差別。謂了知所緣故，喜樂所緣故，能斷煩惱；所依已滅故，已得轉依故，當言已斷一切煩惱。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又有差別，約修止觀的角度來說明什麼是能斷煩惱的智慧，和已斷煩惱。必須了知所修的所緣境，修不淨觀、無我觀、我空觀、法空觀，必須明白通達這些所緣境應怎麼修，要正確的了解，才能斷煩惱；要歡喜這裡所說的種種善方便來斷煩惱，才能斷煩惱。修止觀的所緣境要明明白白，要清楚怎麼樣修止、怎麼樣修觀，正確的方法沒有拿到，喜樂所緣也不能斷煩惱。如果學到止觀的方法以後，要很喜歡繼續練習，這二條件具足可以使令行者斷煩惱。阿賴耶識中的煩惱種子，已經完全的滅除，使阿賴耶識轉捨雜染分，轉得清淨分，不再輪轉生死時，稱為已斷一切煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》了知所緣等者：本地分中聲聞地說：修瑜伽者，略有四種瑜伽所作。一、所依滅，二、所依轉，三、遍知所緣，四、愛樂所緣。如彼釋義應知。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/28.htm#47721:23655">陵本二十八卷十三頁2369</a>）</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　〈本地分‧聲聞地〉說：修止觀的人要作的事情有四種：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、所依滅，所依阿賴耶識中的煩惱種子必須滅除。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、所依轉，所依的阿賴耶識必須轉變，煩惱種子去除了，成就清凈的種子。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、遍知所緣，必須完全正確的了解所緣境的染淨差別。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、愛樂所緣，依遍知所緣斷染得淨心生歡喜，由此能愛樂修止修觀的所緣境，愛樂會有動機修行，有動機會有驅動的力量，有驅動的力量而能不斷修止修觀斷除煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在〈本地分‧聲聞地〉卷28，954頁那裏有詳細的解釋。以上是回答能斷已斷的第一個及第二個問題。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、斷所從3　辰一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科斷所從，從煩惱生起處斷煩惱，分三科；第一科標，標示出來。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，從彼相應及所緣故，煩惱可斷。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，斷煩惱的下手處，是從對治煩惱與心相應，使煩惱無從生起，不會再有煩惱緣境，就可以斷煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">所以者何？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這句話怎麼說？</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="59p4805"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰三、釋2　巳一、相應斷</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科相應斷，斷煩惱的相應。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">對治道生，煩惱不起，得無生法，是故說名斷彼相應。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有能對治煩惱的無分別智生出時，煩惱種子斷除，煩惱就不會生起，得到無生法忍，通達一切法是不真實的，沒有真實的因緣造作法，法本不生，證得無生法。煩惱與識相應，這件事不會再有了，因為將煩惱種子也斷了，稱為斷彼相應。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、所緣斷</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科所緣斷，從所緣境斷。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">相應斷已，不復緣境，故從所緣亦說名斷。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　無分別智生出時，根、塵、識、能所、器世間、語言六不現，此時心無分別，無所緣，不再緣境，因此說從所緣亦說名斷。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　於後得智與煩惱相應這件事已經斷除了，煩惱種子究竟斷除了，不會再緣境產生煩惱，於所緣境相，不會被它繫縛，也可以說是斷。這是回答前面的第三個問題。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯三、斷頓漸3　辰一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科斷頓漸，斷煩惱是頓斷或是漸斷，分三科；第一科標，標出頓斷。</span></span></span></div>
