<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，見斷煩惱頓斷，非漸。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，見道所斷的煩惱是頓斷，不是漸斷。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">所以者何？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這句話怎麼說？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰三、釋2　巳一、頓斷攝</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科頓斷攝，頓斷所攝。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由現觀智諦現觀故，能斷見道所斷煩惱。然此現觀與壞緣諦作意相應，是故三心頓斷一切迷苦諦等見斷煩惱。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　現量親證苦、集、滅、道四諦的真實相貌，稱為現觀智諦現觀，這是見道位時的智慧。這種無分別的智慧能斷除見道所斷的煩惱。這現前觀察的智慧，對苦集生起厭離心，與四諦真實的道理能夠相應，由我空智、法空智、我法二空智，這三心頓斷一切迷苦諦等見所斷煩惱。壞緣，是指對所緣的苦集諸行生厭離心。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="59p4806"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、漸斷攝</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科漸斷攝，漸次斷所攝。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">修斷煩惱漸次而斷，數數修道方能斷故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　修道時，斷除煩惱是漸次而斷，數數修道才能斷除。見道位的時候是頓斷，頓斷三界分別起的112種煩惱，通達我空、法空、我法二空真如，這是根據大乘的角度來說的。這是回答前面的第四個問題。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》與壞緣諦作意相應等者：謂從正觀四種諦理，起十六行智，從是以後，復轉修習。先緣自心總厭心智生，名壞緣諦作意相應。從此無間，無有加行，解脫見道所斷隨眠三心智生。一、內遣有情假緣智，二、內遣諸法假緣智，三、遍遣一切有情諸法假緣智。此中前二是法智，第三是種類智。如是三智，能斷一百一十二煩惱，如是煩惱十種所攝。一百一十二煩惱者，謂欲界見苦諦等所斷，各有十種；色無色界見苦諦等所斷，各有九種，謂各除瞋；如是名為一百一十二煩惱。是名三心頓斷一切迷苦諦等見斷煩惱。義如顯揚論說。（十七卷一頁）</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　從正確的觀察苦集滅道四種真實的道理，生起十六種內心的智慧。包括苦諦的苦、空、無常、無我四種行；集諦的因、集、生、緣；滅諦的滅、靜、妙、離；道諦的道、如、行、出。在〈本地分‧聲聞地〉卷34，1107頁起有詳細的解釋，如何觀察，如何斷除煩惱，稱為四諦十六行智，在四諦中要有這十六種心，來配合觀察四諦的所緣。正觀四諦十六種行以後，還要繼續的修習。先緣慮自己的心，相應於厭離苦集諸行的智慧生起，稱為壞緣諦作意相應。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　從此以後沒有間斷的、也不用再作意加行，這時能解脫見道所斷的煩惱種子，此時有三種智慧產生。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、內遣有情假緣智，內心遣除執著有情為我我所的虛妄分別，證得我空智。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、內遣諸法假緣智，內心遣除執著諸法是實的虛妄分別，證得法空智。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、遍遣一切有情諸法假緣智，內心完全遣除有情為我我所的虛妄分別，及諸法是實的虛妄分別，雙證我空和法空的智慧。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其中前二種緣我空、法空，是緣現在的五蘊所生，稱為法智。第三種是推察上二界的智慧，稱為類智。這三種智慧能斷除112種煩惱，〈本地分‧有尋有伺等三地〉卷8說過，這是薩迦耶見等十種煩惱所攝。112種煩惱，是指欲界見道位苦、集、滅、道四諦所斷的煩惱各有十種，共四十種；色、無色界是沒有瞋心的，這二界各只有九種煩惱，色界四處、無色界四處，共八處，九乘八是七十二，七十二加上欲界的四十，共為112種煩惱，稱為三心頓斷一切迷苦諦等見斷煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在《顯揚聖教論》卷17，1頁有說到，觀內心是無常苦空無我，不斷的內緣，到最後證得無分別智，就頓斷一切煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯四、斷次第2　辰一、辨8　巳一、在家攝</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科斷次第，斷煩惱的次第，分二科；第一科辨，說明，又分八科；第一科在家攝，在家斷煩惱的次第。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，最初應斷不善事業及諸惡見。謂在家者。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，在家者最初應斷除會使令自己或他人生起貪瞋癡，如殺生等不善的事業，及各種錯誤的思想，沒有因果的思想，有邪見的思想，這些顛倒的惡見。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、出家攝</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科出家攝，出家斷煩惱的次第。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">次復應斷樂出家障。謂欲尋思、恚尋思、害尋思。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，出家者，最初應斷除愛樂出家的障礙。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《瑜伽論記》說：凡夫在家障，包括染著色聲香味觸、男女欲的欲尋思，與瞋心相應的恚尋思，及傷害他人的害尋思。斷除欲尋思、恚尋思、害尋思現行才能使善法欲穩固，好樂出家、安住出家修道的生活。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳三、不定地攝</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科不定地攝，不定地所攝斷煩惱的次第。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">次復應斷不定心者三摩地障。謂眷屬尋思、國土尋思、不死尋思。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　出家以後應當修習禪定，因此又應斷除不能得定，不定心者成就三摩地（最初修欲界定漸次得未到地定）的障礙，亦即修定地資糧加行作意的障礙，包括：眷屬尋思、國土尋思、不死尋思。出家以後若仍時常憶念親里眷屬，生起眷屬尋思，希望親屬獲得安隱快樂，想到親屬衰惱的事就生起愁憂，若想到與親里種種歡娛的事，就生起掉舉；或是常常憶念要到哪個國家旅遊，生起國土尋思；或是生起不死尋思的想法：我應當慢慢修習聖道，應當先讀誦經、律、論等大小乘經典，乃至廣讀外道典籍，多畜弟子，牽引善人供養四塔，勸化眾生令大布施，以後再修聖道。這三種尋思都極為障礙修習禪定，應該觀察這些尋思的過患，不要陷入無義的尋思，才不會白白出家，入寶山而空手回。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="59p4807"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳四、定地攝</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科定地攝，定地所攝斷煩惱的次第。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">次復應斷得作意障。謂樂遠離品身諸麤重。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，又應斷除修禪定時成就得作意（得未到地定）的障礙，亦即修定地作意的障礙，即於歡喜遠離修習得作意的因地時，生起的五蓋及身疲倦性，如腰酸腿疼、體力不濟等身諸麤重。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳五、見斷攝</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科見斷攝，斷除見道所斷的煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">次復應斷見斷煩惱。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，應當斷除見道所斷的112種煩惱。這112種煩惱，是指依著三界迷於四諦所生起的欲界各有薩迦耶見、邊執見、邪見、見取見、戒禁取見、貪、恚、癡、慢、疑十種煩惱，及色、無色界（除瞋）迷於四諦所生的各有薩迦耶見、邊執見、邪見、見取見、戒禁取見、貪、癡、慢、疑九種煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳六、修斷攝</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科修斷攝，斷除修道所斷的煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">次復應斷修斷煩惱。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，應該斷除修道所斷的十六種煩惱。這十六種煩惱，是指於欲界對治修中，有六種煩惱迷執，包括薩迦耶見、邊執見、貪、恚、癡、慢；於色界及無色界對治修中，各有五種煩惱迷執，包括薩迦耶見、邊執見、貪、癡、慢，三界合有十六種煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳七、諸定障品攝</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第七科諸定障品攝，斷諸定障品所攝的煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">次復應斷屬苦、屬憂、屬樂、屬喜，及屬諸捨諸定障品障礙煩惱。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，應該斷除屬苦、屬憂、屬樂、屬喜以及屬諸捨的這些定障品障礙煩惱。在〈本地分‧三摩呬多地〉卷11，368頁說到出諸受事，得初禪可以斷除憂根，第二禪可以出離苦根，第三禪出離喜根，第四禪出離樂根，出世間的無相定，可以出離捨根等諸定障品障礙煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　佛於《無倒經》中說：行者於憂受等生起時，應當如實了知生起憂受等的因、緣、序、相、行才能斷除憂受等的障礙。知因：是指了知憂受等種子相續。知緣：是指了知生起憂受等的所依根，及與憂受等和合運轉的助伴心所。知序：是指了知憂受等託什麼事而生，能發憂受等的相狀及無明種子。知相：是指了知憂受等是慼行相等。知行：是指了知由不如理作意相應思而發起憂受等。能如是了知，就能於制持憂受等生起瞋等染污心，於思惟修能持堅住，證得各種禪定。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳八、所知障品攝</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第八科所知障品攝，斷諸所知障品所攝的煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="59p4808"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">次復有一補特伽羅，應斷所知障品諸障。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，修菩薩道的人，不只應斷除煩惱障，還應斷除引生所知障的障礙。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科結，結語。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由此次第，應斷煩惱。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由這八種，應該斷除煩惱。這是回答前面的第五個問題。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》應斷屬苦屬憂等者：苦等五根相屬煩惱能障諸定，本地分中三摩呬多地說：出諸受事，謂初靜慮出離憂根，第二靜慮出離苦根，第三靜慮出離喜根，第四靜慮出離樂根，於無相中出離捨根。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/11.htm#47763:8594">陵本十一卷十頁880</a>）能障諸定，一一差別翻彼應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　與苦樂憂喜捨根相屬的煩惱能障礙諸定，〈本地分‧三摩呬多地〉說：應當出離於種種受所引生的煩惱。得到初禪可以出離憂根；得二禪可以出離苦根，沒有苦受，入定時身體這些病痛苦沒有辦法障礙了；得到三禪可以出離喜根，喜受不會湧動；得到四禪可以出離樂根，必須出離三禪的樂根才能證到第四禪；證無漏的無相定可以出離與四禪及四空定相應的捨根，捨受也要出離，不可以耽著。〈本地分‧三摩呬多地〉卷11，368頁說過。五受能障礙初禪等定，一一差別，如卷11所說應知。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯五、斷多種2　辰一、略標列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科斷多種，斷除煩惱有多種，分二科；第一科略標列，要略標列出來。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，諸煩惱斷，當知多種，略則為二。一、諸纏斷，二、隨眠斷。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，各種煩惱的斷除，應當知道有很多種。要略可分為二種，一是煩惱現行斷除了。二是煩惱的種子也斷除了。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、隨別釋2　巳一、諸纏斷</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科隨別釋，接著各別解釋，分二科；第一科諸纏斷，斷煩惱的現行來說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">諸纏斷者，謂貪瞋斷乃至疑斷，薩迦耶見斷乃至邪見斷，見苦所斷斷乃至修道所斷斷，欲界所繫斷乃至無色界所繫斷，散亂斷、曉悟斷、羸劣斷、制伏斷、離繫斷。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　諸纏，煩惱數起現行稱為纏，斷除現行煩惱，可以分成九類：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、貪瞋斷，將貪心、瞋心乃至慢、無明、疑等五鈍使斷；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、薩迦耶見，乃至邊執見、見取見、戒禁取見、邪見等五利使斷；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、見苦所斷乃至修道所斷的煩惱斷，指見道及修道所應斷的各種煩惱必須斷除；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、欲界所繫欲恚害等煩惱，乃至無色界所繫煩惱斷，指三界所繫煩惱必須斷除；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、應斷除散亂心生起的諸惡尋思煩惱，散亂斷除才能得定；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　六、曉悟斷，明白了知、猛利的煩惱要斷除；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　七、羸劣斷，調伏煩惱，使煩惱的力量薄弱，稱為羸劣斷。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　八、制伏斷，依止定地作意得到禪定伏除煩惱；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　九、離繫斷，斷除煩惱種子。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　約煩惱的次第說：散亂斷、曉悟斷、羸劣斷、制伏斷、離繫斷。從沒有得禪定一直到得禪定以後，伏煩惱到最後斷煩惱種子，作了五個次第的說明。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="59p4809"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、隨眠斷</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科隨眠斷，斷煩惱種子。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">當知離繫斷，即是隨眠斷。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　應當知道離繫斷是將煩惱的繫縛完全斷除，是指隨眠斷：斷除煩惱種子。回答第六個問題。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》散亂斷等者：如前已說散亂對治、諫悔對治、羸劣對治、制伏對治、離繫對治。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/55.htm#47772:43203">陵本五十五卷七頁4413</a>）又說散亂位煩惱、諫悔位煩惱、羸劣位煩惱、制伏位煩惱、離繫位煩惱。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/55.htm#47772:43374">陵本五十五卷十頁4429</a>）由是今說彼煩惱斷亦有五種。於中少分名別義同。當知前四，謂諸纏斷；後一，謂隨眠斷。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如前面已說：散亂對治能對治散亂心；諫悔對治能對治犯戒的煩惱，如果沒有持戒清凈，不能得定；羸劣對治能調伏煩惱，使令煩惱微薄，不生起粗猛的煩惱；制伏對治，是指禪定的力量使煩惱不現行；離繫對治是斷除煩惱種子。又說散亂位煩惱，指未得定散亂心時的煩惱，如欲、恚、害等；諫悔位煩惱，犯戒時生起的煩惱，如忿、覆等；羸劣位煩惱，煩惱生起現行了，可是很薄；制伏位煩惱，禪定所對治定障品煩惱；離繫位煩惱，聖道所對治的煩惱種子。前面是能對治的智慧，名散亂對治等，後面是所對治的煩惱，名散亂位煩惱等，在決擇〈五識身相應地意地〉卷55，1820頁已說。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　因此說煩惱斷也有五種：散亂斷即散亂對治、曉悟斷即諫悔位對治、羸劣斷即羸劣對治、制伏斷即制伏對治、離繫斷即離繫對治。前面已經說過，這裏再重複說，名稱不一樣，但是道理是一樣的。前四種是屬於煩惱的現行，應當斷除，後一種是煩惱的種子也應當斷除。以上是回答前面的第六個問題：諸煩惱斷復有幾種？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯六、斷已相2　辰一、辨4　巳一、三毒不生2　午一、舉不生愛</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科斷已相，煩惱斷了以後的相貌，回答第七個問題，分二科；第一科辨，說明，分四科；第一科三毒不生，煩惱斷了以後三毒不生，又分二科；第一科舉不生愛，斷除煩惱以後不再生愛了。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，煩惱斷已，於可愛法若劣、若勝、若現在前、若不現前，雖猛利見而觀察之，亦不染著。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，煩惱斷了已後，對可愛法是較劣的、或殊勝的、現前接觸的境界、或者沒有現前的境界，雖然用力作意將最可愛的境界現前觀察，也不會染著，乃至數數的接觸這些可愛的色聲香味觸的境界，心裏也不會愛著了。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、例無瞋癡</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例無瞋癡，例不生瞋與癡。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如於可愛而不生愛，如是於可瞋法亦不生瞋，於可癡法亦不生癡。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如對於可愛的境界不會生起愛著，對於可生氣的境界也不會再生氣，對於可愚癡的境界也不會生起愚癡，貪瞋癡永斷。斷除煩惱的第一種相貌是三毒不生。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、住捨念知2　午一、舉眼見色</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科住捨念知，心裏安住在最上捨，正念正知，分二科；第一科舉眼見色，眼見色時但住於捨，正念正知。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="59p4810"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又眼見諸色，不喜不憂，但住於捨，正念正知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又眼看到種種的色，不論好的、不好的，過去、現在、未來，若劣若勝，若遠若近，若粗若細，心不喜也不憂，一切時住於最上捨，心裏沒有執著，安住在正念中，能正確的覺知所觀的境界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、例餘一切</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例餘一切。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如眼見色，乃至意知法亦爾。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如眼見色是這種情形，耳聞聲、鼻嗅香、舌嘗味、身覺觸、意知法，也是一樣，沒有貪瞋癡，一切時住最上捨，正念正知，心平等住這是斷除煩惱的第二種相貌。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳三、成沙門法2　午一、舉少欲</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科成沙門法，成就出家的沙門十法，分二科；第一科舉少欲，沙門法的特性之一是少欲。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又性少欲，成就第一真實少欲。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　已斷盡煩惱的阿羅漢，心性少欲，成就第一真實少欲。〈本地分‧聲聞地〉卷25，881頁說：少欲，是指雖然成就善少欲等所有功德，而不於此諸多功德欲求他人知道，讓他人知道我具足少欲成就諸多功德。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《雜阿含經》說：佛滅度之後時，阿育王遍禮諸塔廣施珍寶，聽聞薄拘羅少欲第一，於是布施一金錢，是時塔神又丟出來。阿育王不禁讚歎尊者：善哉！真實少欲！連一錢也不受。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、例喜足等</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例喜足等，例喜足等也一樣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如少欲，如是喜足、遠離、勇猛精進、安住正念、寂定、聰慧亦爾。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如同少欲，同樣的，少許資具就能歡喜滿足；遠離煩惱等雜染；能勇猛精進修習善法；能安住在佛法僧的正念；具足寂靜定力；身善、口善、意善具足聰慧者相也是一樣。這是斷除煩惱的第三種相貌，少欲、喜足、離染、精進、安住正念、寂定、聰慧。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳四、離諸戲論</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科離諸戲論，遠離沒有義利的戲論。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於無戲論任性好樂，於有戲論策勵其心方能緣慮。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　於沒有戲論，沒有名言分別、也沒有義利的境界，自然好樂，任運安住於第一義諦，心性好樂安住於無戲論界，於王論、國論、賊論、飲食論等有戲論的境界，必須鞭策鼓勵，特別作意，才能緣慮這些戲論，才會想這些事情。聖者的心任運都是清凈的，安住在空、無相、無願、無戲論的境界中，不像凡夫心裏面想的多半是色、聲、香、味、觸等戲論。這是斷除煩惱的第四種相貌，離諸戲論。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科結，結語。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="59p4811"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是等輩，當知煩惱已斷之相。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如是能夠做到沒有貪瞋癡三毒、安住最上捨、正念正知、成就出家人少欲、喜足、遠離、勇猛精進、不忘念、禪定、智慧等沙門莊嚴、內心沒有散亂與戲論的境界，這樣的人就是煩惱已經究竟斷除的相貌。以上是回答前面的第七個問題。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯七、斷勝利3　辰一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第七科斷勝利，諸煩惱斷的勝利，回答最後的問題，分三科；第一科標，標出來。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，煩惱斷者有多勝利。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，煩惱已經斷除的人有很多殊勝的利益。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、釋2　巳一、自義行攝2　午一、列超越</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科自義行攝，對自己有義利所攝，分二科；第一科列超越，列出能超越很多境界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂隨證得超越憂、苦，超越喜、樂，超越色想及與有對種種性想，超惡趣苦，超越生等一切種苦。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　斷除煩惱成就聖道的好處，若是俱解脫阿羅漢，能超越憂證得初禪，超越苦證得二禪，超越喜證得三禪，超越樂證得四禪，超越色想及與青黃赤白等顯色和合積集的有對礙想、飲食瓶衣乘等種種性想證得四空定；由於斷除見道所斷分別起的愛見煩惱，能超越惡趣苦、超越女人身、超越第八有業：不會有第八次來人天往返受報、超越北俱盧洲和無想天的業力，不會生到無暇處：沒有佛法的地方；由於斷除修道所斷俱生起的愛見煩惱，能超越生老病死、怨憎會苦、愛別離苦等三界生死一切種苦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》謂隨證得超越憂苦等者：此中超越憂、苦、喜、樂，謂由證四靜慮。超越色想及與有對種種性想，謂證無色。超惡趣苦，謂證有學。超越生等一切種苦，謂證無學。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　此文中說超越憂、苦、喜、樂四受，是指證得四種禪定。超越色想及與有對種種性想，是指證得無色定。證得有學初果以上能超越惡趣苦，超越生等一切種苦，是證得無學阿羅漢，永遠不會於三界生死輪迴了。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、明證得5　未一、安隱</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科明證得，說明超越以後證得的功德，分五科；第一科安隱，內心很安穩。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又證安隱第一安隱。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又有學聖者煩惱寂滅，內心沒有煩惱的動亂，分證涅槃，證得安穩；阿羅漢聖者，成就全分涅槃，究竟涅槃，證得第一安穩。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、清涼</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科清涼，證得清涼。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又證清涼第一清涼。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　煩惱是熱惱，離煩惱即清涼。有學聖者已斷除部分煩惱，證得清涼；無學阿羅漢，究竟斷除煩惱，證得第一清涼。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="59p4812"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》又證安隱等者：煩惱寂滅，是名安隱，亦名清涼。集論中說：何故此滅復名安隱？離怖畏住所依處故。何故此滅復名清涼？諸利益事所依處故。（集論五卷十四頁）在有學位所證寂滅，但名安隱及與清涼。在無學位，轉名第一，已究竟故，更無上故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　煩惱寂滅不再動亂，內心是很安穩的，是名安隱，也可以稱為清涼。《集論》中說：為什麼煩惱滅除也稱為安穩？因為煩惱是恐怖、畏懼的依止處，遠離煩惱時，內心不會恐怖、不會畏懼。為什麼煩惱寂滅時，又稱為清涼？因為所有有利益的事依止的就是清涼。煩惱滅了沒有怖畏，而且能做自利利他的各種事情，有利益的事都得到，內心很清涼。在有學位所證寂滅，只稱為安隱及與清涼；無學阿羅漢，轉稱為第一，因為已究竟斷除煩惱，沒有能夠超越他了，又稱為第一安穩、第一清涼。聖人也有差別，凡夫的差別更大。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未三、樂住自在</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科樂住自在，證得禪定很自在的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又得第一現法樂住，隨其自心自在而轉。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又斷除煩惱證得第一最殊勝的現法樂住：四禪八定、乃至滅盡定，使令自己能隨心自在而轉，任何時候能令心安住在聖住、天住、或梵住，乃至神力自在，心想事成。一般說第一現法樂住特指滅盡定。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未四、所證無退</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科所證無退，所證不再退轉。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若行、若住，隨所欲樂所證之法無復退轉。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　最殊勝的一點，所證得的聖道不會退轉了。於行住坐臥四威儀中，隨所歡喜做任何事，所證得的諸法實相都不會退失，這一點是最重要的。現法樂住的禪定，如果鈍根的人有可能會退失，但是聖道是永遠不會再退失了。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》隨其自心自在而轉者：謂於或聖、或天、或梵住中，隨所樂住，即能安住故。言聖住者，謂空住、無願住、無相住、滅盡定住。言天住者，謂諸靜慮、諸無色住。言梵住者，謂慈住、悲住、喜住、捨住。如本地分聲聞地說。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/34.htm#47807:28200">陵本三十四卷二十五頁2808</a>）</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　隨其自心自在而轉，是指對於聖住、或天住、或梵住中，隨所愛樂安住在哪個境界，心就能安住。聖住，是指空住、無相住、無願住及滅盡定住。由空住安住在我空、法空的清淨智，由無相住，安住在寂滅無相的第一義諦；由無願住，於後有及名言戲心不願樂；由滅盡定住，安住在前六識及染末那不現行的寂靜處。天住，是指能離欲界欲的四種靜慮，及能離色界欲的四空定。梵住，是指能與眾生樂的慈住、能拔眾生苦的悲住、能隨喜眾生善法功德的喜住、及能令眾生捨三毒的捨住。如〈本地分‧聲聞地〉卷34，1117頁所說應知。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未五、自義圓滿</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科證得自義圓滿，證得自義究竟圓滿。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於自義利圓滿究竟，於諸所作無復希望。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　對於自己有利益安樂的事情，已經圓滿究竟，證得無學果；對於所修的止觀，不再期待達到更高的境界，因為已經究竟圓滿了。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《佛地經論》卷1說：現在得到利益，稱為義，將來得到利益，稱為利；或世間，稱為義，出世間，稱為利；或遠離惡法，稱為義，攝受善法，稱為利；或福德稱為義，智慧稱為利。這位行者究竟斷除煩惱以後，於自己現在及將來的利益、世間、出世間的利益、遠離惡法、攝受善法、福德、智慧等都已圓滿，所作已辦，戒定慧圓滿，不必再有任何所作。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》於自義利圓滿究竟等者：此顯阿羅漢果諸漏已盡，所作已辦，無復所作，故作是說。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這是顯示阿羅漢果於自義利圓滿究竟，所有的煩惱已完全斷除；所有應該修的止觀、善法已經成辦，圓滿成功，不需要再有所作了，所以如此說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="59p4813"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、利他行攝</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科利他行攝，前面說的是對自己有義利的事情，這裏是屬於菩薩道利他行所攝的好處。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">或復有一修利他行，為欲利益安樂眾生，哀愍世間，令諸天人利益安樂。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　前文說明聲聞、辟支佛、乃至菩薩等三乘種性的人若究竟斷除煩惱，可以得到自義利，這裡特別指修大乘菩薩道的人，除了自義利還能成就眾生的義利，自利利他圓滿。如果有一位修利他行的菩薩行者，為了利益安樂無量眾生，哀愍世間，使令天上和人間的有情得到利益安樂，因為他能究竟斷除煩惱障，乃至超越聲聞行者斷除所知障，就能圓滿自利利他的功德。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰三、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科結，結語。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">當知煩惱斷者，有如是等眾多勝利。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　應當知道斷煩惱，如上所說，於自己的修道上，能超越諸受乃至三界苦果、又證得安隱、清涼、樂住自在、所證無退、自義圓滿，成熟自己的諸根、善根、智慧，於利他方面，能利益安樂無量眾生，成熟眾生的諸根、善根、智慧，令眾生獲得利益安樂等很多的好處。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以上是回答前面的第八個問題：斷勝利。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑五、煩惱所緣2　寅一、略標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科煩惱所緣，說明煩惱的所緣境，分二科；第一科略標，要略標出。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，煩惱緣境略有十五。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，煩惱的所緣境要略而言有十五種。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、列釋15　卯一、具分緣</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列釋，列出解釋十五種所緣，分十五科；第一科具分緣，遍緣一切事。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、具分緣。謂身見等。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、具分緣：遍緣一切事，稱為具分緣，如身見等。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、一分緣</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科一分緣，指貪瞋慢等。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">二、一分緣。謂貪瞋慢等。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、一分緣：指貪瞋慢等緣的一部分可愛、可瞋事生。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="59p4814"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》具分緣一分緣者：前說：貪、慢緣有漏一分可意事生，恚緣一分非可意事生，是故此三煩惱一分所生，名取一分。所餘煩惱，通緣內外若愛非愛，及俱相違有漏事生，是故說彼名曰遍行，取一切事。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/58.htm#47824:46730">陵本五十八卷六頁4717</a>）此中道理，如彼應釋。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　前文說，貪心、高慢心緣著有漏的一分可愛事而生，瞋恚緣著一分不可愛的事而生，所以說這三種煩惱是一分所生的，稱為一分緣。是緣一部分境界，不是遍緣一切境界的。其他的煩惱包括無明、疑，與薩迦耶見、邊執見、邪見、見取見、戒禁取見，通緣內身、外境，可愛、不可愛及非可愛非不可愛境等有煩惱的事而生，一切事情都可能生起這些煩惱，稱為具分緣。在〈決擇‧有尋有伺等三地〉卷58，1922頁有解釋其中的道理，應該要了解。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯三、有事緣</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科有事緣，諸有事煩惱與下面無事緣是一對。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">三、有事緣。謂諸有事煩惱。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、有事緣，是指由因緣所生法的蘊處界世俗實有事所生的煩惱，多分是修所斷的煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯四、無事緣</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科無事緣，諸無事煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">四、無事緣。謂諸無事煩惱。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、無事緣，是指見道所斷因迷理而起的十種煩惱。這些煩惱因內心分別而起，並不是有真實的事情在那裏，如凡夫可以無事生非，生出很多的煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》有事緣無事緣者：如前說：十煩惱，見所斷者，名曰無事，彼所緣事非成實故。所餘煩惱有事，彼相違故。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/58.htm#47829:46726">陵本五十八卷六頁4717</a>）此中道理，如彼應釋。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如前文說：十種煩惱，為見道所斷的，稱為無事，這類煩惱所緣不是世俗實有的境，多分是由分別我見而生起，以不解了因緣所生法為空之理而生起各式各樣的煩惱。其他修所斷的煩惱，與上說無事不一樣，是緣著任運的堅固事，由果報引起的種種煩惱，是比較微細、無記的煩惱。在〈決擇‧有尋有伺等三地〉卷58，1922頁中有說到。如那裏的解釋，應該要曉得。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又卷58說：「見修所斷諸漏煩惱，當知略有五種所緣。一緣邪分別所起事境、二緣見境、三緣戒禁境、四緣自分別所起名境、五緣任運堅固事境。此中若緣苦集事境所有諸漏，是緣邪分別所起事境。見取貪等見斷諸漏除疑，是緣見境。戒禁取，是緣戒禁境。緣滅道境及緣不同分界境所有諸漏，是緣自分別所起名境。何以故？非此煩惱能緣滅道，亦不能緣不同分界，非無所緣故。修所斷漏，是緣自任運堅固事境。」。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯五、內緣</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科內緣，內緣的煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">五、內緣。謂緣六處定不定地所有煩惱。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、內緣，得禪定或沒有禪定者，緣所依的眼耳鼻舌身意內六處所生起的煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯六、外緣</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科外緣，緣妙五欲所有煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">六、外緣。謂緣妙五欲所有煩惱。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　六、外緣，向外緣身體以外的微妙色聲香味觸五欲而生的煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="59p4815"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯七、現見緣</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第七科現見緣，緣現在所有煩惱，與不現見緣是一對。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">七、現見緣。謂緣現在所有煩惱。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　七、現見緣，緣現前可以看得到的，現在遇到的境界而生的煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯八、不現見緣</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第八科不現見緣，緣不現見的煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">八、不現見緣。謂緣去來所有煩惱。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　八、不現見緣，緣想到過去或想到未來，不是現前的境界而生的煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯九、自類緣</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第九科自類緣，緣自類煩惱所有煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">九、自類緣。謂緣自類煩惱所有煩惱。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　九、自類緣，緣自己那一類的煩惱所生的煩惱。欲界眾生有欲煩惱可緣欲界一切煩惱事。或如貪緣貪名自類緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯十、他類緣</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十科他類緣，緣他類所有煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">十、他類緣。謂緣異類煩惱及緣煩惱事所有煩惱。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　十、他類緣，不同種類的煩惱互緣。如欲界煩惱可緣上界一切煩惱事；然非上界煩惱可緣下界煩惱事。或如貪緣瞋及緣五蘊名他類緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》自類緣他類緣者：前說：十種煩惱，亦緣事轉、亦緣煩惱。謂十煩惱皆與自地一切煩惱展轉相緣，亦緣自地諸有漏事。下地煩惱能緣上地煩惱及事，非上地惑能緣下地煩惱及事。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/58.htm#47844:46672">陵本五十八卷五頁4713</a>）今此自類煩惱，當知謂彼自地一切煩惱。異類煩惱及緣煩惱事，當知謂彼下地煩惱能緣上地煩惱及事。如是差別應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　前文說：十種煩惱，能緣因緣所生法世俗實有的事而轉：緣色受想行識、色聲香味觸等事生起煩惱，也可以緣分別我見引起的煩惱而生煩惱。十種煩惱都與自地（如欲界）一切煩惱展轉相緣，也緣著自地境界的一切有漏事。下地欲界的人能緣色無色界的煩惱，上地色無色界的人，不會緣下地的煩惱及事，因為下地的煩惱種子在上地不現行了，不再緣慮這些麤重的煩惱和所緣境事，在〈決擇‧有尋有伺等三地〉卷58，1920頁有說到。這裏的自類煩惱，應當知道是指自地的一切煩惱，如欲界眾生能緣欲界一切煩惱事。異類煩惱及緣煩惱事，應當知道是指下地煩惱能緣上地的煩惱及事。如欲界的人能緣色無色界的煩惱，以及色無色界的果報體、色聲觸法等。這些差別應該知道。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯十一、有緣</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十一科有緣，緣後有的煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="59p4816"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">十一、有緣。謂緣後有所有煩惱。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　十一、有緣，認為會有來生的想法，緣來生而生起的煩惱。依有緣，能於後有生起常見。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯十二、無有緣</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十二科無有緣，緣無後有的煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">十二、無有緣。謂緣斷無有所有煩惱。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　十二、無有緣，是指有斷見，覺得這個生命體不好，因無有愛使令生起煩惱，希望斷除後有，使生命永遠不再現起。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯十三、自境緣</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十三科自境緣，緣自己的境界，與自地緣是相似的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">十三、自境緣。謂欲界於欲行煩惱，色界於色行煩惱，無色界於無色行煩惱。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　十三、自境緣，是指欲界眾生於欲界內外諸行生起煩惱，色界的眾生對色界內外諸行生起煩惱，無色界的眾生對於無色的受想行識生起煩惱。三界眾生對自界地諸行，產生的煩惱，名自境緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯十四、他境緣3　辰一、總標列2　巳一、上界於下界</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十四科他境緣，於自地緣他地的煩惱，分三科；第一科總標列，總相標示列舉出來，又分二科；第一科上界於下界，上界眾生對下界境緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">十四、他境緣。謂色界於欲行煩惱，無色界於色行煩惱。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　十四、他境緣，是指色界眾生對欲界內外諸行生起高慢煩惱，無色界的眾生對色界內外諸行生起煩惱，這是緣不同界地而生的高慢煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、下地於上地</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科下地於上地，下地緣上地煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又復下地於上地煩惱。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又下地的眾生可以緣上地的煩惱，如欲界的眾生緣色無色界所生的貪煩惱等。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、徵所以</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科徵所以，問為什麼這樣？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">所以者何？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為什麼？</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="59p4817"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰三、隨難釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科隨難釋，將困難的地方拿出來解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">生上地者，於彼下地諸有情所，由常、恆、樂、淨具勝功德，自謂為勝故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　生到上地的有情，對於下地的有情會生起高慢的煩惱，由於在上地具有常時、恆久、快樂、清淨的具有殊勝功德，他們不用大小便，也不用飲食，有殊勝的神通，一想到下地的污穢情況，就覺得自己很殊勝，而生起高慢的煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》生上地者等者：此釋所以。唯顯前說色界於欲行煩惱，無色界於色行煩惱，故作是說。下地於上地煩惱易可了知，故不具釋。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這段文解釋為什麼，前文說色界的眾生對於欲界的內外諸行能生高慢煩惱，無色界的眾生對色界的內外諸行能生高慢煩惱，所以這樣說。下地欲界的人可以緣著色無色界異類煩惱，容易明白，所以不多做解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯十五、無境緣</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十五科無境緣，緣沒有的境界而生的煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">十五、無境緣。謂緣分別所計滅道及廣大佛法等所有煩惱。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　十五、無境緣，是指緣沒有的境界也能生起煩惱。緣分別心所執著的滅諦、道諦，及大乘廣大不可思議的佛法等所有煩惱。滅諦就是真如，緣我空及法空的真如，一切法的實相我們只知道一個名字，自己從來沒有清淨過，沒有真實的境界，沒辦法取相，不知道那真實的境界是怎樣？道諦也是一樣，能滅煩惱的智慧到底是怎麼回事？這樣想也只是緣名為境，不知道凡所有相皆是虛妄，它的真實境界是什麼，不能曉得。這是有漏修行時是這種境界。緣廣大不可思議的佛法，不是凡夫的境界，沒辦法取相；或者大乘惡取空的人取著中觀的思想，說一切法皆無所有，撥無一切，生起斷滅空的煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》謂緣分別所計滅道等者：前說迷滅道諦所起邪見，即緣分別所計滅道煩惱。又有一類大乘惡取空者，謗一切法皆無所有，即緣廣大佛法等所有煩惱。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　前文說緣滅諦和道諦生起的種種邪見，即是緣分別所計滅諦、道諦的煩惱，前文又說緣滅諦與道諦只是緣名字，不能真實體驗滅諦和道諦。又有一類大乘惡取空的人，誹謗一切法都無所有，就是此處所說緣廣大佛法等所有煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑六、煩惱現行2　寅一、略標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科煩惱現行，說明煩惱現行，分二科；第一科略標，要略標出。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，煩惱現行有二十種。謂二十種補特伽羅，依二十緣，起二十種現行煩惱。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，煩惱的現行有二十種，指二十種人依止二十種所緣，生起二十種現行煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、隨釋3　卯一、二十補特伽羅2　辰一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科隨釋，接著解釋，分三科；第一科二十補特伽羅，二十種人，分二科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何二十補特伽羅？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　是哪二十種人？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列，列出來。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="59p4818"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、在家，二、出家，三、住惡說法，四、住善說法，五、增上煩惱行，六、等分行，七、薄塵行，八、世間離欲，九、未離欲，十、見聖跡，十一、未見聖跡，十二、執著，十三、不執著，十四、觀察，十五、睡眠，十六、覺悟，十七、幼少，十八、根成熟，十九、般涅槃法，二十、不般涅槃法。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、在家人。二、出家人。三、住惡說法，就是外道。四、住善說法，修學佛法的人。五、增上煩惱行，如貪增上，貪心特別強，或瞋增上，瞋心特別強等某類煩惱特別強的人。六、等分行，貪瞋癡等每一種煩惱都差不多的人。七、薄塵行，貪瞋癡都很微薄的人。八、世間離欲，修得世間禪定的人。九、未離欲，沒有證得禪定，沒有遠離色聲香味觸欲的欲界有情。十、見聖跡，見道位的聖人。十一、未見聖跡，還沒有見到聖道的人。十二、執著，有執著心，不如理分別的人。或由於不信三寶四諦的緣故，分別所起煩惱現行。十三、不執著，不執著的人還是會有俱生任運所起的煩惱現行。十四、觀察，有尋伺欲的人。十五、睡眠，睡覺的人，睡覺的時候也會有煩惱。十六、覺悟，醒著的人。十七、幼少，年紀小的人，從兒童到少年，十五、六歲的是幼少。十八、根成熟，六根成熟，有的地方說十五、六歲以上的人，有的地方說二十歲才成熟。十九、般涅槃法，就是有三乘無漏種性的人。二十、不般涅槃法，沒有三乘無漏種性的人。將人分成這二十類。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》執著不執著等者：不如理分別，是名執著。任運無分別，名不執著。有尋伺欲，是名觀察。身心惛昧，令不自在，是名睡眠。與此相違，得自在轉，是名覺悟。此中二十補特伽羅，起二十種現行煩惱，一一次第配釋應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這裏特別解釋，不如佛法的真理來分別種種的境界稱為執著。由分別心執著，執我、我所，執一切是真實的，而生起種種的貪瞋癡，稱為執著。任運生起的沒有分別的煩惱，稱為不執著。有尋伺欲，稱為觀察。睡眠的時候，身心惛沈，使身心不自在稱為睡眠。醒過來了，身心能自在，稱為覺悟。這二十種人會生起二十種煩惱現行，一個一個配著二十緣生起煩惱的現行，先說明人，接下來說明二十種煩惱現行，是配合起來說的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、二十煩惱現行2　辰一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科二十煩惱現行，說明二十種煩惱現行，分二科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何二十煩惱現行？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼稱為二十種煩惱的現行？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列，列出二十種煩惱現行。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="59p4819"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、隨所欲纏現行，二、不隨所欲纏現行，三、無所了知煩惱現行，四、有所了知煩惱現行，五、麤煩惱現行，六、等煩惱現行，七、微煩惱現行，八、內門煩惱現行，九、外門煩惱現行，十、失念煩惱現行，十一、猛利煩惱現行，十二、分別所起煩惱現行，十三、任運所起煩惱現行，十四、尋思煩惱現行，十五、不自在煩惱現行，十六、自在煩惱現行，十七、非所依位煩惱現行，十八、所依位煩惱現行，十九、可救療煩惱現行，二十、不可救療煩惱現行。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二十種煩惱現行是：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、隨所欲纏現行，是指在家人愛著受用諸欲的快樂，隨所愛樂的色聲香味觸諸欲，使煩惱現行。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、不隨所欲纏現行，出家人受持淨戒，精勤修行斷除煩惱，必須克治自己的欲望，未成功前仍有不隨所欲的煩惱纏現行。例如雖然斷除事欲，仍有欲尋思的煩惱欲存在。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、無所了知煩惱現行，住惡說法者，不了解諸法實相的道理，勤修苦行，不依在家愛著五欲樂，以不苦不樂的戒禁為緣而有煩惱現行。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、有所了知煩惱現行，修學佛法的人，明明知道不應愛著諸欲，仍於五欲生起煩惱現行，他是有所了知的，明知故犯。知道可是做不到，因為知道與做到還有很大的一段距離。譬如知道聖人的境界，可是做不到，還不是聖人。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、麤煩惱現行，是增上煩惱行的那一類人。這類人的煩惱很強、很麤，一看就知道他貪心比較重，瞋心比較重，還是愚癡心比較重。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　六、等煩惱現行，等分行的人會有等煩惱現行，各種煩惱差不多，不是貪就是瞋，不然就是癡，差不多什麼煩惱都有的。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　七、微煩惱現行，是薄塵行的人，貪瞋癡都很薄，任何時刻煩惱都很輕微，遇勝上可愛等境，能不起猛利相續貪恚癡纏；於下品中品境，易離易厭，於修善法，加行速疾。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　八、內門煩惱現行，由於內身的眼耳鼻舌身意生起煩惱，這是屬於世間離欲的人，多數是內緣的，不緣外面的欲，是緣內身生起的煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　九、外門煩惱現行，是沒有離欲的人，沒有離色聲香味觸的欲，心常常往外攀緣。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　十、失念煩惱現行，是指見聖跡的人，聖人也會有失去正念的時候，一剎那失去正念，也會有煩惱現行。《俱舍論》有說聖人的智慧像熱的鍋子，煩惱像熱鍋上的水，智慧很快就將煩惱的水蒸乾了，但是他也有失念的煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　十一、猛利煩惱現行，是指沒有見聖道的凡夫，有很強烈的煩惱現行。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　十二、分別所起煩惱現行，是有執著心的人，容易生起分別心所起的煩惱現行，分別心特別強，很執著。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　十三、任運所起煩惱現行，不執著的人還是會有俱生任運所起的煩惱現行，過去生一直延續下來的，沒有特別分別，任運的煩惱就現行了。或不執著人，懈怠緣故，任運煩惱而起現行。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　十四、尋伺煩惱現行，觀察有麤的觀察、細的觀察，常常觀察諸欲，會有尋伺的煩惱現行。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　十五、不自在煩惱現行，睡眠中的人有不自在的煩惱現行，不想讓它出現，可是貪瞋癡的境界就出現了，夢到不該作的夢。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　十六、自在煩惱現行，醒著的時候，生起貪心、瞋心或癡心，名自在煩惱現行。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　十七、非所依位煩惱現行，煩惱不會依止在這個時候生起的，可是它還是生起了，這是幼少，兒童，小孩子也會有煩惱。本來小孩子應該是快樂的，可是他還是生起煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　十八、所依位煩惱現行，就是六根成熟，已經變成大人、就有根成熟的煩惱生起。六根成熟是煩惱現行的所依。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　十九、可救療煩惱現行，有三乘無漏種性的人，煩惱是可以救治、醫療的。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二十、不可救療煩惱現行，沒有三乘無漏種性的人，怎麼樣救也不能救了。怎麼勸都沒有用，就是一直造惡業，這是依教化眾生的經驗方便說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯三、二十煩惱現行緣3　辰一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科二十煩惱現行緣，二十煩惱現行所緣，分三科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何二十煩惱現行緣？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼是二十種煩惱現行生起的所緣？有所緣境才會生起煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列，列舉出來。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、樂緣，二、苦緣，三、不苦不樂緣，四、欲緣，五、尋思緣，六、觸緣，</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、樂緣，在家人緣著五欲快樂的境界，隨所歡喜於追求時，就會有煩惱現行。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、苦緣，出家人精勤辛苦修行斷除煩惱，未證得禪定前，仍有精勤所生苦受，有不隨所欲的煩惱現行，沒有想要這種煩惱，可是煩惱還是會出現。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、不苦不樂緣，外道不依佛法勤苦行，不依在家所著五欲樂，以不苦不樂的戒禁緣故，有無所了知的煩惱現行。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、欲緣，是住善說法的人依著諸欲為緣，生起有所了知的煩惱現行。雖然知道佛法的道理，由於修行不夠，依諸欲還是生起煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、尋伺緣，增上煩惱行的人依尋伺諸欲為緣，內心想著種種世間的事情，生起麤的煩惱。尋伺也可通於尋思，包括欲、恚、害尋思、國土尋思、親里尋思、不死尋思、輕蔑相應尋思、家勢相應尋思。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　六、觸緣，等分行的人六根接觸六境，會生起等分的煩惱現行。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》欲緣尋思緣觸緣者：不善法欲，是名欲緣。八種尋思，名尋思緣。內六觸處，是名觸緣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　不是善法的欲，稱為欲緣。八種尋思，稱為尋思緣。內六根的觸處，稱為觸緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="59p4820"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">七、隨眠緣，八、宿習緣，九、親近惡友緣，十、聞不正法緣，十一、不正作意緣，十二、不信緣，十三、懈怠緣，十四、失念緣，十五、散亂緣，十六、惡慧緣，十七、放逸緣，十八、煩惱緣，十九、未離欲緣，二十、異生性緣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　七、隨眠緣，薄塵行的人貪瞋癡很薄，因為有煩惱的種子，以此為緣，使令他產生微細的煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　八、宿習緣，已經修世間離欲，得了禪定，由過去生的習氣延續下來的宿習而有內門的煩惱現行。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　九、親近惡友緣，未離欲的人因為親近不善知識，在色聲香味觸外門上生起煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　十、聞不正法緣，見聖跡的人聽到外道的不正法，心裏生起譏嫌，覺得他們根本就錯了。明明知道苦集滅道四聖諦是這樣，可是他們偏偏不這樣說，一生起譏嫌的心就是煩惱了。</span></span></span></div>
