<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　十一、不正作意緣，未見聖跡的人不如理作意，依止不正作意緣猛利的煩惱現行，因為想錯了，就出現很強烈的煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　十二、不信緣，執著的人由於不相信佛法的緣故，由分別生起煩惱，執著種種的境界。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　十三、懈怠緣，不執著的人，心裏雖然沒有分別起的煩惱，可是因為懈怠，沒有好好的修行，還會生起任運所起的煩惱現行。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　十四、失念緣，有欲的人，觀察欲時，失去正念，會有尋思煩惱現行。如果是觀察離欲、修初禪的人，偶而失去正念，一下子又緣到欲了，又有尋思煩惱現行。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　十五、散亂緣，是睡眠的時候，因為心裏散亂，不能控制，有不自在的煩惱現行。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　十六、惡慧緣，醒著的時候，因為有惡的智慧，錯誤的分別心，想貪就貪，想瞋就瞋，因此有自在的煩惱現行。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　十七、放逸緣，是幼少的人放逸、遊戲過頭了，就有非所依位的煩惱現行。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　十八、煩惱緣，根成熟的人，依根所需會有所依位的煩惱現行。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　十九、未離欲緣，具備三乘種性的人因為沒有離欲，有可救療煩惱現行。沒有得定，欲、恚、害都可能生起，會有很多的煩惱現行。因為有善根，這種煩惱是可以救療的，只要勤修止觀還是可以離欲的。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二十、異生性緣，沒有三乘種性的凡夫，有種種不同的想法，會產生不可救療的煩惱現行。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰三、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科結，結語。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">依此諸緣故，煩惱現行。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　依止這幾種緣，使令煩惱現行。以上是二十種補特伽羅依止二十種緣，生起二十種煩惱現行，配對而說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑七、煩惱結生相續2　寅一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第七科煩惱結生相續，煩惱結使令凡夫與下一生苦的果報身連接在一起，分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：於彼彼界結生相續彼彼身中，當言全界一切煩惱皆結生耶？為不全耶？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：有情在三界中受生相續得到不同新的生命體中，應說三界中的一切煩惱都在相續的新生命體中嗎？或是煩惱未全部相續在新的生命體中嗎？生命體是承受眾苦的器，煩惱與苦器和合稱為結，煩惱與新相續的生命苦器和合稱為結生相續。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　再詳細說，若生在欲界，是欲界的一切煩惱使令生命體生起；若生在色界，是色界的一切煩惱使令生命體生起；若生在無色界，是無色界的一切煩惱使令生命體生起。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》於彼彼界結生相續等者：此中問意，謂若生此界地，即此界地一切煩惱令生相續，為不爾耶？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這裏的問題意思是說，如果生在欲界，是不是屬於欲界的一切煩惱使令生命體相續？還是不是？是不是生到哪一界，就有哪一界的煩惱？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、答2　卯一、釋道理2　辰一、略標簡</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科釋道理，解釋道理，又分二科；第一科略標簡，要略標示簡別出來。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：當言全，非不全。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：在哪一界受生，就是那一界全分的煩惱使令去結生的，並不是沒有全部的煩惱能去那裏受生。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、釋所以3　巳一、約自生處辨</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋所以，解釋為什麼，分三科；第一科約自生處辨，約自己要去投生的地方來說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">何以故？若未離欲，於自生處方得受生，非離欲故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為什麼？這個人如果沒有離欲，有欲的煩惱種子，自己會到欲界處受生。已經離欲的人，就不會再到欲界受生。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》於自生處方得受生等者：此顯異生，纏及隨眠結生相續應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這裏顯示凡夫的煩惱現行和煩惱種子的作用，使令有情結生相續的道理應該要了解。在〈本地分‧有尋有伺等三地〉卷9～卷10的生雜染中說到凡夫由無明緣行，造業熏習識、名色、六入、觸、受五法種子，由愛煩惱的現行產生欲取等諸取，滋潤業與識等五法種子形成有支的力量，導致煩惱與新相續的生命苦器和合而結生相續。這是《披尋記》所要提示凡夫的煩惱現行、煩惱隨眠、結生相續之間的重點。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="59p4821"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、約麤重隨縛辨</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科約麤重隨縛辨，約煩惱種子隨縛說明結生相續。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又未離欲者，諸煩惱品所有麤重隨縛自身，亦能為彼異身生因。由是因緣，當知一切煩惱皆結生相續。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又已見到聖道，尚未離欲的人，欲界所有煩惱品的種子隨逐繫縛著自身，由將死位中俱生起的自體愛現行，滋潤欲界業牽引中有生起，也能成為其下一生不同的生命體生起的因緣。由此因緣，可知欲界的一切煩惱都能使令欲界有情結生相續。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》諸煩惱品所有麤重等者：此顯已見聖跡，唯隨眠結生相續應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這一段話的意思是說，已經見到聖道的人，為什麼還來這裏受生？因為他還有欲界煩惱的種子，使令他還在欲界人天受生。這裡強調未究竟離欲的聖人由俱生煩惱種子的隨縛也能成為受生的生因。因為初果、二果聖人還沒有完全斷除欲界的煩惱，使得有任運起的俱生煩惱導致他去結生相續，由於欲界有情有俱生的饑渴，需要段食，但是他是不挑食物的；聖人還有果報的力量促使他要去攝食而必須要去受生；凡夫有煩惱現行跟煩惱種子去受生，是為喜貪而食。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　聖人去受生時，初果、二果都是正知入胎，去受生是知道的、不是有煩惱的現行去的，因為果報種子任運的力量讓他不得不去，但能知道這是我的父親、這是我的母親，不像凡夫是以顛倒想入的，但是初果、二果住跟出就不知道。經典上說，有的初果聖人出胎以後，也忘了自己是初果聖人，必須有善緣才會再引發，是較特別的地方。這是說到聖人俱生煩惱來受生的情況。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳三、約將受生時辨2　午一、辨現行3　未一、貪愛等</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科約將受生時辨，再詳細說明將要投胎時結生相續的情況，分二科；第一科辨現行，說明煩惱的現行，分三科；第一科貪愛等，說明貪愛及其它煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又將受生時，於自體上貪愛現行，於男於女若愛若恚亦互現行。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又將受生的時候，對於自己的身體會有自體愛現行；如果未來的自身是女性，會對父親生愛著，對母親生瞋恚；如果未來的自身是男性，會對母親生愛著，對父親生瞋恚，所以受生時，貪愛、瞋恚都現行。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、疑</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科疑，將受生時有疑現行。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又疑現行。彼作是思：此男此女，今為與我共行事不？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又會有懷疑心現行。受生者這樣想：這個男的，這個女的，現在是和我在做這件事嗎？&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未三、薩迦耶見等</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科薩迦耶見等，將受生時還會生起種種的我見。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又於內外我我所見及我慢等皆亦現行。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又投生的時候，對於內身、外境有種種的我見、我所見、及高慢心等，屬於欲界的煩惱也都會現行。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、結相續</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科結相續，煩惱與新生命苦器結合相續。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由此因緣，當知一切煩惱皆得結生相續。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由此因緣，應當知道所有的煩惱都會隨逐而結生相續，都是集諦。經典常常只說愛是集諦，那是簡說的，在投生的時候，還有其他同一界地的煩惱相續。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、辨種類2　辰一、標差別2　巳一、初七種</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科辨種類，分辨結生相續的種類，分二科；第一科標差別，標出差別，又分二科；第一科初七種，說明最初七種煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="59p4822"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，結生相續略有七種。一、纏及隨眠結生相續，謂諸異生。二、唯隨眠結生相續，謂見聖跡。三、正知入胎結生相續，謂轉輪王。四、正知入住結生相續，謂諸獨覺。五、於一切位不失正念結生相續，謂諸菩薩。六、業所引發結生相續，謂除菩薩結生相續。七、智所引發結生相續，謂諸菩薩。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，要略而言有七種結生相續。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、纏及隨眠結生相續，指凡夫由煩惱的現行與煩惱的種子，去投生取得另一個生命體。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、唯隨眠結生相續，指見到聖道的聖者，只由煩惱種子結生相續。例如初果聖人，分別起的煩惱已斷除，可是俱生起的我見等煩惱種子還沒有完全斷除，因此還要再來欲界受生。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、正知入胎結生相續。在投生時，能夠正知入胎，這是轉輪聖王。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《大毗婆沙論》說：正知入胎，是指受生者知道這是我的父親，這是我的母親。如果去投胎只知道這是男的，這是女的，那是不正知了，不知道那是誰？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、正知入住結生相續，是指這一生將要證得獨覺辟支佛的人。入胎、住胎時，他都知道。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、於一切位不失正念結生相續，是指隨願而受生，最少是初地以上的諸菩薩。於一切位，就是入胎、住胎、出胎，完全明明白白，沒有失去正念。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　六、業所引發結生相續，是指除了聖者菩薩以外，都是由業力所引發生命體的相續。前四種都是由業力所引發而得。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　七、智所引發結生相續，是指諸聖者菩薩，由智慧使令他得到生命體。因為菩薩是隨願而受生。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、後二種</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科後二種，另外二種結生相續。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又有引無義利結生相續，謂即業所引發結生相續。又有能引義利結生相續，謂智所引發結生相續。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又凡夫由於業力所引發的結生相續，是沒有義利的，使令自身苦受不斷，生起種種的苦。聖者菩薩是由智慧，隨願受生，是能引義利結生相續，能夠自利利他，為度眾生、住持佛法、才來受生。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、結總說</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科結總說，結論總說結生相續。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是總說結生相續，或七、或九。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如是總說有結生相續，或七種、或九種。如前面說的：由纏及隨眠結生相續，乃至智所引發結生相續，有七種；或九種，是指七種及後二種：引無義利結生相續，及能引義利的結生相續，合說九種。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子二、指決擇</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科指決擇，指出決斷簡擇的文。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，於此處所，有餘一切順前句、順後句及四句等如理決擇文，更不復現。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，在煩惱雜染的處所，所餘一切隨順前句的答案而回答，以狹問寬的順前句；或是隨順後句的答案而回答，以寬問狹的順後句，以及四句等如諸法的真理，決斷簡擇的文章，不會再出現了。決斷簡擇關於煩惱雜染的決擇，就說到這裏，已經說得很廣了。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》於此處所等者：謂於煩惱雜染如理決擇，有順前句、順後句、四句、無事句種種差別，此不更說。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　於煩惱雜染的如理決擇，如同諸法的真理而決斷簡擇，有隨順於前句、隨順於後句、或者以四句、或者以無事句來說明。有種種的差別，這裏不再重說。表示還有很多可以說，但是就說到這裏為止。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="59p4823"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸二、嗢柁南結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科嗢柁南結，以四句偈頌彙集結說煩惱雜染的差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">後嗢柁南曰：</span></strong></span></span><br />
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　業相事樂等　不善等及斷　所緣與現行　續生最為後</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　最後將煩惱雜染的種種差別彙集以偈頌而說：業相事樂等：業指由猛力及分別令煩惱發業；相指煩惱的自相、共相、差別相；事是指有事無事的煩惱；樂等是指任運生及不任運生的十種煩惱與五受根相應等情形。不善等及斷：不善等指三界煩惱聚；斷指以七種問答說明煩惱斷。所緣與現行：所緣指煩惱十五種所緣；現行指二十種有情，依止二十種緣，生起二十種煩惱現行。續生最為後：是指最後說的七或九種煩惱結生相續。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">庚二、業雜染2　辛一、結前生後</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科業雜染，決擇業雜染，分二科；第一科結前生後，結束前文生起後文。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是已說煩惱雜染決擇。業雜染決擇，我今當說。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如是已經說過煩惱雜染的決斷簡擇。業雜染的決斷簡擇，現在我（論主）應該說一說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辛二、辨釋差別2　壬一、長行釋2　癸一、諸門決擇7　子一、自性相2　丑一、略標簡3　寅一、標五相別</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科辨釋差別，分別及解釋業雜染的種種差別，分二科；第一科長行釋，以長的文來解釋，又分二科；第一科諸門決擇，用七門來解釋決擇，又分七科；第一科自性相，決擇業雜染的自性相，又分二科；第一科略標簡，要略標示簡別出來，又分三科；第一科標五相別，標出業雜染的五相差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如先所說業雜染義，當知此業亦由五相建立差別。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如前面〈本地分‧有尋有伺等三地〉卷8、9說到業雜染的義理，應當知道業也由五種相貌建立差別。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　此處主要說明業道。業是指思心所的造作。據丁福保編的《佛學大辭典》說：「善惡之所作，使人向於六趣，故名為道。」；勝鬘經寶窟上末曰：「造作稱業，通人向於三途，名之為道。」《大智度論》九十二曰：「小者不名業道，以其能趣惡處故為道。」業以思之心所為體，十善十惡，共為業（即思遊履之所），故名為道。即業之道也。由此可知業道的意義。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、舉所攝業</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科舉所攝業，舉出五相所攝的業。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂根本業道所攝身語意業，及彼方便、後起所攝諸業。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　業的五相差別，是指十不善業及十善業的根本業道所攝的身業、語業、意業，及彼方便，造業的行動，實際去造業，動身發語或內心發動意業；後起，是指造業究竟時所攝的種種業。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="59p4824"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》亦由五相建立差別等者：前說煩惱由五種相建立差別，此業雜染亦復如是。云何為五？謂根本業道所攝身語意業為三，方便、後起所攝諸業為二。三依自相，二依差別，如是總說，是故成五。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　前文說煩惱雜染由五種相建立差別：自性、自性差別、染淨差別、迷斷差別、對治差別；業雜染也是由五種相建立差別。什麼是五種相？是指十不善業即時善業所攝的身語意業，方便加行，及究竟的後起，這就是業的五相。前三種是依止發業的自相而說，業的自相是身業或者語業或者意業，後二的方便、後起是依業的差別而說，這樣總說有五相建立業雜染差別。後起，是指業的究竟或不究竟的情況。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　〈本地分‧有尋有伺等三地〉卷8說：「業自性云何？謂若法生時，造作相起，及由彼生故，身行語行於彼後時造作而轉，是名業自性。」</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅三、別釋其相2　卯一、舉略說2　辰一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科別釋其相，各別解釋它的相貌，分二科；第一科舉略說，要略說不善業道，又分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如先所說不善業道，名根本業道所攝不善身語意業。云何建立彼殺生等不善業道自相？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如前所說十不善業，稱為根本業道所攝的不善身語意業。如何建立殺生、偷盜、邪淫等不善業道的自相？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、答2　巳一、總標2　午一、出五相</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科總標，總相標出，又分二科；第一科出五相，將五相標示出來。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂染汙心起彼欲樂，即於是處彼業現行而得究竟，當知總名殺生等一切業道自相。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　殺生業道的五相：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、染汙心，有貪瞋癡等染汙心；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、起彼欲樂，生起想殺等造業的意願；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、即於是處，造業的對象，如想要殺人或畜生等；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、彼業現行，開始造業，動身發語了，這是方便；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、而得究竟，完成造業，這是後起。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這是殺生業道的圓滿自相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》謂染汙心等者：此中建立業道自相總有五支，一、染汙心，二、起欲樂，三、於是處，四、業現行，五、得究竟。如下釋義，易可了知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　此處建立業道自相，總共要有五相究竟圓滿，缺一不可。包括：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、染汙心，不善的煩惱；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、起欲樂，想要造業的意願；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、於是處，就是所緣境，想要造業的對象；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、業現行，開始動身發語了，開始策動身手，去做這件事；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、得究竟，造業成功了。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　下面還會詳細解釋它的道理，很容易明白。業道，是指不善業會成為通到三惡趣的道路。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、隨難釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科隨難釋，隨著解釋較困難的地方。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">染汙心者，謂貪者貪所蔽，瞋者瞋所蔽，癡者癡所蔽。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　染汙心方面，貪煩惱，瞋煩惱，癡煩惱能染汙有情的心，稱為染汙心。貪心的人，為貪煩惱所遮蔽，使令他去偷盜等；瞋心的人，為瞋煩惱所遮蔽，使令他去殺生等；愚癡的人，為癡煩惱所遮蔽，使令他不明白因果等道理而生起邪見。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《瑜伽論記》卷17解釋：一染污心方面，是簡別菩薩悲心行殺。如〈本地分‧菩薩地〉卷41說：菩薩見劫盜賊，為貪財故，欲殺多生，或復欲害大德聲聞、獨覺、菩薩，或復欲造多無間業。見是事已，發心思惟：我若斷彼惡眾生命，墮那落迦，如其不斷，無間業成，當受大苦；我寧殺彼墮那落迦，終不令其受無間苦。如是菩薩意樂思惟，於彼眾生或以善心、或無記心，知此事已，為當來故深生慚愧，以憐愍心而斷彼命。由是因緣，於菩薩戒無所違犯，生多功德。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="59p4825"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、別辨2　午一、簡非4　未一、闕無欲樂</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科別辨，各別說明，分二科；第一科簡非，簡別不是圓滿的殺生業道，又分四科；第一科闕無欲樂，如果沒有造惡的意願，這件事不能成為業道。五支如果不俱，不能成為殺生業道。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">設有染汙心，不起彼欲樂，雖於是處彼業現行而得究竟，然此惡業非是圓滿業道所攝。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、有假設有貪瞋癡染汙的心行；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、可是並沒有造業的欲樂；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、雖然於造業的對象，沒有顛倒心；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、也去造業，而且造業成功，因為缺少造業的欲樂，這種惡業也不是圓滿業道所攝。以殺生為例，假設有瞋心，但不想殺害對方，雖然去殺害這位有情，被殺的有情也死了，這件事不算是圓滿業道所攝。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　因為他並沒有想要殺害對方的欲樂，可能是被人指使去殺的，或是被逼迫的，或者生在這種家庭，只好去殺了。以殺生為例，其餘業道也是一樣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、闕於是處</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科闕於是處，所傷害的對象不對。所殺的不是想殺的對象。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">設有染汙心及起彼欲樂，而顛倒心，設於餘事彼業現行而得究竟，此業亦非圓滿業道所攝。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、假設有貪瞋癡染汙的心行；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、也有造業的動機；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、但因顛倒心錯認對象；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、在其他對象上造業；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、而且造業成功，由於生起顛倒心取相錯誤，這種惡業也不是圓滿業道所攝。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以殺生為例，假設有瞋心，也有殺害對方的意樂，但因顛倒心而誤殺了，本來想殺甲，誤認乙就是甲，殺錯對象，雖然做了殺生這件事情，而且對方也死了，這種殺生業也不算是圓滿的業道所攝，因為不是具足五相，不能成為圓滿業道。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這段文相當於〈有尋有伺等三地〉卷9所說業顛倒中的作用顛倒：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　業顛倒云何？ 此有三種應知：一、作用顛倒，二、執受顛倒，三、喜樂顛倒。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　作用顛倒者，謂如有一，於餘眾生思欲殺害，誤害餘者。當知此中，雖有殺生，無殺生罪；然有殺生種類、殺生相似同分罪生。 若不誤殺其餘眾生，然於非情加刀杖已，謂我殺生。當知此中，無有殺生，無殺生罪；然有殺生種類、殺生相似同分罪生。如殺生業道，如是不與取等一切業道，隨其所應，作用顛倒應知。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》而顛倒心設於餘事等者：謂於彼非彼想，及非於彼彼想，名顛倒心。事，謂一一業道各別決定所依處事，或有情數、或非有情數。於非決定所依處事，由顛倒心而有所作，此事名餘。謂如誤殺其餘眾生，或於非情加刀杖已，謂我殺生。如是等類，皆名餘事。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　於造業的對象甲，錯認為不是甲；對於不是對象甲，是乙，當作對象甲，稱為顛倒心。事，是指十不善業道的每一種業道中所造業的對象，可能是有情或者不屬於有情類。不是屬於原來要造業的對象，由於顛倒心錯認而造業，被錯認的對象，稱為餘。例如誤殺其他有情，或於無情物加以刀杖砍殺，自認為：我殺生了。如同這一類，都稱為餘事。殺錯對象，稱為闕於是處。因為不是具足五相，不能成為圓滿業道。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未三、闕業現行</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科闕業現行，有染汙心起欲樂，可是業不現行。沒有殺對方但對方死掉了，這件事情也沒有究竟。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">設有染汙心及起彼欲樂，即於是處業不現行而得究竟，此業亦非圓滿業道所攝。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、假設有貪瞋癡染汙的心行；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、也有造業的動機；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、於造業的對象，沒有顛倒心；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、可是自己沒有造業，但希望造的業完成了，因為闕少業的現行，這種惡業也不是圓滿業道所攝。以殺生為例，假設有瞋心，而且想殺對方，於所殺的對象沒有顛倒心，也沒有動手去殺，可是對方死了。這個業，也不能算是圓滿的殺業。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《瑜伽論記》舉出一個例子，某乙發心想要殺害某甲，某甲聽到要被殺了，自己就生恐怖心而死掉。乙還沒動手殺甲，甲就嚇死了，雖業不行而得究竟。還有一種，怕自己被殺，就自殺了。一個是害怕死的，一個是自殺死的，這也不是圓滿業道，也屬於闕業現行的非圓滿業道所攝。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未四、闕得究竟</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科闕得究竟，前面四個條件都具足，可是對方沒有死掉，造業沒有完全成功。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">設有染汙心及起彼欲樂，即於是處彼業現行而不究竟，此業亦非圓滿業道所攝。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、假設有貪瞋癡染汙的心行；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、也有造業的動機；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、於造業的對象，沒有顛倒心；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、也去造業；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、但造的業沒有完全成功，因為闕得究竟，這種惡業也不是圓滿業道所攝。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以殺生為例，假設有瞋心，而且生起要殺對方的欲樂，也動手去殺對方，殺了以後，就逃離現場，以為對方死了，結果受害者很幸運，被他人救起來，沒有死。這種殺業也不是圓滿業道所攝。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以上說圓滿業道的五種差別相，如果缺其中一種，都不能稱為圓滿業道所攝。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="59p4826"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、顯正</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科顯正，顯示正確的五相圓滿。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若有染汙心及起彼欲樂，即於是處彼業現行而得究竟，具一切支，此業乃名圓滿業道所攝。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、假設有貪瞋癡染汙的心行；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、也有造業的動機；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、於造業的對象，沒有顛倒心；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、也去造業；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、而且造業成功。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　具足這五相的業，稱為圓滿業道所攝。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、例一切</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例一切，例十種業都一樣需要具足五相才圓滿各業自相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由此略說業道自相，一切不善業道自相應隨決了。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由此要略說明業道的自相，一切不善業道的自相需要具足五相，隨其所相應才能圓滿各業自相。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以殺生為例，要具足五相才是圓滿殺生業道，其他九種不善業道的自相也是一樣，都是要具足五相，才能說是偷盜、邪淫、妄語、綺語、惡口、兩舌、貪、瞋、癡的各業自相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》由此略說業道自相等者：前此五支，通說不善業道自相，故名為略。隨此建立，應更決了不善業道各別自相，此有十種，故說一切。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　前面所說的五支，染汙心、起欲樂、於是處、業現行、得究竟，可以通說不善業道的自相，所以稱為略。隨這五支的建立，廣說應該更可以決定十不善業道各別的自相，不善業道有十種，所以說一切。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑二、廣差別3　寅一、辨五相4　卯一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科廣差別，詳細說明十惡業道的差別，分三科；第一科辨五相，提出五種相貌來說，又分四科；第一科標，標出五相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="32808:47958"></a><a name="616:47958"></a>復次，若廣建立十惡業道自性差別，復由五相。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，若詳細建立十惡業道的自性差別，又另外有五種相貌。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">何等為五？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　是哪五種相貌，才是十惡業道的自性？</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="59p4827"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯三、列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科列，列出來。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、事，二、想，三、欲樂，四、煩惱，五、方便究竟。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　十惡業道的自性差別五種相貌</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、事，指造業的對象；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、想，於所緣（造業的對象）沒有顛倒想；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、欲樂，想要造業的希望心（動機）；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、煩惱，有貪瞋癡的煩惱，就是染汙心；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、方便究竟，將業現行和得究竟歸納成一個。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這裏加上想說成五相，由這五種相貌可以建立十惡業道的自性差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯四、釋5　辰一、由事別</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科釋，解釋，分五科；第一科由事別，由造業的對象有差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="68821:47966"></a>事者，一一業道各別決定所依處事。或有情數、或非有情數，隨其所應，十惡業道依之而轉。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　事方面，是指一個一個的業道各別決定有所依處事，如內六處、外六處、或因緣所生法的種種事；或是屬於有情、或者屬於無情，隨其所相應的，十惡業道依止不同對象而生起造作。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》隨其所應者：如下一一分別其事應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　下面還會一個一個的解釋，十惡業道的對象。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、由想別</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科由想別，想的差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">想者，有四。謂於彼非彼想，非於彼彼想，於彼彼想，非於彼非彼想。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　想方面，於所造業的對象有沒有認錯，取相有沒有錯誤，有四種情況，如以甲代表所要造業的對象。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第一種於彼非彼想，於甲想成不是甲，這是顛倒想；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二種非於彼彼想，不是甲想成是甲，這也是顛倒想；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三種於彼彼想，是甲也想成是甲，想對了，這是沒有顛倒想；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四種非於彼非彼想，不是甲也不作甲想，如想殺某甲，也知道現前的人不是某甲，這也是沒有顛倒想。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》於彼非彼想等者：謂如殺生業道，依有情數眾生為事。若於彼眾生所不作彼眾生想，是名於彼非彼想；或於非眾生所作眾生想，名非於彼彼想。如是二想皆顛倒攝。如說殺生，如是所餘業道，隨應準釋。於彼彼想，非於彼非彼想，當知此二無顛倒攝。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　殺生業道，通常以有情為對象。若於那一類甲眾生，不做甲眾生想，稱為於彼非彼想。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果不是所要殺的眾生可是當做眾生想，稱為非於彼彼想，譬如遠遠看到一棵樹，不是所要殺的甲有情，當做是甲有情，將他殺了，稱為非於彼彼想。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這二種想都是有錯誤的。殺生是這樣，其他業道也是一樣。是甲當甲想，不是甲也認為不是甲，這二種是沒有無顛倒，沒有錯誤的想。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰三、由欲樂別</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三由欲樂別，由欲樂的差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">欲樂者，或有倒想、或無倒想樂所作欲。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　欲樂方面，是指造業的動機，或者顛倒想，錯認對象，或者無顛倒想，沒有認錯對象，都有想要造業的動機。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="59p4828"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰四、由煩惱別</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科由煩惱別，造業時的煩惱差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">煩惱者，或貪、或瞋、或癡、或貪瞋、或貪癡、或瞋癡，或貪瞋癡一切皆具。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　煩惱方面，是指或貪、或瞋、或癡，三種煩惱單獨生起；或貪瞋、或貪癡、或瞋癡，二種煩惱同時生起、或前後生起，乃至貪瞋癡，三種煩惱同時生起、或前後生起；這七種煩惱的心，使令有情想造作十惡業道。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》或貪或瞋等者：如下自廣分別應知。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/60.htm#47976:48357">陵本六十卷六頁4863</a>）</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在〈決擇‧有尋有伺等三地〉卷60，1975頁還會詳細說明，什麼樣的情況生起什麼樣的煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰五、由方便究竟別</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科由方便究竟別，實際行動後有圓滿與不圓滿的差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">方便究竟者，即於所欲作業隨起方便，或於爾時、或於後時而得究竟。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　方便究竟方面，是指隨著所想造的業就動身發語造作，或在這時馬上究竟，譬如現在殺，現在死，或在後時得到究竟，譬如現在殺，到次日才死。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》方便究竟者：彼業現行，是名方便。希望滿足，是名究竟。此即前五支中後二應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　要造的業也實際去行動，稱為方便。造業的欲樂達到或滿足了，稱為究竟。譬如說離間語，希望他們分開，結果他們真地分開了，稱為希望滿足，是名究竟。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這是前面五支當中的後二支，彼業現行與究竟。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、釋十業2　卯一、標隨應</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋十業，解釋十種業的差別，分二科；第一科標隨應，標示出所應該具足的條件。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由此五相，於殺生乃至邪見諸業道中，隨其所應，當廣建立圓滿自性十種差別。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由這五相，於殺生乃至邪見諸業道中，隨所相應所造的業，應當詳細建立圓滿十種不善業道的自性差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、辨差別10　辰一、殺生業道5　巳一、依有情事</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科辨差別，說明十不善業道的差別，又分十科；第一科殺生業道，說明殺生業道，分五科；第一科依有情事，以有情數眾生為事的殺生業道。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">殺生業道，以有情數眾生為事。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　殺生業道，是以有情的眾生為對象。事，是指對象。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="59p4829"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、於彼彼想</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科於彼彼想，於甲作甲想，沒有顛倒想。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若能害者，於眾生所作眾生想，起害生欲，此想即名於彼眾生名不顛倒想。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　圓滿業道的第二個條件：能殺害的人、於眾生作眾生想，比方能害生者想殺甲，也確認對方是甲，生起想要殺害對方的欲望，這種想沒有錯，稱為不顛倒想。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳三、依無倒想樂所作欲</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科依無倒想樂所作欲，於對象沒有想錯時，有想殺害對方的意樂。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">依此想故，作如是心：我當害生。如是名為殺生欲樂。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　能害生者依止殺害對方的想，在取相時，看到所要殺害的對象，沒有看錯，沒有顛倒想，生起殺害的心念：我應該將他殺掉。這種心情稱為殺生欲樂。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳四、煩惱不具或具</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科煩惱不具或具，能害者有煩惱不具或具的差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此能害者，或貪所蔽、或瞋所蔽、或癡所蔽、或二所蔽、或三所蔽，而起作心，是名煩惱。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這位能傷害生命的人，有貪瞋癡三種煩惱完全具足或不完全具足的情形，或為貪、或瞋、或癡一種的煩惱所遮蔽，或為貪瞋、或貪癡、或瞋癡二種煩惱所遮蔽，或者貪瞋癡三種煩惱所遮蔽，而生起想要殺害眾生的心情。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳五、隨起方便及得究竟2　午一、爾時究竟</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科隨起方便及得究竟，開始行動而且造業成功，分二科；第一科爾時究竟，當下即死了。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">彼由欲樂及染汙心，或自、或他發起方便加害眾生。若害無間彼便命終，即此方便，當於爾時說名成就究竟業道。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　能殺害的人由於有想要殺的欲樂及染汙心，或者由自己或者由他人，發起實際的行動殺害眾生。若殺的當時沒有間斷地就死了，在實際行動的當時，名為成就究竟的殺生業道。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、後時究竟</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科後時究竟，當下沒死，事後一段時間才死。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若於後時彼方捨命，由此方便，彼命終時乃名成就究竟業道。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若被殺的有情，當時沒有死，過一段時間以後才死，有情命終時，這種殺生行動，才稱為成就究竟殺生業道，殺生業道才圓滿。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《瑜伽論記》中說：聲聞乘是死了才成就根本業道，大乘沒有這個文。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、不與取業道</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科不與取業道，指偷盜，偷盜的業道也要五相具足才圓滿。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="59p4830"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">不與取業道。事者，謂他所攝物。想者，謂於彼彼想。欲樂者，謂劫盜欲。煩惱者，謂三毒，或具不具。方便究竟者，謂起方便移離本處。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　不與取業道五相中：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、事，是指屬於他人所攝物，他人所擁有的物，包括有情或非情物，譬如家畜或者是金銀財寶。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、想，是指對所要偷盜的有情或非情物，確認沒有錯誤。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、欲樂，是指偷盜的欲望生起來，起盜心了。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、煩惱，是指貪瞋癡可能都有，或只有貪瞋癡中的一種或二種。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、方便究竟，只要將偷盜的有情或非情物移開本處，就稱為偷盜了。佛法很嚴格，起了盜心，將它移離本處，就稱為偷盜。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》移離本處者：謂他所攝財穀等事。或於聚落中，或於閑靜處，若積集、若移轉故。義如本地分說。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/08.htm#47999:5706">陵本八卷九頁585</a>）</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　屬於他人的財產或稻穀這些事情，在村落中或寂靜處，將它拿起來積集在一起或是移開。在〈本地分‧有尋有伺等三地〉卷8，242頁說過。移離本處的處，處所，包括山河大地，地上、地下的空間，橋或船，如果盜取船上的物品，船移動，就是移離本處。這些事情在戒律中，有詳細的說明。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰三、欲邪行業道</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科欲邪行業道，說明欲邪行業道五相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">欲邪行業道。事者，謂女所不應行；設所應行，非支、非處、非時、非量；若不應理，一切男及不男。想者，於彼彼想。欲樂者，謂樂行之欲。煩惱者，謂三毒，或具不具。方便究竟者，謂兩兩交會。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在欲邪行業道五相中：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、事，是指對所不應行欲邪行的對象及所不應作的欲邪行事，包括對女性、一切男性及非男性（男根不具之人）。即使是合適的對象，若是不合道理的，如部位不對、地點不對、時間不對、數量也超過了，都是在事的範圍內。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、想，是指欲邪行的對象沒有錯認，沒有顛倒想。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、欲樂，是歡喜做這件事的欲望。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、煩惱，有具足貪瞋癡三毒或者其中一種或二種。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、方便究竟，就是兩兩交會，做欲邪行這件事情。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》謂女所不應行等者：如下自說：若於母等、母等所護，如經廣說，名不應行。一切男及不男，屬自屬他，皆不應行。又此非支、非處、非時、非量，亦如下釋。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如下文說：男眾做這事情時，如果對方是母親長輩等或有母親長輩等守護的女眾，如經上說的，都是不應該作的。對於同性的男眾，或者非男眾（男根不具之人），屬於自己或屬於他人，都是不應該行欲的對象。對於非支、非處、非時、非量，下面還會詳細解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰四、妄語業道</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科妄語業道，妄語是不說真實話，說假話，說明妄語業道五相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">妄語業道。事者，謂見聞覺知，不見、不聞、不覺、不知。想者，謂於見等或翻彼想。欲樂者，謂覆藏想樂說之欲。煩惱者，謂貪瞋癡，或具不具。方便究竟者，謂時眾及對論者領解。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　妄語業道的五相中：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、事，是六識依六根見聞覺知六境時，所說的話是見言不見、聞言不聞、覺言不覺、知言不知，與事實相反。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、想，是對於見聞覺知所取的境相正確無誤，或生起顛倒想；或如披尋記說：於未見、聞、覺、知所取的境相隨他所生起的一種想。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、欲樂，有想將事情的真相覆藏起來的動機，想說假話。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、煩惱，是貪瞋癡具足或不具足，只具其中一種或二種。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、方便究竟，說這句話當時的聽眾或是對話的人，明白自己所說的話，只要對方明白，妄語業道就成就了。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="59p4831"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》謂於見等或翻彼想者：謂於見聞覺知，或於不見、不聞、不覺、不知，隨起一想故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　對於於見聞覺知，說為未見、未聞、未覺、未知隨起其中的一種想，或於不見、不聞、不覺、不知生起見聞覺知隨起其中的一種想。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰五、離間語業道</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科離間語業道，說使對方彼此不和合語，稱為離間語，說明離間語業道五相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">離間語業道。事者，謂諸有情或和不和。想者，謂俱於彼若合若離，隨起一想。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　離間語業道的五相中：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、事，是指說離間語的對象，二個或多個有情彼此是和合的或者是不和合的。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、想，知道他們是和合的或已經乖離了，認識這件事情，稱為隨起一想。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》謂俱於彼若合若離等者：謂於和合有情起和合想，若乖離者起乖離想，是名隨起一想。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　了知對方原本是和合的好朋友，或是知道他們彼此之間已經是有意見分開了，很清楚對方是和合或是乖離的情形，稱為隨起一想。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">欲樂者，謂樂彼乖離，若不和合欲。煩惱者，謂三毒，或具不具。方便究竟者，謂所破領解。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、欲樂方面，是指不論對方是和合或已經不和合了，都希望看到對方互相違背離開，希望他們不要和合的意樂。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、煩惱，想要破壞對方的感情，一定有貪瞋癡三毒全部，或者其中一或二。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、方便究竟，就是所破壞的有情，他們理解這件事情，使得彼此不和合，離間語究竟，破壞成功了。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》所破領解者：和合有情，能令破壞；乖離有情，令更乖違；彼二有情皆名所破。聞離間語，解所說義，是名領解。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　離間破壞，使對方領解的二種情況，一種情況，對方之間原本感情很好，因為向對方說了離間話，使令他們的感情破壞。另一種情況對方之間已經不和合，能令他們更乖違。二種情況都稱為所破。對方聽到離間語，了解所說的道理，稱為領解。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰六、麤惡語業道</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科麤惡語業道，麤惡語就是罵人的話，說明麤惡語業道五相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="59p4832"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">麤惡語業道。事者，謂諸有情能為違損。想者，謂於彼彼想。欲樂者，謂樂麤言欲。煩惱者，謂三毒，或具不具。方便究竟者，謂訶罵彼。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　麤惡語業道五相中：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、事，是指各種有情，由此麤惡語想要違背損害的各種有情。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、想，是於甲生甲想，想罵的對象，正是那個人。</span></span></span></div>
