<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、欲樂，想以麤惡語罵的欲望。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、煩惱，罵人時有貪瞋癡煩惱在裏面，或全部都有，或其中一種或二種。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、方便究竟者，出口罵對方，就算究竟完成麤惡語的業道。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《瑜伽論記》說：不必對象領解。因為要罵人的心情，只是想將心裏的怒氣發洩出來而已，對方聽得懂不懂，都算方便究竟了。與離間語不同，離間語要對方聽懂，才能被離間。麤惡語不論對方有沒有聽懂，只要出口罵，這件事就是方便究竟了。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰七、綺語業道</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第七科綺語業道，說沒有義利的話，就是綺語，說明綺語業道五相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">綺語業道。事者，謂能引發無利之義。想者，謂於彼彼想。欲樂者，謂樂說之欲。煩惱者，謂三毒，或具不具。方便究竟者，謂纔發言。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　綺語業道五相中：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、事，說這句話能引發沒有義利的境界，可能引起他人的貪瞋癡。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、想，沒有認錯所說綺語的對象。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、欲樂，有想說綺語的欲望。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、煩惱，貪瞋癡全部都有或其中一種或二種。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、方便究竟，只要一說出口，就算綺語了。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五相如果具足，綺語業道即成就了。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《瑜伽論記》卷17說：「綺語有二種。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、相應綺語，即前三語非義非時，名為綺語。方便究竟時，如前三語。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、獨頭綺語，若為他說外道邪論，若為調戲前人而作歌詠，亦便他解方成究竟，若私屏自有歌詠哭泣悲歎，纔發言詞即成業道。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》謂能引發無利之義者：不為諸利益事所依處故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　說綺語不能作為引發利益事的依止處。能引發他人的貪瞋癡，都可以稱為綺語。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《成實論》卷8說下列情形都是綺語：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、在不洽當的時間說真實語。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、雖在洽當的時間說真實語，因為所說真實語的內容，隨順衰惱、無義利。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、雖在洽當的時間說真實語，也有利益，但所說真實語的內容，本末沒有道理，沒有次第。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、以貪瞋癡等煩惱，散心說話。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、依不正的身業、意業發出語言。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　六、其餘三種口業皆夾雜綺語不得相離。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　綺語非常微細難可捨離，唯有諸佛能斷其根，因此唯有諸佛獨稱世尊，眾生聽佛說法，能歡喜信受，依教奉行，其他人說話，都沒有這種功德威力。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰八、貪欲業道</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第八科貪欲業道，說明貪欲業道五相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">貪欲業道。事者，謂屬他財產。想者，謂於彼彼想。欲樂者，謂即如是愛欲。煩惱者，謂三毒，或具不具。方便究竟者，謂於彼事定期屬己。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　貪欲業道五相中：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、事者，屬於他人的財產，包括人事物都是財產，如金錢，房子、金銀財寶等。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、想者，確定所要貪的人、事、物，沒有錯認。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、欲樂者，對所貪的對象生起樂欲。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、煩惱者，心裏有貪瞋癡，或者其中一或二。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、方便究竟者，心中所貪的人、事、物，認為一定要歸屬自己。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰九、瞋恚業道</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第九科瞋恚業道，說明瞋恚業道五相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="6015:48022"></a>瞋恚業道。事之與想如麤惡語說。欲樂者，謂損害等欲。煩惱者，謂三毒，或具不具。方便究竟者，謂損害等期心決定。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　瞋恚業道五相中：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、事，是指想要瞋恚的種種有情。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、想，是確定的所瞋恚的對象。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、欲樂，有想損害對方的欲樂。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、煩惱，有貪瞋癡全部，或者其中一、二種。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、方便究竟，只要內心決定損害對方，就已經方便究竟了。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》謂損害等欲者：惡意分別，名損害欲。或欲當殺、當害、當為衰損、彼當自獲種種憂惱。如是一切皆此所攝，故置等言。義如本地分說。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/08.htm#48023:6003">陵本八卷十三頁610</a>）</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　惡意分別，心想損害對方，稱為損害欲。瞋恚的程度是想殺或傷害對方、或希望對方財產衰損，或對方家裏的人事衰損，或使對方獲得種種的憂愁、苦惱，這都是一種瞋恚心，都是屬於瞋恚業道所攝，所以安置「等」字。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在〈本地分〉卷8，251頁有詳細的說明。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="59p4833"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰十、邪見業道</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十科邪見業道，邪見是錯誤的思想，這也是內心的分別，因為愚癡，所以不明白道理。說明邪見業道五相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">邪見業道。事者，謂實有義。想者，謂於有非有想。欲樂者，謂即如是愛欲。煩惱者，謂三毒，或具不具。方便究竟者，謂誹謗決定。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　邪見業道五相中：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、事，是指實有的境界。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、想，對真實有的事作非有想，如對真實有的三寶、四諦等，卻認為是沒有這回事的。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、欲樂，很喜歡這樣的一種想法，認為自己的想法才是對的。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、煩惱，有貪瞋癡全部，或是其中一種或二種煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、方便究竟，對於毀謗實有事等生起決定的執著，稱為方便究竟。若由邪見發出誹謗，屬於重綺語業道所攝，如本論卷60說：若以染汙心，於能引無義外道典籍承誦、讚詠、廣為他說。由事重故，名重綺語。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這五種條件具足時，稱為邪見業道圓滿。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》謂誹謗決定者：於實有義誹謗非有，起決定執故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　對於實有的事，如三寶、四諦，誹謗沒有這回事，生起堅固決定的執著，名誹謗決定。以上是十不善業道的五相具足的情況，做一個說明。最好是配合前面〈本地分‧有尋有伺等三地〉卷8的業雜染閱讀，會更清楚造業究竟的條件。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅三、隨別廣2　卯一、廣殺生2　辰一、標列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科隨別廣，接著各別詳細解釋，分二科；第一科廣殺生，詳細說明殺生的情況。又分二科；第一科標列，標示列舉出三種。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，殺生有三種。一、有罪增長，二、有罪不增長，三、無有罪。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，殺生有三種情況：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、有罪過而且罪過還繼續的增長。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、有罪過，但是沒有增長。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、殺生但沒有罪過。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、隨釋2　巳一、舉罪因</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科隨釋，接著解釋，分二科；第一科舉罪因，說明生出罪過的原因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">生罪因緣，亦略有三。一、煩惱所起，二、能生於苦，三、希望滿足。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　殺生有罪過的因緣有三種：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、由煩惱所生起，由貪瞋癡而想殺害對方；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、能生於苦，使令自己或他人生出痛苦；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、希望滿足，殺生加行究竟，圓滿自己的希望。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、別配屬</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科別配屬，各別配屬。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">初具三緣；次有二種，無希望滿；後唯生苦。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　初有罪還增長，是指具足煩惱所起、能生於苦、希望滿足這三種緣：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、由煩惱所生起的殺生；能生出自苦、他苦；想殺生的願望得到滿足，有歡喜心，覺得做對了，這是有罪過而且增長。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、其次有罪而不增長，是指具足煩惱所起、能生於苦這二種緣，但不具希望滿足，可能是作已究竟卻後悔了，或作已沒有究竟，沒有殺生的希望與滿足感。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、沒有罪過的殺生只具唯生苦一種緣，只是令自他痛苦而已，沒有罪過。因為不是以貪瞋癡惡心來殺的，可能是以慈心而殺或誤殺。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《瑜伽論記》說沒有罪過的殺生，是指菩薩為了救度眾生而殺眾生，這是慈心而殺，沒有貪瞋癡，沒有殺心，但是對方也會受苦。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　還有一種情形是：前一生，甲誤殺過乙，後一生同樣的因緣乙就誤殺甲，這樣的事情是沒有罪，只是業果的關係，一命還一命。如安世高，知道過去生曾誤殺他人，預知這一生自己也會在會稽（今浙江省）被誤殺，因誤殺的因緣而度化一位少年出家修行。這件事不是對方要殺他，是他前生也這樣誤殺過那個人，這生他必須還命，償還前世的債，所以無記心殺生有苦，沒有罪過。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="59p4834"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》生罪因緣等者：謂殺生者殺生為因，生現法罪、生後法罪、生現法後法罪。如本地分說。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/09.htm#48036:6621">陵本九卷九頁671</a>）今於此中，說彼因緣略有三種。由煩惱蔽而起作心，是名煩惱所起。若不能辦隨欲殺事，彼由所欲不會因緣，便受所生身心憂苦，是名能生於苦。彼業現行而得究竟，是名希望滿足。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　殺生的人，以殺生為因緣，生現法罪，使現在的色受想行識生命體有罪過；生後法罪，來生墮地獄；或者生現法後法罪，現在世被治罰，來生也要墮地獄。在〈本地分‧有尋有伺等三地〉卷9，276頁說過。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這裡說到殺生的因緣略有三種：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、由煩惱的障蔽而生起殺害的心，稱為煩惱所起。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、如果想殺生，但不能隨自所想的殺生，得不到殺生的因緣，身心就產生憂苦，是名能生於苦。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、發起殺害業行，對方也死了，稱為希望滿足。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、廣貪欲等2　辰一、總標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科廣貪欲等，詳細說明貪欲等五相，分二科；第一科總標，總相標出由五相，建立貪欲等自相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，略由五相，建立貪欲、瞋恚、邪見圓滿自相。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，要略可以歸納成五相來建立貪欲、瞋恚、邪見業道的圓滿自相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、別釋3　巳一、貪欲2　午一、辨五相2　未一、徵起</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科別釋，各別解釋，分三科；第一科貪欲，說明貪欲五相，又分二科；第一科辨五相，先說明五種相貌，又分二科；第一科徵起，先問起。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">何等名為貪欲五相？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼稱為貪欲的五種相貌？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、列釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列釋，列舉出來解釋什麼稱為貪欲。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、有耽著心，謂於自財所。二、有貪婪心，謂樂積財物。三、有饕餮心，謂於屬他資財等事計為華好，深生愛味。四、有謀略心，謂作是心：凡彼所有，何當屬我。五、有覆蔽心，謂貪欲纏之所覆故，不覺羞恥，不知過患及與出離。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　貪欲的五相：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、有耽著心，對於自己財產耽溺、愛著，很貪愛自己的財產。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、有貪婪心，歡喜積聚財物，古人說貪財名貪，貪食名婪，或貪得無厭稱為婪。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、有饕餮心，對他人的財物，認為很美好，心裏深深的貪愛、味著，像老饕一樣，有了還不滿足，還要更多。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、有謀略心，有計謀，心想凡是屬於他人的財物，何不也屬於我的。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、有覆蔽心，有貪欲的煩惱覆蔽自己的心，所以不覺羞恥，耽著心、貪婪心、饕餮心、謀略心、覆蔽心等會有很多的過患及不知應該出離自己的貪心。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這是貪欲業道的五相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、顯圓滿2　未一、簡非3　申一、闕餘四種</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科顯圓滿，說明成就貪欲業道的圓滿相，分二科；第一科簡非，簡除不圓滿的情況，又分三科；第一科闕餘四種，如果缺乏其它四種心，都不能稱為貪欲業道的圓滿。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">設於自財有耽著心，無餘心現，當知此非圓滿貪欲意惡行相。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有貪欲時，必須具足如前所說的五種心，才能說是貪欲業道究竟。如果只是對自己的財產有耽著心，而沒有其它四種的貪婪心、饕餮心、謀略心、覆蔽心，只有耽著心的話，不能說是圓滿貪欲業道的惡劣行相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="59p4835"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、闕餘三種</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科闕餘三種，缺其它的三種也是不圓滿的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是有耽著心及貪婪心，無餘心現，亦非圓滿貪欲之相。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果有耽著心及貪婪心二種心情，對於自己的財產有耽著心喜歡積聚財物，但是沒有饕餮心、謀略心、覆蔽心三種心，也不是圓滿的貪欲業道之相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申三、隨闕一種</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科隨闕一種，隨闕一種都不算圓滿。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是廣說，乃至如前所說諸相隨闕一種，即非圓滿貪欲之相。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　再詳細說，只要於前所說其中一種心不具足，都不能算是圓滿貪欲業道之相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、顯正</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科顯正，顯出圓滿貪欲業道相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若全分攝，乃名圓滿貪欲之相。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若貪欲者，具足耽著心、饕餮心、謀略心、覆蔽心五種心，才是圓滿貪欲業道相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、瞋恚2　午一、辨五相2　未一、徵起</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科瞋恚，說明瞋恚五相，分二科；第一科辨五相，瞋心也有五種相貌才是圓滿的，又分二科；第一科徵起，問起。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">何等名為瞋恚五相？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼稱為瞋心的五種相貌？。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、列釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列釋，列舉出來解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="59p4836"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、有憎惡心，謂於能損害相隨法分別故。二、有不堪耐心，謂於不饒益不堪忍故。三、有怨恨心，謂於不饒益數不如理隨憶念故。四、有謀略心，謂於有情作如是意：何當捶撻、何當殺害，乃至廣說故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　圓滿瞋心業道的五種相貌包括：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、有憎惡心，隨著過去的因緣或現前的境界，由分別心生起損害他人的心相。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、有不堪耐心，於對方有不饒益的損害心及不能忍耐的心情，而生起瞋恚心。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、有怨恨心，怨恨對方，心裏不斷的思惟不利對方的事情，與煩惱相應、不如佛法的真理的瞋恨，常隨念於心。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、有謀略心，對所瞋恨的有情生起這樣的心情：思惟應該如何捶打、殺死加害對方，乃至使對方獲得種種的憂愁苦惱等，生起種種不利對方的想法。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》何當捶撻等者：欲為損害，由是說言何當捶撻。欲為殺害，乃至欲彼自獲種種憂惱，由是說言何當殺害，乃至廣說。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　心中想要損害、不利益對方，所以說應當如何捶打撻罰對方。心中想要殺害對方，乃至希望對方獲得種種的憂愁苦惱，因此說應當如何殺害，乃至詳細說有各種殺心。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">五、有覆蔽心，謂如前說。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、有覆蔽心，如同前面所說。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有貪瞋煩惱，覆蔽自己的心情，起了瞋心還不知道羞恥，不知道起報復的心是錯的，不知瞋心是有過患的：一念瞋心起，百千障門開。雖然對方對自己不好，可是自己起了瞋心，第一個傷害到的是自己，所有的功德都燒掉了。不知道修行人不可以有瞋心。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　佛在《四十二章經》說：在家行欲之人，瞋恚還可以說，出家人離欲了，怎麼還可以有瞋心呢！如果出家人有瞋心，譬如清冷雲中，霹靂火起。本來是要離欲，應該是很清淨的，可是忽然生起霹靂般的瞋火，破懷清淨的天空，這是不應該的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、顯圓滿</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科顯圓滿，顯出圓滿瞋恚五相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於此五相隨闕一種，即非圓滿瞋恚之相；若具一切，方名圓滿。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在憎惡心、不堪耐心、怨恨心、謀略心、覆蔽心這五種相貌當中，如果缺乏一種就不是圓滿瞋恚之相；如果具足一切，才是圓滿的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳三、邪見2　午一、辨五相2　未一、徵起</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科邪見，也名癡，說明邪見業道，分二科；第一科辨五相，說明邪見五種相貌，分二科；第一科徵起，問起。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">何等名為邪見五相？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼稱為邪見的五種相貌？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、列釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列釋，列舉出來解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、有愚癡心，謂不如實了所知故。二、有暴酷心，謂樂作諸惡故。三、有越流行心，謂於諸法不如理分別推求故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　邪見的五種相貌：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、有愚癡心，不如實明了事情的真相。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、有暴酷心，有暴戾殘酷的心，歡喜做種種的惡事。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、有越流行心，有超越善流的不善心，這是由於對諸法，包括三寶、四諦，不如真理分別、推求的緣故，導致不善心相續流轉。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="59p4837"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》有越流行心者：前說流轉差別。有善流流轉，謂諸善行。又有不善流流轉，謂諸不善行。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/52.htm#48068:40604">陵本五十二卷十三頁4188</a>）今說不善流流轉，名有越流行心，違越善流流轉故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　前文說流轉差別。流就是平等流類，同樣都是善的心行活動，稱為善流流轉。又有不善流流轉，相似相續的不善行，稱為不善流流轉。在〈決擇‧五識身相應地意地〉卷52，1736頁曾說過。此處說不善流流轉，稱為有越流行心，是指違背善的心行活動─善流流轉，而生不善行。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">四、有失壞心，謂無施與、愛養、祠祀等，誹謗一切妙行等故。五、有覆蔽心，謂邪見纏之所覆蔽，不覺羞恥，不知過患及出離故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、有失壞心，認為沒有布施，布施不能得到善果；沒有愛養，恭敬愛養父母或者師長不能得到善果；沒有祠祀等，執著除了祭祀供養火天以外，其他沒有麼對象值得祭祀供養，誹謗一切善行，如修五戒十善，修禪定，認為沒有意義，這是錯誤的邪見。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、有覆蔽心，被邪見煩惱覆障遮蔽，不覺得羞恥，又不知道邪見有很多過患，也不知道要出離邪惡的思想。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、顯圓滿</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科顯圓滿，顯出圓滿邪見五相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於此五相隨闕一種，即非圓滿邪見之相；具一切分，乃名圓滿。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這五種相貌中：一、有愚癡心，二、有暴酷心，三、有越流行心，四、有失壞心，五、有覆蔽心。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果缺乏一種就不是圓滿的邪見之相，具足一切五相，才稱為圓滿。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以上是業雜染七門決擇裏面的第一科是自性相。約十不善業道來說。第二科是說到方便相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子二、方便10　丑一、殺生攝3　寅一、約所作辨</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科方便，說明造作十不善業道的種種行動，分十科；第一科殺生攝，說明殺生所攝方便，又分三科；第一科約所作辨，約所作的來說明。第二科約所為辦，約造業的目的、動機來說，第三科約自他辦，約自己和他人來說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，若以手等害諸眾生，說名殺生。如是以塊、杖刀、縛錄、斷食、折挫、治罰、呪藥、厭禱、尸半尸等害諸眾生，皆名殺生。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，殺生的方法有：用自己的手將眾生殺死，稱為殺眾生。或者用石塊、木杖、刀子、用繩子綁起來再殺死；使令對方沒有東西吃而餓死；做一些事令對方有挫折或折磨到死；處罰對方到死；將符咒放在藥裏面，對方吃了就死掉；以厭惡心禱告將人殺死；或以假人頭插幾個針將人殺死。屍與半屍殺害眾生有三種解釋：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第一種是神泰法師說：屍，是有人想要殺仇人，就咒令死屍殺害怨家。用咒術使屍體活過來，用屍體來殺害人，稱為屍。半屍，指所咒的屍體是沒有頭的，無頭屍稱為半屍，用咒術使半屍殺害人。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二種解釋是圓測法師法師說：屍，是用咒術使令鬼或屍體來殺人稱為屍；半屍，用屍體的手足來殺有情稱為半屍。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　另外一位法師說《薩婆多律》有部律面說：有一種咒屍是使屍體乘著二輪車，雙手拿劍來殺人，稱為全屍；另一種咒屍是乘著一個輪子的，只有一隻手拿劍，將人殺掉，稱為半屍。都是用鬼用死人來殺人。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以上都是殺生的方便、方法。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、約所為辨</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科約所為辨，約殺生的動機來說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="6199:48075"></a>為財利等害諸眾生，亦名殺生。或恐為損、或為除怨、或謂為法，乃至或為戲樂害諸眾生，亦名殺生。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　殺害眾生的動機有：為了得到財產利益而殺害對方，也稱為殺生；或者怕被對方損害，如果自己不殺對方，對方就要殺自己；或是很怨恨對方，想要將對方殺掉；或認為殺生是合法的，例如外道認為豬、雞、鴨本來出生就是要給人殺的，將牠殺掉是合法的；或為了好玩去灌蟋蟀、抓青蛙、釣魚而殺生，覺得這件事情很愉快，很快樂，也稱為殺生。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅三、約自他辨</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科約自他辨，約自己或他人來說明，約自作或令他人作來說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若自殺害，若令他害，皆得殺罪。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若自己動手殺害有情或唆使他人去殺害有情，都會得到殺生罪。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="59p4838"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》或謂為法等者：謂如有一，於殺生事起是法想，名謂為法。或復有一，於殺生事現在前時，如遊戲法，極為喜樂，名為戲樂。或復邪見為因而行殺生，是故於中置乃至言。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如有一種人，認為殺生是合法的，稱為法。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　或是在做殺生事時，非常歡喜快樂，覺得很像是在玩遊戲，稱為戲樂。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　或是因邪見而行殺生，因此於文中安置乃至這句話。例如認為殺人祭祀是合法的，或拜拜一定要殺雞殺鴨等，都是因邪見而行殺生。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這些是約殺生的方便來說，殺生的途徑有這麼多，這裡是舉出認為是合法、戲樂、邪見三法來說明。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑二、不與取攝2　寅一、約所作辨</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科不與取攝，說明偷盜的行為模式，分二科；第一科約所作辨，約所作的事情來說明。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，若有顯然劫他財物，名不與取。如是竊盜、攻牆解結、伏道竊奪，或有拒債、受寄不還，或行誑諂矯詐而取，或現怖畏方便而取，或現威德而取彼物，或自劫盜，或復令他，如是一切皆不與取。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，如果有很明顯、公然劫奪他人的財務，名為不與取。不與取的方便有：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　竊盜，竊是私下，私下將它盜取過來；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　攻牆解結，戰爭時攻倒城牆，將繩子或其他的障礙解開，搶奪他人的財務；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　或伏道竊奪，躲在路邊、樹林裏，當有攜帶珍寶的人經過時，就出來搶劫；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　或有欠他人債，拒絕歸還他人，拒絕還債就是不與取了；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　或他人將東西寄放在自己的處所，該歸還時不還給物主；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　或是欺騙、諂媚、矯飾詐現而取，如有些人沒有禪定、聖道，矯飾詐現自己有禪定、聖道，現出威望道德，以謀取他人的供養；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　或是顯現出很恐怖、害怕的樣子，使人覺得楚楚可憐，就將財物布施給他；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　或是現出很有威德很強勢，帶有一些威脅強勢，硬將對方財物奪取過來；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　或自己去劫盜；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　或唆使他人去做這件事。以上所說各式各樣的情況都稱為不與取。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、約所為辨</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科約所為辨，約偷盜的動機說明。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">或有自為，或有為他，或怖畏故，或為殺縛，或為折伏，或為受用，或為給侍，或憎嫉故不與而取，此等皆名不與取罪。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　種種不與取的動機包括：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為了自己得到財物；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　或者是為了他人做這件事情；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　或是因為害怕、畏懼；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　或是為了怕被殺或者被繫縛，偷錢來贖罪；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　或為了折伏對方；或為了受用；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　或者為了供給侍奉父母、師長等；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　或者憎恨嫉妒對方太多錢，而行偷盜。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這些都稱為不與取罪。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑三、欲邪行攝3　寅一、約所作辨2　卯一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科欲邪行攝，說明欲邪行所攝方便，分三科；第一科約所作辨，約做的行為來說明，分二科；第一科標，標出欲邪行相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="6158:48085"></a><a name="563:48085"></a>復次，若行不應行，名欲邪行。或於非支、非時、非處、非量、非理，如是一切皆欲邪行。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，如果做不應該做的事情，都稱為欲邪行。包括非支、非時、非處、非量、非理，這些都是欲邪行。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　欲邪行分六科來說明，以下一一解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="59p4839"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、釋6　辰一、不應行</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分六科；第一科不應行，於所不應行的對象。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若於母等、母等所護，如經廣說，名不應行。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這是就男子的角度，約所行的對象來說明。如果對於阿羅漢尼或者對於母親等，或有母親等守護的女人，或沒有母親守護而有家長、姑姑、婆婆、叔叔、其他親戚朋友守護，乃至是公家機關收留她，有人守護的這些女子，都稱為不應行。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》若於母等母等所護等者：謂於阿羅漢尼及於母所行穢染行，名於母等。此成無間業同分，如本地分說。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/09.htm#48090:6295">陵本九卷三頁641</a>）未適他者，為三守護之所守護。一、尊重至親眷屬自己之所守護，二、王執理家之所守護，三、諸守門者之所守護。是名母等所護，是不應行。又他妻妾，由已適他，亦不應行。為顯此義，指如經說。如是一切，如本地分釋相應知。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/08.htm#48090:5779">陵本八卷十頁591</a>）</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果欲邪行的對象是阿羅漢尼或者對於母親行穢染行，稱為名於母等。這件事的罪過，一定下地獄的，是相等於無間地獄的業。在〈本地分‧有尋有伺等三地〉卷9，263頁有說到這件事情。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　未適他者，是還沒嫁人的女子，她有三種人在守護。包括：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、尊重的父母或者至親或者眷屬或者她自己，有人守護的女人。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、王執理家的官府，被官府收留的，可能是宮女，國王的後宮，是不能侵犯的。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、諸守門者之所守護，有守門人守護的女人。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　總之，有人保護的女人，是不應該與她有欲的。還有他人的妻妾，已經嫁給他人，也不應該作這件事。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為開顯這些道理，指出如經典上說，很多經典說到這些事。這些在〈本地分‧有尋有伺等三地〉卷8，243頁那裏曾解釋這件事的相狀，應當了知。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一切男及不男，屬自屬他，皆不應行。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果站在男子的角度來說，一切男及不男，不男是男根有損壞的，自己也不可以自淫也不可以淫他，這樣都不可以作的。佛法這件事情是說得很清楚。前面是說對象是女的，這裡是說對象是男的。佛經的角度多半是站在男眾的角度說，由此可以很明顯的說，佛法不贊成同性戀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、非支</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科非支，不是合適的處所也名欲邪行。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="5799:48093"></a>除產門外，所有餘分皆名非支。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　除了婦女的產門外，其他的部位都稱為非支。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰三、非時</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科非時，時間不對也是欲邪行。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="59p4840"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若穢下時、胎圓滿時、飲兒乳時、受齋戒時，或有病時，謂所有病匪宜習欲，是名非時。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在女方有月事的時候、胎兒圓滿的時候、母親在餵奶時、受八關齋戒時、或是對方有病時，都是不可以有欲的。如果還做這件事，稱為非時。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰四、非處</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科非處，處所不對名欲邪行。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若諸尊重所集會處，或靈廟中，或大眾前，或堅硬地高下不平，令不安隱，如是等處說名非處。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　不合適的處所，指眾所尊重的大德集會的地方，例如講堂或是靈廟，供養三寶的寺廟中，或大眾前，或者堅硬、高下不平的地方，使令對方不安穩，這都稱為非處。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰五、非量</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科非量，非量也名欲邪行。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">過量而行，名為非量。是中量者，極至於五，此外一切皆名過量。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　過量就是超過了，稱為非量。其中所說的量，最多到五次，此外一切都稱為過量。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰六、非理</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科非理，不依世間的禮俗。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">不依世禮，故名非理。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　不依世間的方法，稱為非禮。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、約自他辨</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科約自他辨，以上是約所不應做的事來說明，第二科是約自己與他人來說明。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若自行欲，若媒合他，此二皆名欲邪行攝。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果自己有欲邪行的事，或者媒介他人完成這件事情，這二種都稱作欲邪行。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅三、約顯隱辨</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科約顯隱辨，約公開顯示或隱蔽的方式說明。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="59p4841"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若有公顯，或復隱竊，或因誑諂方便矯亂，或因委託而行邪行，如是皆名欲邪行罪。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果是公開顯示要做這件事情；或是沒有公開顯示但是私下偷偷地；或是用欺騙諂媚對方，或是假現威儀欺騙對方；或因受託而做這件事，這都稱為欲邪行罪。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑四、妄語攝3　寅一、約所因辨</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科妄語攝，妄語所攝方便，分三科；第一科約所因辨，約說妄語的原因分辨。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，若自因故而說妄語，或他因故，或因怖畏，或因財利而說妄語，皆名妄語。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，妄語的原因有很多種，有為了自己而說妄語；或是為了他人的原因；或是害怕他人知道而對自己不利，如矯亂外道，因為怖畏他人知道自己無知，而說妄語；或者為了要得到錢財利益或所需物品而說妄語，由這些原因所說都稱為妄語。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、約覆想辨</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科約覆想辨，約覆蓋想說明。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若不見聞覺知言見聞覺知，或見聞覺知言不見聞覺知，皆名妄語。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若沒有見聞覺知說自己有見聞覺知，或有見聞覺知卻說自己沒有見聞覺知，覆藏遮蓋自己所想的，都屬於妄語。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅三、約所作辨</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科約所作辨，約妄語的方式說明。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若書陳說，或以默然表忍斯義，或動支體以表其相，或為證說，或有自說，或令他說，如是一切皆妄語罪。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　妄語表達的方式有多種，用文字的書信表示假象、用不說話的默然表示忍可這種道理、用肢體語言點頭、搖頭、微笑或手勢、或用不實的證明表示、或是自己直接用不實的語言說出，或使他人說假話等都是屬於妄語罪。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑五、離間語攝2　寅一、約所依辨</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科離間語攝，說明離間語所攝方便，分二科；第一科約所依辨，約所依止的方便說明。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="5861:48116"></a>復次，若以實事毀訾於他，為乖離故而發此言，名離間語。或以不實假合方便以為依止，為損壞他而有陳說，或依親近施與、或依知友給侍而有陳說，名離間語。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，說離間語所依止的方式有幾種。一是以真實的事情來毀謗他人，如甲曾罵乙，就去對乙說：甲罵你了。這是真實的事情，藉這樣的事說出來使令他們乖離，這是離間語。或是以不實的事情，用假的方式，製造假象，為了損害他人而說一些話，使令他們乖離，或藉著親近、布施、或供養給侍對方的機會，說出使對方乖離的話，這都是離間語。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、約因緣辨</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科約因緣辨，約離間語的因緣說明。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="59p4842"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若自利緣，或損他緣，或由他教，或現破德，或現怖畏，為乖離故，或自發言、或令他發，如是皆名離間語罪。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　說離間語的因緣，有的是為了自利；或是為了損害他人；或是他人教唆這樣做的；或是宣說他人沒有真實的功德或功德不圓滿；或是利用對方之間的矛盾，假裝顯現很害怕，來乖離他人彼此的感情，或自己說出離間語、或使令他人說出離間語，這些都稱為離間語罪。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》或現破德者：謂宣說他無實功德故，或不圓滿故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　於有功德的人，對外宣說說他沒有真實的功德，或是功德不圓滿，離間他人對他的尊敬，使令他人對他的感情乖離了，稱為或現破德。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑六、麤惡語攝</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科麤惡語，惡言口似犁，說一句粗話，像耕田的犁，犁過他人的心田，使人痛楚不堪，名麤惡語，說明麤惡語的方便。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，若有對面發辛楚言，名麤惡語。或不現前，或對大眾，或幽僻處，或隨實過不隨實過，或書表示，或假現相，或依自說，或依他說，或因掉舉，或因不靜，或依種族過失，或依依止過失，或依作業禁戒現行過失，或自發起辛楚之言，或令他發，如是皆名麤惡語罪。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，發出麤惡語也有多種。當面向對方發出令人痛苦的語言，稱為麤惡語。或是在背後說；或當大眾面前；或在幽靜偏僻的地方，或隨對方真實的過失，或隨對方不是真實的過失，或以書信方式表達，或假裝罵出來，或依自己說，或依他人說，或因內心掉動高舉，或因內心不寂靜，就是有煩惱而罵，或因為種族歧視，白人看不起黃人，黃人又看不起黑人，或者罵的是因為這個人諸根不俱，名依止過失，如眼瞎、耳聾、或啞巴，就罵對方一定是造什麼大惡業，才會這樣，或依對方做的事情或所持的戒，現出種種過失，而破口大罵。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以上種種粗惡語或由自己發起，或令他人發動，都稱為麤惡語罪。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》或依種族過失等者：生下賤家，是名種族過失。諸根不具，是名依止過失。身語所作違犯禁戒，是名作業禁戒現行過失。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　生下賤家，稱為種族過失。如在印度四姓種族中，生旃荼羅家，就是除糞家，會被輕賤。六根不具足，稱為依止過失，如眼瞎耳聾的人，畸形兒或低能兒等。身業及語業有犯戒的過失，稱為作業禁戒現行過失。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑七、綺語攝2　寅一、約種種辨4　卯一、依舞樂歌詞</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第七科綺語，說明綺語的方便，分二科；第一科約種種辨，約種種綺語說明，又分四科；第一科依舞樂歌詞，依舞樂而發歌詞名綺語。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，若有依舞而發歌詞，名為綺語。或依作樂，或復俱依，或俱不依而發歌詞，皆名綺語。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，若依跳舞而寫歌詞，稱為綺語。或依作樂而寫歌詞，或俱依跳舞作樂而寫歌詞，或不依跳舞作樂但卻寫出不能引發義利的歌詞，都稱為綺語。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、依外道書論</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科依外道書論，依外道書論所發綺語說明。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="59p4843"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若佛法外能引無義所有書論，以愛樂心受持讚美，以大音聲而為諷頌，廣為他人開示分別，皆名綺語。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若佛法以外，世間不能引發利益安樂的書本言論，以歡喜好樂的心情來受持讚美，以大音聲而為背誦朗讀，又到處為他人開示分別，都稱為綺語。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯三、依鬥訟諍競等</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科依鬥訟諍競等，依鬥訟諍競等所發綺語說明。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若依鬥訟諍競發言，或樂處眾宣說王論、臣論、賊論，廣說乃至國土等論，皆名綺語。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若依止世間上種種的鬥爭、訴訟的事情，打官司，爭吵、競賽而發表言論，或在大眾中，宣說王道之論、為臣之論、盜賊之論，廣說乃至哪些國土殊勝、哪些國土下劣等論，與善法、修行及解脫沒有關係的事，都稱為綺語。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯四、依說妄語等</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科依說妄語等，依說妄語等所發綺語說明。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若說妄語、或離間語、或麤惡語，下至不思不擇發無義言，皆名綺語。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若說妄語、或離間語、或麤惡語，乃至沒有經過思考、決擇就發出令人沒有利益安樂的話，都稱為綺語。綺語的範圍很廣，包括前面的妄語，離間語，麤惡語，都可以算在綺語裏面，稱為相應綺語。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、約七事辨</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科約七事辨，約七種事情而發綺語。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="32868:48135"></a>又依七事而發綺語。謂鬥訟諍競語、諸婆羅門惡呪術語、苦所逼語、戲笑遊樂之語、處眾雜語、顛狂語、邪命語，如是一切名綺語罪。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又依止七種事情而發出綺語：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、鬥訟諍競語：由鬥爭、訴訟、爭論、競賽而發出綺語；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、諸婆羅門惡呪術語：外道婆羅門有很多惡咒術語；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、苦所逼語：苦所逼迫時生起瞋心，不思不擇發出沒有意義的語言；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、戲笑遊樂之語：喜歡開玩笑，或到處去遊玩快樂說的戲樂之語；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、處眾雜語：大家在一起散心雜話，沒有討論佛法修行的事，說一些世間五欲的事，名處眾雜語；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　六、顛狂語：精神顛倒、狂亂而亂說話；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　七、邪命語：為追求維持生命資具的來源，說諂媚不實的語言，使令對方能供養。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以上這一切都稱為綺語罪。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》邪命語者：謂為非法希求所有衣服、飲食、臥具、病緣醫藥諸資生具，方便現相而有所說故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為了非法希求得到衣服、飲食、臥具、病緣醫藥諸資生具，方便現出各種相貌，而有所說，稱為邪命語。</span></span></span></div>
