<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑八、貪欲業道攝2　寅一、辨起欲8　卯一、於供侍</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第八科貪欲業道攝，說明貪欲業道所攝方便，分二科；第一科辨起欲，詳細說明內心生起的八種貪欲，分八科；第一科於供侍，在供養給侍家主時心裏生起貪欲。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="59p4844"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，若於家主起如是欲：云何我當同於家主，領諸僕使，隨欲所作。是名貪欲。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，在供給服侍家主時，看到主人的威德勢力、自在方便，呼風喚雨，生起這種欲望：怎麼樣自己可以同主人一樣，領導僕使，想作什麼都可以隨意差遣他人，當心裏這樣想時就是貪欲。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、於攝受等</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科於攝受等，於攝受等生起貪欲。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又起是欲：即彼家主所有父母、妻子、奴婢及諸作使，廣說乃至七攝受事、十資身事，謂飲食等，皆當屬我。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又生起這樣的欲望：希望主人所擁有的尊貴的父母，賢慧的妻子，奴婢及諸僕使，種種替他做事的人，廣說乃至七攝受事，前面說父母事、妻子事、奴婢僕使事、朋友官僚兄弟眷屬事、田宅邸肆事、福業事及方便作業事、庫藏事等七攝受事，及十資身事，包括：食、飲、乘、衣、莊嚴具、歌笑舞樂、香鬘塗末、什物之具、照明、男女受行，凡是家主所擁有的財富，包括父母、妻子、兄弟、姐妹、奴婢、朋友、牛、羊及金銀財寶、房地產等有情或無情的資產，都希望屬於自己的。這是第二種貪欲業道。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯三、於稱頌</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科於稱頌，於稱頌生起貪欲。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又起是欲：云何令他知我少欲、知足、遠離、勇猛精進，安住正念、寂定、聰慧，諸漏永盡，施戒多聞。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　前面二科是約居士，第三科是約出家人。又生起這樣的欲望：如何令他人稱讚我是少欲、知足的人，已遠離色、聲、香、味、觸欲證得禪定，修行非常勇猛精進，隨時有力而且持續不斷安住正念、與法相應，內心非常的寂靜、安定，好像平靜無波的水、身善、口善、意善具聰慧者相，煩惱已經永遠斷除，常作布施的功德、持戒精嚴、學問又很充足，如果內心動了這樣的念頭，稱為貪欲。這是貪欲業道，此時已經與惡法相應了。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯四、於供養</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科於供養，於供養生起貪欲。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又起是欲：云何令他供養於我。謂諸國王乃至商主，若苾芻、苾芻尼、鄔波索迦、鄔波斯迦等，皆當恭敬、尊重、承事、供養於我。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這修行人的貪欲很大，又生起這種貪欲：如何使令他人來供養我？尤其是國王乃至大財主如果來供養，就不用那麼辛苦化緣；比丘、比丘尼、優婆塞、優婆夷等，都應該恭敬尊重、對我奉承，為我辦事，供養於我，生起這種心，稱為貪欲業道。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯五、於資緣</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科於資緣，於資生具的各種緣生起貪欲。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又起是欲：云何令我當得利養、衣服、飲食、諸坐臥具、病緣醫藥及資生具。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又生起這種欲望：怎樣使我得到名利、供養、衣服、飲食、坐具、臥具及各式各樣的資生具。這樣想的時候就是貪欲業道，要警惕！</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="59p4845"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯六、於妙欲</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科於妙欲，於妙欲生起貪欲。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又起是欲：云何令我當生天上，天妙五欲以為遊戲。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又生起這種欲望：如何使令我生到天上，在天上享受微妙的五欲，與天女遊戲歡樂，這也是一種貪欲。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯七、於勝生</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第七科於勝生，於勝生生起貪欲。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又起是欲：云何令我當生魯達羅世界、毗瑟笯世界，人中希有眾同分中，乃至令我當生他化自在眾同分中。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又生起這種欲望：如何令我生到魯達羅世界：這是外道的大自在世界，不是佛教的大自在天，佛教的大自在天在色界頂天。魯達羅，是暴惡的意思。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《瑜伽論記》說這是在欲界第六天他化自在天之下的天，或生毗瑟笯世界：就是毗丑天，四天王天裏面其中一天，屬於欲界天，或生在人中特別大富大貴，乃至令我生在他化自在天的眾同分中，他人變化的，我可以受用，這件事多麼快樂。這種後有愛，也是貪欲業道。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯八、於資產</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第八科於資產，於資產生起貪欲。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又起是欲：云何令我乃至當得父母、妻子、奴婢、作使、朋友、宰官、親戚、兄弟、同梵行等所有資產。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又生起這種欲望：如何使我得到父母、妻子、奴婢、作使、朋友、宰官、親戚、兄弟、同梵行等所擁有的資產。心想貪求他人的財產，也是貪欲業道。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、結所攝</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科結所攝，結說名貪欲業道所攝。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是一切，皆名貪欲業道所攝。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如上面所說的八種起心動念，都稱為貪欲業道所攝。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑九、瞋恚業道2　寅一、辨所思2　卯一、約九惱害事辨2　辰一、舉於己身2　巳一、報彼欲</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第九科瞋恚業道，說明瞋恚業道所攝方便，分二科；第一科辨所思，說明內心的思惟，分二科；第一科約九惱害事辨，約九種惱害對象分辨，又分二科；第一科舉於己身，舉出於自己生瞋，又分二科；第一科報彼欲，想要報復對方的欲望。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="59p4846"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若作是思：彼於我所有無義欲，故我於彼當作無義。是名瞋恚。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果心裏這麼想：他想對我做不利於我的事，所以我應該對他以牙還牙，也要做不利於他的事，名為瞋恚。世間人都能以德報怨，何況佛法？不應該有這種想法。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、報彼作</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科報彼作，報復對方所作的思惟。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又作是思：彼於我所已作、正作、當作無義，我亦於彼當作無義。亦名瞋恚。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又這樣想：對方已經做過對我不利的事、或者現在正在做，或者將來還會再做，我也要做傷害他的事情，這是依自己而生瞋恚，也稱為瞋恚業道。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、例於所愛有情事</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例於所愛有情事，推例於所愛有情事生瞋，道理也一樣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是廣說九惱害事，當知亦爾。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　乃至九惱害事，於九種對象也這樣想的話，都稱為瞋恚業道。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》如是廣說九惱害事者：前說瞋恚，唯依己身。又復緣彼所愛有情、非所愛有情、過去怨親、未來怨親、現在怨親而起瞋恚，如是一切，皆名有情瞋。彼所依事，名九惱事，如前已說當知。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/55.htm#48165:43290">陵本五十五卷八頁4420</a>）</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　前面說的瞋恚，只是依止己身；第二是自己所愛的有情；第三不是自己所愛有情。加上過去的怨家，過去所愛的有情；未來會成為仇人的怨家或者未來會成為所愛的有情；及現在的怨親而生起瞋恚，這樣加來就有九種。這是一切瞋恚，都名有情瞋。依止這九種有情，生起瞋恚的心情，稱為九惱害事。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在〈決擇‧五識身相應地意地〉卷55，1817頁中說瞋事有十種，包括這裏所說的己身、所愛有情、非所愛有情、過去怨親、未來怨親，現在怨親、不可意境、嫉妒、宿習、他見等都會生起瞋恚。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、約損害他心辨3　辰一、令我自在</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科約損害他心辨，約損害他人的心情來說，分三科；第一科令我自在，損人利己的思惟。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又作是思：云何令我於能損害怨家惡友而得自在，縛害驅擯，或行鞭撻，或散財產，或奪妻妾、朋友、眷屬及家宅等。此惱害心亦名瞋恚。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又這樣想：怎樣令我於能損害自己的怨家、惡友，能夠自在的繫縛他、迫害他、驅逐他、擯除他、鞭打他、使他財產破散，或將他的妻妾、朋友、眷屬及家宅奪取過來，這種惱害心也稱為瞋恚。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、令遭他損</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科令遭他損，使令遭他人損惱的思惟。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又起是思：云何令彼能損於我怨家惡友，於他處所遭如上說諸苦惱事。此損害心亦名瞋恚。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又這樣想：如何令能損於我的怨家惡友，希望他在他人那裏遭到上面所說的被縛害驅擯，或行鞭撻，或散財產，或奪妻妾、朋友、眷屬及家宅等苦惱事，這種損害心也稱為瞋恚。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》於他處所者：他有情處，名他處所。簡非由自，故作是說。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其他有情的地方，稱為他處所。簡別不是由自己來迫害他，希望他受到他人的迫害，所以這樣說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="59p4847"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰三、令自然損</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科令自然損，希望對方自然受損害的思惟。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又作是思：願彼自然發起如是如是身語意行，由此喪失資財、朋友、眷屬、名稱、安樂、壽命及諸善法，身壞當墮諸惡趣中。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又這樣想：如果對方沒有被我害，也沒被他人害，希望他自己自然發起不恰當的身語意三業，而喪失資財、朋友、眷屬、名稱、安樂、壽命，喪失各式各樣的善法，而且死了以後墮到惡道。總之就是希望對方不好，這也是瞋恚業道。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、結所攝</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科結所攝，結說瞋恚所攝。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是一切惱害之心，皆名瞋恚根本業道。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這一切惱怒對方，想要傷害對方的心情，都是瞋恚根本業道所攝。心裏生起這樣的念頭，就是瞋恚業道。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑十、邪見業道2　寅一、明所攝2　卯一、舉無施</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十科邪見業道，說明邪見業道所攝方便，分二科；第一科明所攝，說明邪見所攝，又分二科；第一科舉無施，舉出撥無布施等邪見。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，若作是思：決定無施。是名邪見。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，如果這樣想：決定沒有布施的善因能得善果這件事，這樣想稱為邪見。印度很多外道有這種邪見。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、例一切</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例一切，例餘一切邪見。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">廣說乃至謗因、謗用、謗果，壞真實事，如是一切皆名邪見根本業道。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　廣說乃至謗因：撥無布施、無愛養、也無祠祀；謗用：撥無妙行，也無惡行；謗果：撥無妙行惡行諸業的等流果及異熟果；壞真實事：撥無父、無母、無化生有情，也無世間真阿羅漢諸漏永盡等錯誤的思想，這一切都稱為邪見根本業道。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、問答辨2　卯一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科問答辨，以問答的方式來說明邪見，又分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：一切倒見皆名邪見，何故世尊於業道中，但說如是誹謗之見名為邪見？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：一切顛倒錯誤的思想都可以稱為邪見，為什麼佛在業道當中，只說這類毀謗之見稱為邪見？&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、答2　辰一、明業道2　巳一、由最勝3　午一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科明業道，說明邪見業道，又分二科；第一科由最勝，因為這種邪見是最厲害的，又分三科；第一科標，標出毀謗之見是最嚴重的惡業。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="59p4848"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：由此邪見，諸邪見中最為殊勝。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：因為這種邪見，在所有的邪見當中是最糟糕的一種，破壞力最強。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">何以故？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　怎麼說？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午三、釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科釋，解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由此邪見為依止故，有一沙門、若婆羅門斷諸善根。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於以這種邪見為依止，這位出家人或有學問的婆羅門，因此除斷善根，這一生不會再做善事。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又因為這些錯誤的想法，既不布施，也不持戒，更不修行，盡做些惡事，因此毀謗的邪見是所有邪見中最具殺傷力的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、由隨順惡</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科由隨順惡，因為毀謗的邪見最隨順惡業。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又此邪見最順惡業。懷邪見者，於諸惡法隨意所行，是故此見偏說在彼惡業道中。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又這種邪見最能隨順生起惡業。懷有這種邪見的人，撥無因果、作用、實事等在種種的惡法當中肆無忌憚，隨意而行，所以說毀謗邪見，特別說屬於惡業道中最糟糕的邪見。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、簡自相</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科簡自相，簡別其他的顛倒見不能說不是邪見，但毀謗的邪見最嚴重。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">當知餘見非不邪見自相相應。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　應當知道其他的顛倒見不能說不是邪見，但毀謗沒有因果、沒有業的流轉作用、壞真實事，毀謗沒有真實的阿羅漢，沒有世間真實的聖德、聖道，這是最厲害的邪見，最隨順惡業的，能使令有情斷善根。邪見有很多種，佛陀特別強調這種毀謗的邪見，在十惡業道中屬於毀謗的倒見，是舉出最嚴重的邪見來說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">瑜伽師地論科句披尋記卷第五十九</span></strong></span></span><br />
&nbsp;</p>
